“No, Little Hime just secretly glanced at me earlier. That means I win!” Lili immediately shot back, refusing to concede.

“A sneak peek doesn’t count as looking, so I still win!” Zerene finished triumphantly, her face breaking into a comically smug grin.

Seeing that smug expression dripping with mockery, Lili nearly flared up again.

“Alright, that’s enough. Both of you say less.” Yae-hime quickly stepped in to extinguish the sparks once more.

“Little Hime, did you gain anything else in Jade City?” Realizing that continuing the quarrel would be too childish, Lili simply changed the subject.

As one side lowered its banner, the other side also called off the drums of war. Tonight’s battle ended without either a victor or a loser.

“I did,” Yae-hime said, straightening her posture as she recounted everything she had seen and heard in Jade City.

“It’s more or less the same as the intelligence I received.” After listening, Lili nodded thoughtfully.

“Will those clerics have a fatal impact on our actions?” Yae-hime asked with some concern.

“Fatal? Not quite.” Lili bit her lip lightly. “But it will make things much more troublesome. In the end, though, the outcome will still be decided by Alicia and Richard.”

“What if their battle ends in a stalemate?” Yae-hime asked.

“…” Lili fell silent. It wasn’t as if she had never considered that possibility. If such a situation truly occurred, then the ones who would determine victory or defeat might instead become the others.

After pondering for a moment, Lili finally spoke. “Even if the probability is low, we still have to guard against it.” Then she turned her gaze toward Zerene. “Richard has outside help. So do we.”

Following her line of sight, Yae-hime looked over, only to see Zerene wearing a completely confused expression. It seemed she had not understood a single word of their conversation.

+++

# **770 – Oh my, there’s a big bug here~**

“Isn’t this a bit inappropriate?” Yae-hime said.

“There’s nothing inappropriate about it. As the saying goes, waste… no, that’s not right, it’s making full use of everything!” Lili reached out and patted Zerene on the shoulder. “Mm-hmm, so what do you think of Little Hime?”

Zerene had still looked confused just moments ago, but the instant she heard that question, her eyes sparkled brightly and she answered with cheerful delight. “I like her! I love staying by Little Hime’s side the most. She smells nice and it feels really comfortable!”

“Mm, you really get it!” Lili nodded vigorously. She then continued, “Right now, Little Hime has run into a huge problem and needs your help. So, will you help or not?”

“I’ll help!” Zerene answered instantly.

“Settled.” Lili turned her head toward Yae-hime.

The latter’s lips twitched slightly. What kind of ‘settled’ was that supposed to be!? “Zerene, you agreed without even asking what the matter was. Isn’t that a little reckless?” she said.

Zerene shook her head. “Little Hime’s problem is my problem. No matter what it is, I’ll help!”

“This matter is very dangerous,” Yae-hime said gently.

“I’m not afraid.” Zerene moved closer and grabbed Yae-hime’s hand. “As long as I’m with Little Hime, I’m not afraid of anything!” Even though she had lost her memories, her instincts told her that what she had just grasped was not merely a beautiful arm. ‘This is the future!’

“…” On the other side, Lili clenched her pink fists tightly, her large eyes seeming as though flames might burst from them. ‘She’s actually taking advantage of the moment to cop a feel of Little Hime! I should smack her!’

Though that was what she thought, she did not make a move. After all, the other party had already climbed aboard their pirate ship in a muddled haze. If they didn’t offer at least a little benefit, it would feel rather unreasonable.

“Alright then, let’s work hard together.” Yae-hime patted Zerene’s hand, a faint smile appearing on her face. At this point, they had no way back. The only path left was success. With Zerene joining them, their chances of victory would certainly increase.

“Mm! I will do my best!” Zerene nodded, a bright smile blooming across her face.

Seeing this, Lili could not help but feel somewhat worried. ‘Having such a powerful helper is undoubtedly a good thing. Our chances of success have also increased. However, if Little Hime helps her restore her strength, there’s no guarantee that unexpected complications won’t arise. For instance… her memories returning. If she regains her old memories, whether she’ll still treat Little Hime the way she does now is completely uncertain…’

There was a very real chance she would explode in fury. After all, she was the incarnation of some great power. Just thinking about it gave Lili a headache. In her view, restoring Zerene’s strength was hardly a clever move.

But with the situation having developed this far, whether the move was good or bad no longer mattered. As long as it worked, that was enough. That was also the main reason why she had suddenly thought of tying Zerene onto their war chariot.

‘We can’t afford to lose!’ Clenching her fists, Lili thought to herself.

“So then, Little Hime should sleep with me tonight~ Of course, just the two of us!” Zerene said with a smile.

The moment she heard this, Lili snapped back to her senses. “No way! Little Hime is sleeping with me tonight!”

“Hmph, no way! Little Hime is mine tonight!” Zerene stuck out her little pink tongue at her, full of provocation.

Without another word, Lili pounced forward, and the two little troublemakers tumbled together once more in a tangled scuffle. However, this time they were quickly pulled apart by Yae-hime.

“What are you two even fighting over? Isn’t this bed big enough?” she said irritably.

The two little ones exchanged glances and both nodded helplessly. Since neither of them could win, they might as well compromise. In any case, it wasn’t the first time the three of them had slept together.

As the saying went, once there was a first time, there would inevitably be a second. Once certain things began to be compromised, they would keep being compromised again and again.

Lili could not help letting out a soft sigh in her heart. She felt that she still lacked resolve.

“It’s getting late. Let’s rest,” Zerene said. Her body was still recovering, and her energy was clearly insufficient. Once drowsiness set in, it was almost impossible to resist.

“Lili, what do you think?” Yae-hime asked.

“Let’s rest first. Whatever it is, we can talk about it tomorrow morning,” Lili said after glancing at the drowsy Zerene.

“Mm, then let’s rest.” Yae-hime nodded.

By this time, Zerene had already lain down, her eyelids locked in a fierce battle against sleep. Even so, her hand still clung tightly to Yae-hime’s, refusing to let go.

“Just like a child,” Yae-hime said with a wry smile as she lay down as well.

Lili followed closely behind. The three of them lay extremely close together, almost pressed against one another.

“Good night…” Zerene murmured as she suddenly scooted closer, sticking herself to Yae-hime’s side. Just before her eyelids finally shut, she softly spoke those words.

Seeing the other side launch her offensive, Lili refused to fall behind. She swiftly pressed herself against Yae-hime’s body and then closed her eyes as well.

“…” Lying flat between them, Yae-hime found herself utterly speechless. At that moment she felt like a sea turtle being simultaneously clung to by two octopuses, completely immobilized and unable to move even an inch.

‘Fortunately, I can still log out. Otherwise, if I slept like this all night, my back and waist would definitely ache tomorrow.’

She gave a faint, helpless smile before suddenly recalling the matter of the Apostles. Since Lili had not mentioned anything about them, it likely meant they had not come attacking.

---

The night grew deep and silent.

Inside the room, only two steady breathing rhythms could be heard. Yae-hime, having finished her “night watch,” had already logged out.

Suddenly, Zerene opened her eyes. However, she saw nothing at all. A mysterious force had bound her consciousness in place.

“Zzz… Zzz…” Moments later, Zerene closed her eyes again, releasing calm and steady breaths as she drifted back into sleep.

Back in reality. Within the City of Chaos.

Yae-hime stepped out of her room and entered the main hall. Even from a distance, she could smell the aroma of food drifting from the dining hall.

“These little troublemakers… why are they eating all day long?”

Despite looking so adorable, every one of them behaved like starving ghosts, never seeming to have their fill.

“My wallet is going to be eaten empty by them sooner or later,” Yae-hime said with a bitter smile. After all, including the original body, there were still thirteen Veras that had yet to be captured. That meant thirteen more stomachs to feed!

“Wallet crisis.” At that moment, she even felt as though her own stomach was twitching. ‘Looks like I’ll have to harvest a few more _leeks_ soon.’

When she walked into the dining hall, she indeed found six little ones devouring their food with wild enthusiasm.

“Master!” Little Blue, with her sharp senses, immediately noticed someone entering the dining hall. She lifted her head and saw that it was her master.

The other five little ones heard her voice and instantly stopped eating. They straightened their backs and quickly put on refined, well-behaved expressions.

“If you don’t fix those ugly table manners, believe me, I’ll lock you up and starve you for a few days,” Yae-hime said with a smile that did not quite reach her eyes.

The moment those words fell, the temperature in the living room seemed to drop noticeably. All six little ones felt a chill run down their spines. A few days without food… how unbearable would that be? No way. Absolutely not!

With perfect synchronization, they shook their heads while wailing pitifully.

“Wuuu… Master, we won’t dare do it again!”

“There must not be a next time,” Yae-hime said sternly. As the head of the household, she had the responsibility to properly teach and discipline her family.

“Yes!” the six little ones answered quickly.

“You can keep eating. Come gather in the living room afterward.” Yae-hime nodded in satisfaction.

Ten minutes later. All seven of them had gathered in the living room.

“Has anything unusual happened on Aqua Blue Star?” Yae-hime asked first.

“No,” Little Blue replied. After a moment, she added that things were more or less the same as usual.

“And Roc City?” Yae-hime continued.

“N-no… wait! Master, I saw a really big bug earlier!” As if suddenly remembering something, Little Blue exclaimed excitedly.

+++

# **771 – Squash the Bug, Little Hime!**

“A big bug?” Yae-hime tilted her head slightly and asked in confusion.

“Yes, yes! Really big!” Little Blue spread her arms wide, gesturing enthusiastically. The more she gestured, however, the harder it became for Yae-hime to understand what she meant. After all, when a creature measured fifty or sixty centimeters long, whether it could still be called a “bug” was already questionable.

‘Could it be one of those giant insects?’

“Did you see it inside City of Chaos, or outside?” Yae-hime hurriedly asked.

“Outside!” Little Blue replied.

“Through the city cameras?” Yae-hime asked.

“Yep.”

“Do you have a photo?”

“I do.”

“Then hurry up and show it!” Yae-hime felt a strong urge to knock her on the head.

Seeing that her master seemed a little impatient, Little Blue quickly opened a floating panel and displayed the photo. The moment Yae-hime looked at it, her eyes widened. There really was a huge bug in the picture.

To be precise, it was a mantis nearly fifty to sixty centimeters long, its entire body a vivid green. Clamped in its jaws was an adult black cat! The photo itself was not very high in resolution, but the surrounding environment could still be made out.

The giant mantis stood in what appeared to be a somewhat filthy alley. Scattered on the ground were bits of leftover food, likely discarded kitchen scraps from a cafeteria or restaurant behind the building. Under the dim orange streetlight, the mantis’ scythe-like forelegs glinted with a chilling metallic sheen.

“This bug is abnormally large,” Yae-hime said. A hint of concern crept into her voice.

Aqua Blue Star had awakened ahead of time, and the consequences of that early awakening were already beginning to reveal themselves. First came strange anomalies appearing across the world, followed by the awakening of ancient creatures.

“And now even giant bugs are starting to show up…” In her previous life, Yae-hime had seen news reports about giant insects attacking humans. Back then, she had assumed those creatures had come from the Saint Demon World. She never expected them to be native species!

“Master, do you think a bug this big would taste delicious if it were roasted?” At that moment, Little Blue asked while drooling. Hearing this, Yae-hime and the Vera clones blinked, wondering if they had misheard.

“I really want to try it!” Little Blue added eagerly.

“….” Silence immediately filled the room.

“Huh? Why are you all looking at me with such weird expressions?” Little Blue tilted her head, completely puzzled.

“You actually want to eat a bug like that?” Yae-hime’s eyelid twitched.

In this world, quite a few insects were edible and even highly nutritious. However, even if insects were tasty and packed with nutrients, the majority of people still preferred not to eat them. Not to mention a monstrous bug like this. Just looking at it was enough to ruin anyone’s appetite.

“Little Blue, that’s so scary…” Vera 18 whispered.

“Mm-mm!” The other clones nodded in agreement.

“That’s so mean! What’s wrong with eating bugs!?” Little Blue protested when she saw their increasingly strange looks.

“There’s nothing wrong with eating bugs,” Yae-hime said. “The problem is that you want to eat a monster like this.”

She enlarged the image so everyone could clearly see the details of the giant mantis.

“There are so many little black spots on its body… that’s disgusting!”

“And that green liquid dripping from its mouth is gross!”

“It’s probably highly poisonous… ugh, it might even be crawling with parasites!”

“A carnivorous insect… that’s just revolting!”

The Vera clones began talking all at once as they stared at the zoomed-in image.

“You’re making it sound so disgusting… fine, I won’t eat it anymore!” Little Blue said miserably, on the verge of tears.

“Alright, that’s enough,” Yae-hime said, raising a hand to signal them to stop. The room quickly fell silent. Seeing this, Yae-hime nodded in satisfaction before continuing, “Little Blue, this photo was captured from surveillance footage, right?”

“Yeah. Right after this was recorded, the camera stopped working,” Little Blue said with a nod. “The location is nearby.”

“With Roc City so heavily urbanized, there clearly isn’t a suitable environment for such a giant insect to survive. It’s very likely an invasive species.” Vera 1 said.

“I think so too,” Yae-hime nodded. She remembered that the earliest reports of giant insects attacking humans had come from a small island nation in South Asia. That insect might very well have invaded from overseas.

“Little Blue, send me over there. I need to check the situation.” Yae-hime said. When it came to unknown dangers like this, it was always best to eliminate them as quickly as possible.

A faint chill of killing intent arose in her heart toward the giant mantis that had suddenly intruded into her sphere of life. For now, it was attacking small animals, but who knew when it might begin attacking humans.

“Okay!” Little Blue’s eyes widened as a blue glow flickered across her entire body.

The next moment, Yae-hime was teleported away. At the same time, inside a narrow alley that carried a faint stench of decay, a flash of white light suddenly appeared, revealing a graceful figure.

“There’s still a subtle trace of its presence in the air. It seems it hasn’t been gone long.” Yae-hime closed her eyes and concentrated, carefully distinguishing the various scents lingering in the air.

After reaching Level 40, her body’s latent potential had developed even further, and her sensory perception had improved significantly compared to before.

“I should be able to track it from here,” she murmured softly as she opened her eyes. Her gaze then shifted toward the ground not far away. There were traces of blood, scraps of flesh, and patches of black fur scattered there.

“So it ate right here. Quite bold.” It was obvious that the giant mantis had enjoyed a full meal here before leaving. “How foolish. If you had left immediately, it would have been much harder for me to find you.”

The moment she finished speaking, Yae-hime lightly tapped the ground with her toes and shot upward between two buildings. In less than three seconds, she appeared on the rooftop of a nearby building.

“Strange… that unusual presence still hasn’t dissipated.” Yae-hime scanned her surroundings and spoke with a hint of confusion.

**Swish!**

At that very moment, a dark shadow dropped from above. A cold gleam flashed as it shot downward like an arrow! Yae-hime remained standing exactly where she was, as though completely unaware that something was plummeting toward her at high speed.

In 0.5 seconds, the shadow closed in to an extremely short distance. 0.8 seconds later, the shadow was about to make contact with Yae-hime, but… at the exact instant before it could touch her, a half-transparent tentacle lashed out with lightning speed. It struck the shadow violently and sent it flying.

With a loud bang, the dark figure slammed hard into a wall, the impact cracking the tiles embedded in its surface.

“You actually stayed here wandering around. Your courage is quite impressive.” Yae-hime turned to look over, a mocking smile curling at the corner of her lips. Over there, the shadow slowly slid down the wall. It was the giant mantis. Apparently, after devouring the black cat, it had continued roaming around this area instead of leaving.

“I thought insects had sharp instincts, that they knew how to seek fortune and avoid danger.” Yae-hime walked toward it step by step. “But you don’t seem to be very intelligent.”

“…Ksssh… ksssh…” The giant mantis struggled to stand up, its body trembling as it stared at Yae-hime, strange sounds coming from its mouth.

“Heh, you still want to resist? Good. Go ahead and try.” As soon as she finished speaking, the aura radiating from Yae-hime surged forward like a violent storm, wrapping tightly around the mantis.

A human-like expression of terror instantly appeared on its face. Immediately afterward, it began struggling wildly. However, how could a mere insect break free from Yae-hime’s aura restraints?

One minute later, the giant mantis finally gave up struggling. Just as Yae-hime thought she was about to claim her prize, the creature’s head suddenly began to swell. Then, like a watermelon dropped from a great height, it exploded completely.

+++

# **772 – The Insectman Attacks, A Terrifying Opening Move!!**

At the same time. Several kilometers away, the sudden fluttering of thin wings echoed from the rooftop of a building. Immediately afterward, a dark shadow shot upward into the night sky.

Under the pale moonlight, the figure revealed itself as a strange creature, half human and half insect.

“Kssshkssh-kssh!” A peculiar sound escaped from its mouth, carrying a faint trace of anger. Its wings beat violently as the mantis-like humanoid, armed with a pair of enormous sickle-shaped blades, surged through the air and sped off toward a distant location.

On the other side, the instant the giant mantis’ head exploded, Yae-hime swiftly retreated several meters, then raised a layer of aura to shield herself from the fragments that shot outward.

**Squirt! Squirt! Squirt!**

The green liquid that burst from the mantis’ head splattered onto the ground, and the moment it touched the surface, it began corroding the concrete floor. Wisps of white smoke curled upward as the chemical reaction rapidly ate into the pavement.

“This bug is way too extreme. I was planning to capture it and take it back for research.” With a casual flick of her slender hand, Yae-hime swept away the nauseating stench lingering in the air using a wave of aura.

Her gaze then shifted back to the giant mantis. At that moment, its body was visibly dissolving, melting away at a speed the naked eye could easily perceive.

“It didn’t even leave me a corpse…” Yae-hime muttered with obvious frustration. She had originally intended to use the mantis’ remains for medical research. After all, mutated creatures like this often contained unknown biological elements that could yield unexpected discoveries.

Unfortunately, the creature had chosen to destroy itself rather than give her the opportunity to study it.

“Come to think of it… a giant insect like that probably isn’t the only one around.” Looking at the puddle of green and white slime spreading across the ground, she spoke uncertainly.

Just before the creature killed itself, she had faintly sensed a peculiar mental fluctuation spreading outward at incredible speed.

“Maybe… that was just my imagination.” Retracting her gaze, Yae-hime took out her phone and opened a special application developed by Little Blue.

“Master, did you finish it?” The moment the interface appeared, a tiny face popped up on the screen.

“It went south,” Yae-hime replied.

“What, what!? The omnipotent and magnificent Master personally took action, yet you still couldn’t catch that bug… I-Is it some kind of divine insect!?” Little Blue shouted in exaggerated shock, clearly putting on a performance.

“Your acting gets a score of 0.1.” Yae-hime shot back irritably.

“Hehe, I’m still working hard to improve! But never mind that. Master, you really miscalculated?”

“Miscalculated… well, technically speaking, I suppose it counts as a miscalculation.” Yae-hime briefly explained what had happened. Then she tilted the phone slightly so Little Blue could see the puddle of slime on the ground.

“Ugh! That’s disgusting! I never want to eat bugs again!” High above on the City of Chaos, Little Blue retched violently.

The Vera clones nearby stared at her in confusion. ‘Did she eat too much or something?’

“Bleeegh! Bugs are so gross!” Little Blue bent over in midair, looking as if she were about to actually vomit.

“If you’re going to throw up, wait until I get back and then—” Before she could finish speaking, Yae-hime’s expression suddenly changed. Her body shot backward in a rapid retreat.

The next instant, a deep fissure split open exactly where she had been standing. The crack was perfectly smooth, as though it had been sliced open by something unimaginably sharp.

If that attack had struck her directly, Yae-hime would not have come away unscathed. At the very least, her clothes would have been ruined. She was currently wearing a simple white casual outfit. Its value was difficult to estimate.

After all, it had been specially custom-made for her by Nangong Lin, and only three sets existed in the entire world.

“Kssshkssh-kssh!”

Just as Yae-hime steadied herself, that strange sound echoed from somewhere not far away. Following the sound, she looked up and immediately spotted a dark figure hurtling toward her at incredible speed.

“Launching such a sharp attack from that distance just to ambush me… this thing’s got some skill.” Yae-hime slowly clenched her fist, her eyes fixed on the approaching shadow. It was a creature that looked half human and half mantis.

“An insectman!?” The moment she clearly saw its true form, a trace of surprise appeared on Yae-hime’s face. What surprised her even more happened next. The mantisman swooped down from the air and landed heavily on the ground, shattering the concrete beneath its feet.

Immediately afterward, a powerful aura erupted from within its body, surging outward like a raging typhoon sweeping across the area.

This was the aura of a Grandmaster. There was no time for further surprise. With a swift lift of her slender hand, Yae-hime conjured a shield of aura before her.

In the blink of an eye. The mantisman’s surging aura slammed forward with ferocious force and crashed heavily into the shield. The shockwave burst outward instantly, and the shield twisted violently under the impact.

Yet despite the severe distortion, the barrier held firm. Not a single crack appeared as it completely blocked the powerful aura attack. Yae-hime remained completely unharmed.

Seeing this, the mantisman immediately revealed a humanlike expression of shock. It had believed that single strike would be enough to destroy her. This human who had killed its kin was no ordinary opponent.

Unlike the earlier giant mantis, the mantisman clearly possessed a level of intelligence comparable to that of a human. Until it fully understood the enemy before it, it dared not act rashly. As one of the top predators in the insect world, the mantisman possessed extraordinary patience.

“Who are you? Why did you attack me?” Yae-hime dispelled the aura shield and looked toward the mantisman as she spoke.

The creature had patience, and so did she.

“Kssshkssh-kssh!” As if it had understood her words, the mantisman first glanced at the small patch of slime still lingering on the ground. Then it gestured with its scythe-like arms. An unmistakably humanlike fury appeared on its strange face.

“…” Yae-hime could neither understand its speech nor decipher its gestures. However, the creature’s anger was something she could clearly sense. ‘This insectman clearly has more research value than that giant mantis. I wonder if I can capture it and bring it back…’

If the mantisman had known what Yae-hime was thinking at that moment, it would probably have exploded with rage on the spot. The two stared at each other in silence. The scene grew so quiet that the faint whisper of the breeze could be heard.

Seconds ticked by. The predator remained still, while the prey also showed no intention of moving. After several minutes passed.

“Ksssh!” The predator, the mantisman, finally lost its patience. With a powerful stomp of its left foot, its muscular body shot toward Yae-hime like a cannonball.

Before it even arrived, its overwhelming aura surged forward first.

“An intermediate Grandmaster, huh? Not bad. Now I wonder just how much stronger your physical ability is compared to a human’s.” Yae-hime calmly assumed the opening stance of her self-created Taiji.

Unlike the traditional Taiji she had studied, her stance was simple. Her left foot stepped forward half a pace, her body sank slightly, and both hands rose to chest height, one forward and one behind. Then she slowly opened her palms.

It looked almost casual. Yet the moment Yae-hime took this stance, the mantisman’s heart tightened. Because it sharply sensed a terrifying pressure emanating from her. The instant it entered her attack range, it would be crushed beneath that overwhelming pressure.

‘I absolutely cannot get close. I have to defeat her from a distance!’ The mantisman immediately changed its combat approach, gathering its power into both scythe blades before slashing forward with brutal force.

In an instant, two enormous, visible blade arcs shot toward Yae-hime. The violent aftershock carved two deep gouges into the ground as it passed, sending shattered stones flying and dust billowing into the air.

Faced with such fierce and razor-sharp strikes, Yae-hime merely shifted her footing slightly while her left and right hands traced slow circles through the air. At that moment, the pressure the mantisman had sensed earlier became even more terrifying. It felt as though heaven and earth themselves were now under her control.

++++

# **Two as One Princesses - Chapter 180 - Spirits, Song and Dance, and Hunter Guild**

「Incidentally, have you not asked Miss Rulinia about my Job?」

Recalling something before I exited the door, I asked the princess this question, and, in response, she tilted her head before saying, 「I don’t necessarily require her every single observation, you know?」

That’s true; if she needed to report about every single person, it would be hard on both of them, so Rulinia probably only reports about unusual people like us.

Well, I don’t exactly know how they work together, so I shouldn’t think too deeply about it.

「Well then, I shall take my leave now.」

「Right. Thank you for coming over to chat today.」

Since we’ll likely have more opportunities to talk again, I ended our meeting there and left the princess’ room… to go to the rooftop, as usual.

I don’t know if they feel my presence from the roof or if they come here every day, but there were many spirits gathered. From young ones to large ones, spirits of various shapes and sizes practically sprang at me as soon as I appeared. Still, since we can’t touch each other, they just cheerfully went through me.

「For now, why don’t I sing something?」

『Right. After all, the spirits gather when they hear Ain singing.』

「Don’t they also dance together whenever Ciel starts dancing?」

『I’ll dance afterwards. The spirits want to meet Ain, after all.』

That may be true, but I think they like Ciel as well. Anyway, after checking that there isn’t anyone who can hear us nearby, I began to sing.

The first one was a calm song, an insert song of a movie, a carefree one that I was addicted to for a period of time. Even singing it again, it never stops being fun. Unlike before, there are a lot of people… beings? listening, which might be part of why I’m enjoying it.

The spirits flew around freely and disorderly, but I can tell that they’re listening to my song. Some of them drew near me and were listening with satisfied expressions. Looking like dogs or rabbits, they’re adorable, and I really wish I could touch them.

The intermediate and high spirits are watching from a short distance away. They’re probably letting the smaller ones go in front. Lisyl, in particular, who is usually near our side, is watching from afar with a gentle smile.

As the first song was over, Ciel didn’t really say anything, so I began thinking about what the second song should be. And then, an idea popped into my mind, so I decided to sing a very loud and rowdy song.

As I started singing, the spirits got up in surprise and glared at me for a bit. I might have gone a bit overboard with my prank, but after a while, they’ve begun enjoying the song, so it’s all good.

Being used to my singing, Ciel was laughing inside my head. In the past, I would sing songs randomly as I remembered them, and there were many times where the contrast between the songs’ energy was extreme, so this likely isn’t surprising to Ciel.

Since I switched to a more energetic song, the spirits took some distance and danced. I call it dance, but it’s mostly them flying around. The way they’re trying their best to express themselves in their own way is really adorable.

By the time I finished singing, they seemed to have either forgotten about my prank or didn’t care anymore, as they’re cheerfully playing around.

『It looks like they forgot about your prank.』

「As long as they’re having fun, I don’t really mind.」

『It wasn’t much of a prank for me, but I do want to experience being pranked by Ain. Don’t you want to try?』

「Umm, let’s consider that for another time. Our current priority is to play with the spirits, after all.」

『Fair point.』

「With that said, I’ll be switching now.」

While playing with spirits with my hand, I spoke to Ciel for a bit before switching. Immediately, the spirits stopped fawning to my hand and are assessing the situation. Playing with them is fine and all, but I want them to properly recognize Ciel as well. I haven’t had the opportunity to dance with Ciel as of late either, so I want Ciel to take the opportunity to dance as much as she wants.

「As expected, they move away.」

『I think they’re just surprised. They had the same reaction when I began singing earlier, you see.』

「I know, but it still feels lonely, you know?」

『Then shall we start dancing to make friends with the spirits? We are trying _that_ today, aren’t we?』

「Right, that’s right! No need to worry about me, so I want you to give it your all, Ain!」

While it was painfully obvious that I was changing the topic, Ciel is in high spirits now, so it’s good enough. Part of the reason we came here today is because of a certain thing we previously discussed and wanted to try. Though it’s not really something that would make us stronger, it actually might hold us back, to be honest, but that’s a minor issue.

『In that case, I’ll be doing it now.』

After giving Ciel a heads-up, 「A—h, a—h,」 I started vocalizing. For now, there are no issues. And so, I proceeded to use Ciel’s mouth to sing. Hearing my song, Ciel began dancing.

Some time before, when we were still imprisoned by Rispelgia, I was able to move Ciel’s arm while she was conscious. So we already knew this before, but doing something like this, where I sing with Ciel’s mouth while she maintains control of everything else and dances, is actually possible.

In theory, to be exact.

The reason why we don’t do it is because, first of all, there’s no merit in doing so. It’s partially because Ciel is the only one who can hear my song that we are able to obtain S-rank level strength while managing to keep it a secret.

Additionally, using the Song Princess’ powers while in this state is extremely difficult. If I try to use Song Princess in this state, its power will be exercised through Ciel’s body as a whole, which would then be obstructed by her Dance Princess powers. Perhaps it’s because the body is originally hers, but we’re practically in a state where only Dance Princess is operable and Song Princess is dormant.

And this is the biggest obstacle for us, but while I’m singing, breathing is under my control. It’s most noticeable when doing sports, but breathing is extremely important for moving your body. However, in this state, Ciel can’t breathe freely. Regardless of how impressive Ciel is, she can’t properly dance in this state, so we refrained from doing this.

But as Ciel progressively got used to my breathing—and perhaps because she’s gotten closer to divinity, so we no longer need to breathe as much as before—it has become achievable, which led to our unveiling here today. There’s nowhere else for us to show off, after all.

Another reason is that as our interactions with people have increased, the chances of Ciel using Dance Princess in public might increase as well. While Ciel doesn’t really care much about it, I’d feel bad making Ciel dance in silence. I personally want Ciel to always appear at her best.

For Ciel, it’s delightful to dance while hearing my singing voice in a different way than usual, so she proactively cooperated. In fact, you could say that she’s the more proactive one between us.

We’re aiming to reach a higher level of mastery, but that’s something to look forward to in the future.

The sound spirit is making sounds to the rhythm of my song, so I’m sure it’ll eventually be perfect.

For now, since this is a test run, I chose a song that’s on the calmer side; still, it genuinely feels strange to hear my voice while Ciel is dancing. It’s different from when Ciel and I spent the day together. It feels kind of close yet kind of far.

Ciel is having a harder time dancing than usual, but she continues dancing with great delight, and following her lead, the spirits dance as well. The spirits look more organized than earlier, which might be because they’re imitating Ciel’s movements.

As the song ended, Ciel was jumping in joy, cheering, 「That was fun! So fun!」 despite being out of breath. She normally wouldn’t run out of breath just from this, but it must have been considerably tough on her— honestly, it was also tough on my part; I really admire her energy. I feel like she might want to do it more, so I’ll stop her first. I do want to see Ciel dancing, and I do want to sing more, but it’s really difficult to sing in our current state.

Ciel being out of breath means that I’m also out of breath, and singing in this condition is extremely difficult.

『Shall we have a short break before continuing on?』

「It’s a shame, but it can’t be helped. This isn’t a situation to overexert ourselves over anyway.」

『I’m glad that you understand.』

After this, we played with the spirits while having our break before performing together once again.

---

「So there hasn’t been any message from the headquarters?」

「Y-yes, there hasn’t. And so, the guild master…」

「I don’t plan to meet them. There should be A-rank hunters other than me, and I don’t intend to stay working here for a very long time.」

With the academy being on holiday today, we went to the Hunter Guild for the first time in a while. Not as the E-rank Ailneige, but as the A-rank Ainsel, so you could say that it’s my first time coming here.

Since I had a mask on and wore my hood low, we were seen with suspicion the moment I entered the building. The hood and mask combo made us look so dubious that no one approached us, so we were able to easily reach the reception desk; since the receptionist was already on guard due to the hunters’ strange behavior, the receptionist didn’t raise a voice when I presented my A-rank Hunter Card. She was very surprised, though.

Nonetheless, since there’s really no hiding our shortness, I still expected some trouble. Maybe the hunters also behave when there are students present, so I suppose I can’t make a judgement yet. Though since the process went smoothly, I guess there’s no need to bother thinking about it.

The reason we came as Ainsel is to check if any information regarding the Artificial Divine Messenger had arrived. The result: there wasn’t. And since we’ve achieved our objective in coming here, I asked Ciel what to do next.

『What should we do?』

『Since we have the time, why not do some work as Ainsel? Since having Ain take on requests occasionally was part of the plan to begin with, right?』

『Understood. In that case, shall we look at the bulletin board, then?』

As I was about to leave the reception desk for the bulletin board, 「Oi, you,」 I heard a young yet proud voice. Though I said young, he’s about as young as Ciel. Not feeling the need to respond, I opted to ignore him. It might have been directed to us, but he didn’t enter my field of vision, and there are other people in my general direction.

While hoping that he would just give up, he unfortunately wasn’t pleased with my response and, 「Oi,」 began to reach for my shoulder. As I moved quickly to avoid it, his hand cut the empty air, causing him to slump slightly forward—or so I saw through detection.

『Is there something wrong?』

『A student was about to approach us, so I avoided him.』

『Really?』

『He didn’t enter my field of vision, you see. But it looks like quiet avoidance isn’t working well, so I might have to ask Ciel a favor.』

『Yes, yes! Feel free to leave anything to me!』

He started shaking violently when I avoided him, so he’s unlikely to let us go. It’s difficult to run away when already targeted, so there’s not much that can be done. After all, no matter what I do, the other party is probably fixated on my appearance.

「Oi! You think you’re too good for me!?」

「Are you speaking to me?」

「Y-yeah! That’s right, you masked b… person.」

As I responded to the person following us—Alcrei—his attitude suddenly changed for whatever reason; it’s clear that he’s shaken. I thought that he found us out, but I did change my voice, so he shouldn’t know that I’m Ailneige.

Hmm, he paused in the middle of saying what I assume to be _‘masked b̲a̲s̲t̲a̲r̲d̲,’_ so maybe the surprise was because he expected me to be male?

「You have an odd-looking attire, but you’re an academy student too, aren’t you? I’ll let you join my party.」

And while I don’t know what possessed him to say that, I tried my best to suppress my emotions as I responded, 「I refuse.」

+++

# **181: Alcrei, Song Princess, and the Church**

After curtly declining the party invitation, Alcrei did not get angry but instead had a blank expression.

That’s fine, since that means I won’t need Ciel’s help for this, but when I was about to leave, 「You, you think you can refuse my proposal!?」 a loud voice echoed out.

I see; he simply blanked out because he didn’t consider the possibility of being refused. Still, now this is getting annoying. For now, since this is genuinely my first time meeting him as Ainsel, I curtly asked, 「In the first place, who even are you?」

This might not necessarily be the correct choice, but even without the status of being Fiiyanamia’s daughter, an A-rank is still higher in status than an earl’s child who isn’t even a direct heir. Even at best, we’d only be equal.

For that reason, from an objective standpoint, my remark is not a problem, and it’s instead Alcrei who’s playing with fire. Still, it’s not like there is much I can do legally or using my influence; I can probably have the Hunter Guild file an official complaint to Alcrei’s family at best.

Since things like these are tied to the local customs, it’s hard to make proper judgments.

That aside, while I did change my voice to prevent being traced back to Ailneige, it’ll be troublesome if Alcrei starts following us in the future. After all, Ainsel will be appearing in the Hunter Guild regularly, and the chance of Alcrei being around is relatively high.

The only time we have to go to the Hunter Guild is during academy rest days, and the same goes for Alcrei. For that reason, we need to somehow settle this issue right now, cutting all loose ends in the future.

This is why even though I can run if I wanted to, I’m not running. We can do that anytime.

「I didn’t think there would be any student who doesn’t know, but I’ll allow your ignorance this time. I’m Alcrei Tweisel. You do know the Tweisel family, don’t you?」

「Earl Tweisel’s kin, is it…」

While acting as if I only learned it now, judging from his statement, I guess students from the first academy don’t become hunters? The first academy only accommodates nobles, and even those who aren’t next in line can still aspire to become knights or bureaucrats. I vaguely recall a certain prince attending the first academy while also being a hunter, but perhaps people like him are the minority.

Actually, does that mean that there’s a chance that I could bump into the said prince here in the Hunter Guild? I need to verify with the princess later.

「If you know, then that saves the explanation. Join my party.」

「I refuse.」

「Why!?」

「Because we simply have too large of a rank difference. If you are not at least B-rank, I cannot agree to it.」

「What are you even…」

Has his mind not processed it yet, or is he refusing to understand? I don’t know, but since Alcrei is needlessly repeating himself, I showed him my A-rank card while making sure to cover my name.

I’d hate it if he knew my name, and there is a chance that he’ll argue that it’s a fake, but since Alcrei should have a certain level of education as a noble, I hope that he knows that it’s risky to show off a fake card inside the Hunter Guild, enough that no one—there are exceptions, but no sane person at least—would take such a risk.

「As such, please do not speak to me in the future.」

「Wait, so I just need to be B-rank, right?」

「I’ll at least hear you out when that happens.」

「Once you join my party, I’ll have you take off that hood and mask.」

For some reason, he seems convinced that reaching B-rank would automatically mean that I’d join his party; he’s not listening at all. Still, reaching B-rank while being a student is impossible, and we should be out of this country once we’re done with schooling, so if this makes it so he doesn’t constantly involve himself with us, then that interpretation is good enough.

Nonetheless, he actually didn’t doubt the authenticity of my card. He’s at least sharp-witted, I suppose. Even if he had doubted it, inquiring with a receptionist would quickly reveal the truth, so it’s not—actually, that might end up spreading the word to the other hunters present, so I’m glad he’s quick on the uptake.

「If you don’t speak to me until reaching B-rank, I’ll consider it.」

「Don’t you turn back on those words, alright?」

「Alright. Now if you’d excuse me.」

We haven’t looked at the requests yet, but it’s not really necessary, so I quickly left the Hunter Guild.

Since we don’t have any other plans for the day, I headed somewhere unpopulated so I could speak with Ciel.

『Come to think of it, why did Alcrei behave obediently back then?』

『I want to know, too. I was so looking forward to Ain relying on me; that was disappointing.』

『Sorry to hear that. But still, why…』

Why did he relent that easily? I didn’t really think about it earlier since it was convenient for us, but thinking about it more, that was a bit too convenient.

Am I just being overly conscious because it’s different from the usual pattern? Alcrei isn’t thinking of some weird scheme, is he?

I assume that he changed his attitude after noticing that I’m a girl from my voice, but it’s not like he’s inexperienced with girls, is he? Alcrei is the son of a noble, so that shouldn’t be the case. But then maybe his attitude towards Belltina is because…

As I was in deep contemplation, Ciel muttered in a bewildered tone, 『Oh, Ain, you genuinely haven’t realized it yet?』

『Do you know why he acted that way, Ciel?』

『I can’t say for sure, but I can vaguely understand why.』

『Why is it?』

『Just for confirmation, my movements draw people’s attention, right?』

『I believe so. Even in my eyes, I find Ciel’s movements to be beautiful, after all.』

Regarding Ciel’s movements, there’s no arguing it at this point, and after some lessons, she’s no less elegant than royalty, so it obviously draws attention. Still, I’ve been charmed by Ciel’s movements long ago, so I don’t know how beautiful her movements look in the eyes of other people. After all, I find Ciel’s gestures to be the most beautiful out of all.

Well, I’m completely aware that I’m not being objective; dunno why I explicitly said, _‘Even in my eyes,’_ though.

『And that’s partly because I’m a Dance Princess, right?』

『That’s right. I can’t even mimic Ciel’s movements.』

『In that case, it wouldn’t be strange for Ain’s voice to draw people as well.』

Ciel’s words shook me. She’s right; if the Dance Princess’ influence―even if it’s only secondary―affects her normal movement, then it wouldn’t be strange if the Song Princess’ abilities can affect my normal voice, too. I have, in fact, changed my speaking voice to the point of being unrecognizable.

The reason it didn’t have the same level of potency as Ciel’s movements up until now could either be because my Job mastery is much lower than Ciel’s or because I didn’t have many opportunities to actively speak with a changed voice until now. And I think it’s the latter.

Could this also be why he quickly believed that I was A-rank?

『But I can’t actually tell the difference, you see?』

『Really? Since you mentioned it, I was actually convinced with that assessment.』

『After all, Ain’s voice has always been enchanting to me. That’s why I don’t really understand how people don’t fall for Ain’s voice just from hearing it. In that sense, Alcrei at least has a good sense of judgment!』

While I did have a similar thought, being praised like that feels really ticklish; I don’t know how to react―And because I’m currently in control, Ciel can probably see me voicelessly flapping my lips, making it feel even more embarrassing. 『Oh, I’ll say it again if you want to hear it, you know?』 Hearing Ciel say that, I’m now sure she saw right through me…

Since there’s nothing else I can do, I’ve decided to change the topic before she teases me even more. But before that, I told Ciel, 『I feel the same with your movements, you know?』

There are many things that can’t be relayed unless put into words. If this had a significant effect, it might turn the tables, but Ciel only responded, 『I’m happy, so happy!』 with pure joy, so I decided to change the topic as planned.

『By the way, I couldn’t get us a request, so what shall we do now?』

『That’s a bummer, isn’t it? After all, today’s plan was just to go along with Ain’s request work. At the earliest, I expected us to stay outside until evening. Ain, is there something else you want to do right now?』

『Let’s see…』

Hearing Ciel’s question, I mused for a moment. The truth is, there’s been a place I’m thinking we should visit, but I’ve been postponing it, or rather, I personally wanted to ignore it.

If my memory serves me right, there should be one in the capital, too, but I do have reasons for avoiding it outside of personal feelings.

『I believe it may be best to go to a temple at least once. I do have some things I want to ask the Creator God as well.』

『Come to think of it, we’ve never been to one. Though since Fii’s manor does serve the same function as a temple, that might not be completely right. Still, we haven’t been to a church either.』

『There wasn’t any good reason to go to one, after all. Besides, if I get called to the Creator God’s realm, there’s no telling when I’d be able to return.』

『Since we have the opportunity, why don’t we try going to both? It’s not like I don’t understand why Ain prefers to avoid those places, but I think it should be alright now.』

The reason I didn’t want to approach the church is because I believe that they could be highly hostile against Song Princesses. If I ever get discovered, we’ll either be captured or dead… Either way, I didn’t think it would end well for us. Additionally, the church must have their own Job identifying sorceric tools, which is why I exercised great caution against them.

While the fact that I’m a Song Princess hasn’t changed, even if I were discovered, I don’t plan for us to get captured or killed; most of all, being the daughter of Mother Fii, I don’t believe the church would treat us lightly.

While exposing my relationship with Mother should only be the last resort, our circumstances are different from when we were active back in Estoque, not only strength-wise but also in terms of support system. That’s why Ciel is correct in thinking that it should be alright now.

『We might have to bring Palra or Belltina to the church if they happen to get injured, so let’s try visiting. As for the temple…』

『Will we be given an oracle, perhaps?』

『I feel like we’d be given one, yes.』

While I can personally heal them, I don’t intend to expose myself to being a Song Princess, and there’s no telling what could happen in the near future. Maybe they’d get invited to a hunter party during the holidays, and there’s no assurance that they won’t get injured during that. Even if you can perceive approaching monsters, accidents can still happen.

As for meeting the Creator God in the temple, I feel like she’d grant an oracle if asked. Last time, it took around 3 days for me to recover because of my mental state, so maybe it’ll only take a few hours to return this time.

In any case, just as Ciel suggested, I decided to head to the church.

---

It’s been approximately 13 years since I came to this world―to Ciel’s side, and this is our first time going to a church-related establishment.

I can’t recall when I heard this, but there are gods other than the Creator God, and the church worships one of those gods: Alsharohs, the Goddess of Love, the only god who grants oracles to humans. The Creator God did grant me an oracle, but only Alsharohs grants oracles to humans. In other words, I’m not human―!? I mean, even back then I was already 1/10th divine, so it is hard to say if I’m human.

I don’t really know my status in relation to the gods other than the Creator God. Maybe Alsharohs and the others are of greater divinity than me since I’m half-baked; maybe I’m greater since I’m practically a child of the Creator God, the Highest God. I’ll have to ask the Creator God for verification.

This capital has both a church and a temple, but while anyone can enter the church, the temple is generally exclusive for the people of the church. They do allow non-church-related individuals to enter the temple, but it costs money, and there’s not much point for regular people to go there.

Well, let’s try entering the church first. The church that looks kind of like a castle and probably costs money to enter.

+++

# **182: Church, Chat, and Suspicion**

「Jobs and humanity have been inseparable, granted to us by Goddess Alsharohs’ plea.」

「Was it not granted to us by Goddess Alsharohs directly?」

「That is correct. To be precise, it is said that Jobs were granted to the then powerless humanity by the gods. As Goddess of Love, healing is Goddess Alsharohs’ domain, but she is by no means skilled in battle.」

「So each Job has a specific god that governs over it, I see.」

Lowering the hood, removing the mask, and turning my black hair back to white, I’m back to Ciel―Ailneige―style. As anyone can guess, going to the church in our Ainsel getup would likely cause a ruckus. Honestly, I also wanted to give the reins back to Ciel, but she refused because today is Ainsel Day.

The church has two fairly distant entrances, one that rough-looking people are using and another that regular-ish townsfolk are using. In other words, hunters seem to have their own entryway. Well, having people coming to worship and hunters going through the same entrance could result in trouble―or make it harder for regular people to enter―so this arrangement is understandable.

For now, we tried entering through the regular townsfolk’s entryway. While our outfit leans on hunter fashion, I probably look like a noble lady incognito, and we just had some trouble at the Hunter Guild, so I’d rather not be near a gathering of hunters for a while.

As we entered the church, we were caught by a sister who asked for alms. From a quick scan, they don’t seem to ask from everyone, so they must be only approaching those who seem to have money.

While I’m sure we wouldn’t be barred from entry if we refused, it’s pretty much like giving offerings at a shrine, which I’m used to doing, so I thought of giving alms after discussing with Ciel. I thought about it, but I have no idea how much we should give.

I tried asking how much would be good, but the sister responded, _‘Any amount is more than enough.’_ That doesn’t help me at all, but I guess it might not be good to specify an amount on their part.

『I wonder how much would be good.』

『How about we give 10 large gold coins?』

『That’d be too conspicuous. Well, let’s try around 2 or 3 gold coins.』

『Yeah, that sounds good.』

While Ciel probably wanted to get rid of our excess money with this given opportunity, 10 large gold coins is a bit too much. After all, that’s around a year’s worth of our dormitory room rent. Honestly, 2 or 3 gold coins is not an amount to easily give away either, but if the sister already suspects that I’m a noble, this should be the right amount for a noble visiting in secret.

However, after actually handing it over, the sister was completely taken by surprise, so I decided to ask for a simple guide around the area. Either due to the amount or due to confirming―in her mind―that I’m a noble, she gladly undertook the request, and now she’s currently giving explanations while leading me through a long hallway of doors.

Specifically, she talked about the gods and Jobs, but on the topic of Jobs, it sounds like there are parts where I’m more knowledgeable. For example, in regard to how the Creator God was the one who created the foundation of the Job system.

Speaking of gods, other than Alsharohs, she also spoke about the God of Technology Mehtestos, the God of War Quacres, the God of Sorcery Waltorus, and the Chief God Tyrnorus.

Like how both Quacres and Tyrnorus were in love with Alsharohs, and so on and so forth; I feel like I’ve already heard this somewhere, and I’m honestly not interested.

While she continued her exposition, when we reached the chapel, the sister immediately stopped speaking. The chapel, bathed in the kaleidoscopic light from the stained glass windows, looked so divine; this is probably a popular tourist spot. 『It’s a beautiful place.』 Ciel even explicitly praised it, scoring it additional points for me.

If the sister actually fell silent so we could have a proper look, she’s quite the considerate person.

「It’s such a beautiful place. The air here feels so soul cleansing.」

「Yes. It’s a bit presumptuous for me to say, but we take pride in our chapel’s beauty.」

Seemingly delighted by my words, the sister cheerfully responded.

「Is the statue in front that of Goddess Alsharohs?」

「That’s right. I have been told that this statue of the goddess has been here since this church’s construction.」

「It’s… a quite splendid statue. If it’s alright with you, may I hear more stories about Goddess Alsharohs?」

「If you are fine with what little I know… But before that, could we change locations first?」

「Of course.」

Since it’d be obstructive of us to talk in front of the entrance, I agreed to the sister’s suggestion and sat down on an unoccupied bench. I don’t know if this is an unpopular time or not, but along the long benches arranged in a line, there is only one person offering a prayer and another reading a book.

Perhaps the sister is not allowed to sit down, as despite there being available sitting space, she remained standing.

「Now then, I would like to apologize in advance, but other than what I have shared earlier, I don’t really have that much I can share about Goddess Alsharohs. Is there anything specific that you would like answered?」

「You said that Goddess Alsharohs is the only god to speak to humans, but do you know what words she had said?」

「That, I can answer. Most recently was when I had just been born; she had apparently announced that a powerful monster was to appear by the frontier lands. Some time before that was, “Impart our teachings to more people.”」

If she had just been born, could it be around 20 years in the past? Perhaps she’s even younger than that, but the last oracle is still more recent than I expected. Personally, that’s somewhat suspicious enough for me; the second-to-last oracle is a lot more dubious on whether it was actually spoken by the Goddess. After all, Alsharohs… or rather, the church does not forbid the worship of other gods. The church is likely this world’s most widespread religion, so I find it hard to believe that it would need to be spread more.

There is a chance that Alsharohs meant it as spreading her and the other gods’ teachings, but it’s still fishy. Most of all, the sulking god the Creator God mentioned is likely to be Alsharohs.

「The most famous of her messages is, “Grant healing to everyone impartially.” Following her word, the church impartially heals anyone in need.」

「Goddess Alsharohs must care for us greatly, then.」

「Yes, that’s right.」

Seeing her delighted as though she herself were being praised, this sister must be very pious. Or she’s a good swindler, or I just can’t read her.

「Speaking of healing, what should I do if I wish to request medical treatment?」

Since the previous topic was at a good stopping point, I asked the thing I’m curious about, and the sister’s expression immediately froze. You can practically hear a pin drop in this sudden silence. It’s probably because right after speaking of granting impartial healing, they charge a fee for it.

As I was wondering how she’d reply, she frantically responded, as though to compensate for her silence.

「Are you perhaps injured?」

「I’m currently enrolled in the second academy, and there’s a chance that my peers could get injured. I don’t really know what to do in case we encounter that predicament…」

「Umm, if you inform us, then you will be guided to a dedicated treatment room. If you enter from the other entrance, then there is also a reception desk there… But either way, we will need to ask a considerate amount of alms…」

「Since even the church surely needs money to continue operating, that really can’t be helped.」

「That’s exactly the case. I’m glad to see that you understand. There are occasionally people who immediately turn to anger, you see…」

The sister’s distant gaze is telling of her hardships, but let’s poke a little more. I didn’t want to come here, but since I’m already here, I’ll take all the information I can get.

「Specifically, how much would it cost?」

「A standard miracle would be 2 large silver pieces, while higher miracles would need a few large gold coins.」

「Around what degree of injuries can a standard miracle heal?」

「It can heal a fracture immediately and can also cure certain common diseases. For the higher miracles, it can regenerate recently lost limbs and organs, and can cure more severe diseases. However, when it comes to diseases, there are regrettably many that miracles simply cannot cure.」

The said standard miracle has around the same healing effect as a basic potion and can heal illnesses. If I remember, a basic potion should be around 5 large silver coins, so this should be cheaper. Still, it’s not cheap for the regular populace. For a regular household, it’s probably difficult to afford several miracles in a year.

The most expensive healing likely has a greater effect than the Song Princess’ healing. For the Song Princess, reconnecting detached body parts is the limit; regenerating lost limbs is impossible.

The talk about impartial healing probably refers to providing equal pricing regardless of social status, so I guess that makes sense. While the ideal could be to heal anyone for free, since the church does employ people, they inevitably require money; even nonprofit organizations still need the bare minimum operating capital. Let’s put aside whether the church is nonprofit or not for now.

It likely costs them money to maintain the temples as well.

_Nonetheless, I guess there isn’t any resurrection magic, huh?_ As this thought went through my head, 「However—」 the sister confidently continued.

「—For light injuries, you can get it healed as long as you come to the chapel at a certain time.」

「At a certain time?」

「Yes. It should begin right about now.」

A few seconds after saying so, a song suddenly echoed. It’s a very church-ish song, singing praises for the goddess. I looked around to find where it could be coming from, but I didn’t see anyone who could be the source, and most importantly, this singing felt awfully familiar.

『Isn’t this a Song Princess’ singing?』

『I believe so.』

『It’s my first time hearing a Song Princess who isn’t Ain, but Ain is a much better singer.』

『That’s… Thank you very much. Umm, would it be fine to do a small experiment?』

『Sure, I don’t mind.』

I didn’t mention what I planned to do, but since Ciel gave the permission, I made a small knife wound on my fingertip in a way unnoticeable to the surrounding people. I really didn’t want to wound Ciel’s body, but there is something I really needed to confirm for Ciel’s future safety.

Observing the wound for a few seconds, there was no particular change. The pain is still there, and the blood flow isn’t stopping.

After this, I put up a certain barrier and switched with Ciel, who seemed to have realized my intentions.

Then, the pain slowly but gradually started fading. Ciel glanced at the wound, and the bleeding had stopped, proof that the wound was healing.

I could just let Ciel stay in control as is, but the moment we had proper confirmation, Ciel once again switched with me.

『I suppose I’ll have to leave this one to Ain.』

『I don’t think there’s a need for excessive caution… but in case anything happens, I’ll probably have to be the one to run.』

『So, what are you going to do, Ain?』

『Nothing at all. I was simply proving my suspicion.』

This series of actions was an experiment with a Song Princess’ song. I wanted to see if one can defend against a Song Princess’ abilities, and the conclusion was that only another Song Princess can defend against it. Even shutting out all sound didn’t work, so it can apparently go through my current barrier.

Still, I don’t believe the Song Princess’ debuff can work against Mother Fii, and it shouldn’t work against spirits either, so maybe they can choose whether it can influence them or not. That’ll probably be possible for us when we reach around 50% divinity? Maybe a bit higher.

Anyway, even if it can affect Ciel, it doesn’t seem to affect us when I’m in control, so I guess that’s a relief for now.

Now, about Ciel’s question of what to do about the Song Princess that should be here, I don’t plan on doing anything. While this did increase my suspicion towards the church, unless Ciel wants to help, I won’t be helping, and I don’t think she wants to do anything either.

「Is that… Singing?」

As the song ended, I asked the sister.

「It’s a song that only priests of higher power can utilize, which grants some level of healing to anyone who hears it. As it is channeled through song, people first experiencing it may find it odd―or even distrust it―but it is by no means anything sinister, so there’s no need to be anxious.」

「I see. May I ask who the individual singing may be?」

「That, I unfortunately cannot answer, since I do not know who it is either.」

Are the higher-ups the only ones that know her identity?

Well, digging deeper probably won’t get me answers, so let’s shift to a different question.

+++

# **183: Temple and the World**

「Can anyone receive oracles?」

「Only individuals of certain Jobs, such as the Saintess, can.」

「I suspected as much. I wanted to visit a temple in hopes of receiving an oracle, but it appears that it’s not that easy even among the members of the church.」

「In the end, it all depends on Goddess Alsharohs’ will.」

I, a Song Princess, was able to receive an oracle, though… That aside, it’s giving me a bad feeling.

「Is there a Saintess in this kingdom?」

「There is not. It is said that there is only one capable of receiving an oracle at present, who is currently at the Church headquarters at the Holy State of Ecricoby.」

「Is the headquarters not in Central?」

There being only one sounds a bit fishy to me, but more importantly, the headquarters not being in Central is odd. From my memories, the church headquarters should be in Central, but… Hearing my question, the sister had a wry smile.

「Many people share this very same misunderstanding. It is somewhat complicated to explain, but the church headquarters is located in Ecricoby, while the head temple is located in Central.

Central’s temple is said to be closest to the divine realm, but the one at the headquarters is larger in size and is said to house many acolytes. Unfortunately, I have never been outside of Ausente, so I only know second-hand information.」

「Then would it be better to go to Ecricoby?」

「If size is what you’re going for, then yes… but I don’t think there’s much significant difference. Both of them are very well maintained.」

I don’t plan on going there, but I asked since I wanted to know more about the organizational structure, and this was her response.

It’s difficult to say for sure, but Central and Ecricoby are probably two divided factions. There might be a factional dispute between Central (the head temple faction) and Ecricoby (the headquarters faction). However, since the pope and the person supposedly capable of receiving oracles are in the headquarters, they may have the upper hand.

For now, I got a rough layout of the situation, so this should be enough.

「I see… In that case, I’ll try visiting either of them if I happen to travel by the vicinity. Wait, that’s right. There is also a temple here in Ausente, correct? I would like to visit at least once, but…」

「That would not be an issue at all! Entry will require a small offering, however—」

「Forgive my lack of common knowledge, but is the amount I’ve offered before enough for me to enter the temple?」

「Let me see… if you intend to go by yourself, I believe it should be enough.」

「Thank you very much.」

From my imagination, I thought that the church is where the nobles would give a large amount of alms, but I guess in this world―even if it’s the same organization―it might be the temple where the big money goes. Still, since we’re still children, I guess it won’t cost us that much money.

I feel like Ciel has been giggling every time I’ve spoken for a while now, but I’ll leave that for later.

「Thank you for entertaining my questions. I would like to offer a prayer before heading to the temple.」

「Alright, please take your time. May the protection of the divine be with you.」

For now, I’ve asked about everything she probably has answers for, so I finally freed the sister. Then, I joined my hands together and closed my eyes, mimicking the act of prayer. If I were to pray to anyone, it would only be to the Creator God, since I don’t have any particular attachment to Alsharohs. Thinking about how we were able to leave Estoque before reaching 15 years old thanks to the existence of the Job system, I’m genuinely grateful.

『That reminds me, you were laughing earlier; was there something funny?』

『There’s no deep meaning behind it. It was just so funny how Ain kept on saying insincere things again and again.』

『Now that you say that, it was pretty impressive how I was able to say those without much thought.』

While it’s a bit late to say this, ever since I’ve been with Ciel, I have gotten into more situations where I had to lie, so I ended up getting used to it. Also, since I was confident we couldn’t be harmed even if my lies were exposed and things turned hostile, that confidence may have helped. I still remember the one creature that broke through my barrier in the past, but I’ve grown since then, and I don’t believe there to be many who can land an attack as powerful as Tur of the den’s deepest depths.

And if there was, they probably wouldn’t show their full power for trivial lies.

For that reason, there’s generally no risk of us getting physically harmed. And if insults are thrown against us, I can simply shut out the noise. Rather, unless the insults are directed to me, Ciel probably wouldn’t even mind whatever gets said about her.

『Still, I can’t be too confident.』

『What’s that all of a sudden?』

『I simply recalled that I can’t neglect self-improvement.』

『I see. I’ll do my best not to fall behind Ain as well!』

I opened my eyes and left the church. Now, time for the temple.

---

The temple is on top of a small hill not very far from the church. Considering that we started from the heart of the capital, it’s not a short walk by any means, but they can’t really compromise the temple location for human convenience, so I guess it can’t be helped. In Ausente, the church and the temple are separated, but there are apparently places where they’re a single establishment, so they’re surprisingly flexible when given the chance.

Now, this temple in the outskirts, despite its location―or perhaps due to its location―is a building with immense presence. It has divinely white walls and a large bell; its doors appear to be made from a single whole tree trunk, and with it being wide enough to accommodate a carriage, I can’t even imagine where they found a tree large enough for such an entryway.

No, actually, I’ve seen many such trees deep inside the forests. Due to the threat of monsters, many of them remain growing untouched in areas where people can’t easily reach them.

For this reason, there are places where large millennia-old trees that are normally treated as tourist attractions in my old world can be seen in droves. You’ll need to get through swarms of B-rank monsters to reach those areas, but on the other hand, people who can easily defeat B-rank monsters―like those in A-rank parties―are capable of reaching them.

Carrying a whole tree back would be very difficult, but it probably wouldn’t be impossible for us.

Paying the temple fee, I went inside. This time, I don’t have a guide, so I don’t need to be as conscious of my behavior; but perhaps because they didn’t anticipate anyone arriving, there were no chairs, and I was only allowed up until the entrance to the ceremony area.

Telling them that I’m deeply moved and wish to stay for a while, I then asked if I could take out a seat, and they brought me a chair. It’s one of those expensive-looking chairs that can be found in aristocratic homes.

I thankfully took the seat, then acted pious and prayed.

『If I suddenly stop being responsive…』

『Yup! I’ll wait here until Ain returns!』

Ciel responded with no hesitation. The way she responded made me feel happy and somewhat ticklish.

But I don’t wish to keep Ciel waiting for too long, and making her feel worried is out of the question. If possible, I want to know how long this will take before going to the Creator God’s realm.

Because of this, I instinctively prayed for the Creator God to tell me. And I don’t know if it actually worked, but I then heard, 【Around one hour,】 right next to my ear. The priests around us don’t appear to hear it, as they stayed completely still.

『Then I’ll wait here for around an hour. Still, how long is around one hour?』

『It shouldn’t be that long… but it’s hard to say.』

I’m glad that I got an immediate reply, but is it really just that easy? I guess it is. To begin with, just because I want to go to the Creator God’s realm doesn’t mean that I can actually get there; all that I was told was ‘around one hour.’ Will it really be alright?

Anyhow, I then tried praying for an invitation, and my consciousness suddenly started fading.

---

When I came to be, I was at the familiar garden, in front of a familiar table, facing a familiar lady. I was already sitting down, and the black-haired lady was gracefully tipping her teacup.

「Long time no see, Creator God.」

「It hasn’t been that long, but I suppose it is from your point of view.」

「I’m still 13 years old. Unlike stepmother, I’m still young.」

「There aren’t many things older than me, you know? Being young is nothing.

That said, good to see you here.」

The Creator God welcomed my casual tone without being particularly bothered.

While I can’t be sure if I interrupted her work, since she brought me here, it should be fine. More importantly, I have something I need to confirm.

「How is Ciel’s barrier right now?」

「Same as before. You’re subconsciously maintaining it.」

「That’s good to hear. By the way, how long is ‘around one hour’ this time?」

「I’ve made it so that there’s no difference in your perception and the actual flow of time. We speak here for one hour, and only one hour will pass on the other end.」

「That’s a relief.」

「Overprotective as always, you are.」

To the Creator God’s flabbergasted tone, I merely responded with a smile. Call me overprotective or whatever, but I don’t intend to stop protecting Ciel. I don’t plan on making Ciel separate from me, and I would never―except for occasions like this―separate from Ciel.

「By the way, the oracle this time seems more modest.」

「Would it be easier to understand if I say that Fii’s place has the best signal reception?」

「I get it.」

「Now then, I already know why, but what brought you here?」

I don’t know how much she’s seen through me, but as expected, she knows my main objective.

In that case, no need to hold back; I’ll ask as much as I want. I don’t want to frequently visit church-related establishments, after all.

「First, could you teach me about how divine punishment works in this world?」

「To teach you that, it’ll likely be best to explain how this world came to be first. And the difference between me and the other beings referred to as gods.」

「Can you teach me that?」

「I wouldn’t if you had the intention of committing a taboo, nor would I even consider telling you this if you were a normal human, but you’re satisfied and won’t take any action as long as Cielmer is safe―as long as this world doesn’t move to eliminate her, right?」

The Creator God grinned, her eyes seemingly piercing right through my soul, but since I don’t plan on denying it, I responded, 「That’s right.」

If the world ever considers Ciel an anomaly and acts to eliminate her, I would resist with all I have. But as long as that doesn’t happen, even if this world is revealed to be made only for monsters, I wouldn’t care. Even if there were only monsters remaining and Ciel and I were thrown into the wilderness, we could probably survive it.

Well, since the Creator God has recognized us, the world trying to eliminate Ciel would be preposterous.

「You seem to have some understanding, but that’s not exactly the case.」

「So it’s not like this world is made for monsters’ sake.」

「The monsters are simply a part of the system.」

「It’s the role of monsters to transform miasma into harmless magic power. In this world, at least.」

「Uh-hm. This world is not exactly made for monsters, but the monsters are the most important component in this world. More than the humans, more than the spirits, monsters are the most necessary.」

「I’ve somewhat figured that out.」

I recall feeling that this was the case around when we challenged the den.

Even if humanity goes extinct, the world would probably continue as normal, but if monsters stop spawning, the world would overflow with miasma.

「This world exists to collect and purify the miasma of other worlds.」

Seemingly reading my mind, the Creator God spoke firmly. It seems like this is much larger in scale than I initially thought.

+++

# **184: The World, Gods, and Divine Punishment**

「If, hypothetically, this world were to be destroyed, would that lead to miasma overflowing in various other worlds?」

「Momentarily, yes. Creatures worse than the so-called Demon Lord would be born, cataclysmic disasters would be rampant, and all that. I can just make a quick replacement world, so it’ll be just a small nuisance to me, but from the perspective of mortals, it would be several centuries of day-to-day danger.」

「So would that equate to frequent outbreaks of earthquakes and typhoons in my old world?」

「There’s even a possibility that monsters would appear, but that’s about right. As such, depending on the world, humanity might go extinct. That would simply be the consequence of the said world’s humanity lacking in effort.」

That’s just like the Creator God, I guess; her response really shows that she’s a God of Worlds. I think it’s been mentioned before, but the Creator God is not a God of Humanity. Alsharohs and the other gods known on the surface seem to be Gods of Humanity―similar to gods of mythology.

Personally, I align more with the Creator God’s stance, but that’s just my opinion; we’re talking about the taboo right now. From the conversation so far, I already have an inkling of what counts as a taboo, but just to be sure, humanity’s position is important to know.

「Now then, about this world, there was originally no plan of having humanity born here.」

「The purpose of this world seems achievable enough by the monsters themselves, after all.」

「I properly configured it that way. At the very beginning, Fii and the spirits didn’t even exist. It was a world of nothing but monsters. That all changed when humanity came to this world.」

「The first of humanity came from another world?」

「They apparently escaped from a place that was under no god’s jurisdiction. And since my intention was to generally leave this world alone, I noticed them far too late. By the time I discovered them, they had already started adapting to life in this world.」

So humanity arriving was outside of the Creator God’s expectations, huh. To be exact, they were probably outside of her perception. Had they been visitors from a world made by the Creator God, she likely would have immediately noticed.
