So at this point, there must be another world-creating god other than the Creator God, but enough of that for now. It’s completely unrelated to this world.

「Did you try to remove them?」

「I considered doing so at first, but by the time I found them, they had even made the framework of what eventually became sorceric tools, so I allowed them to settle down after deciding on some rules. The act of breaking those rules is my taboo.」

And that’s how it is. I also understand now that sorceric tools have a special status. Since sorceric tools need magic cores to operate, they actively accelerate the purification process, and the act of defeating monsters in order to obtain magic cores aids in it as well. Humanity’s role is to help with the purification process, but in the Creator God’s eyes, I guess it doesn’t really matter if they exist or not.

「Since this world was never made to be inhabitable, spirits were sent in to transform it into one that humanity―and other living creatures―could properly live on, and as their numbers increased, the den was created to both secure a living space for monsters and to make it difficult for powerful monsters to spawn near humanity’s living areas. Fiiyanamia was assigned the role of managing the den where the one you two named Khyturi resides in.」

I nod in agreement to the Creator God’s statement. Were strong monsters quarantined as an act of mercy for humanity to not easily go extinct? Or was their containment requested by another god? If it’s the latter, I’m honestly impressed with that god… Am I being blasphemous right now?

「You should be higher than her in terms of divine status. Since you have me as something of a patron, the other gods can’t be careless with you.」

「I see. What about you, Creator God?」

「My actual body is among the highest of divinities. This one is around high-grade in divinity.」

「Is that so? In that case, what would I be in the future?」

「Eventually, you’ll be just a bit lower in status than this fragment of me, I think? Though there’s no telling what the state of this world will be by that time.」

「That sounds like a very long time.」

「That’s the nature of my existence. Now then, back to our discussion.」

I nodded in response. I might need to be concerned about it eventually, but I don’t think this issue can be resolved in one lifetime, much less tomorrow, so there’s no particular reason to ask about it now.

「When speaking about taboos, there’s a need to differentiate based whose rules are being broken, but my rule in general is for humanity to continuously live dependent on magic cores—and so the taboos for me are things that greatly transgress this.」

「So the development of sorceric tools that don’t require magic cores, the invention of an energy alternative to magic cores, finding ways to inhibit the spawning of monsters—and other things like those, right?」

「That should be most of it, I suppose. It doesn’t really count if it’s just on a small scale, but those that would greatly affect the world would break the rules.」

「What about the optimization of the energy usage of sorceric tools?」

If this isn’t allowed, then what I’ve done before would be crossing the line, so it should be alright to some extent. But there is a chance that I was specially overlooked.

「As a general rule, if you’re using a magic core, then it’s good. No matter how optimized it is… Actually, the more optimized it becomes, the more accessible sorceric tools will be, resulting in the total increase of magic core usage. As for alternative energy, I do allow it to some extent. Otherwise, burning wood to cook wouldn’t even be possible.

However, things like thermal and hydroelectric power generation are transgressions. As a rule of thumb, technologies that rely on magic cores are permitted, while those that make magic cores obsolete are not.」

In other words, electricity itself isn’t forbidden, and electric power generation through the use of magic cores is still acceptable. Rather, since it could require a large amount of magic cores, it might be a welcome development for the Creator God. I glanced at the Creator God for confirmation, and she directed a cheerful smile at me.

Even if I’m able to generate electricity, I don’t really know how to utilize it, so I hope it gets naturally discovered and popularized on the surface.

「Besides this, the other acts that are considered taboo are those that were decided by the gods born in this world—the first people who settled on this land—and so those are unrelated to me.」

「Wait, hold on.」

I needed some time after the sudden revelation. I considered the possibility, and there have been myths of humans becoming gods even in my old world, so it shouldn’t be that absurd of an idea. Still, hearing this so suddenly was just too much for my mind to process.

In short, those former mortal gods are―

「The individuals recognized as gods by the people of this world, yes.」

「… That explains why even the names of gods who never give out oracles are known.」

「Their names could have remained in written records, too. These gods are individuals who were worshiped by people and satisfied various conditions for divine ascension. They are a bit different from you; in a sense, they’re natural-born divinities.」

「They seem quite close to humanity.」

「After all, from their eyes, the humanity of this world are like their own children.」

At the very least, humanity undoubtedly descended from their generation, so I can understand them having the urge to help as much as they can. While it may not be the case at present time, they must have been more proactive with helping in the past.

That is greatly different from the Creator God’s stance, but since the Creator God has allowed it, it doesn’t seem like they are particularly going against the Creator God’s wishes.

「What is the difference between the taboos you’ve established and theirs?」

「I guess, from humanity’s perspective, only those that get hit by divine punishment are mine.」

「So Goddess Alsharohs and the other gods’ taboos are less breaking an established rule and more disobeying their requests?」

「There aren’t any specific penalties for breaking theirs. Being viewed badly by a higher-order being can be considered a penalty, but it’s not an issue for those that don’t care.」

No matter how many taboos you commit, if those aren’t the taboos established by the Creator God, you probably won’t die. Well, I don’t intend to actively commit taboos to begin with, and I don’t even know the taboos of Alsharohs and the other gods.

「Well, it’s reduced to a formality at this point. If you’re curious, you could ask Alsharohs about it herself… but she’s currently sulking, so I don’t know if she’ll hear you out.」

「Ah, I knew it… the one who was sulking really was Goddess Alsharohs.」

Since Alsharohs is the only one who gives oracles, she must have been the one to speak about the taboos. And I suspect that the reason she’s sulking is due to people repeatedly committing taboos.

「About that, she actually isn’t the only one giving out oracles.」

「Is that so?」

「She simply does it in far greater frequency and the church doesn’t catch every instance of oracles happening, which is why it appears that way.」

Of course, it’s also possible the church deliberately kept some of the oracles it discovered out of public view. This is this, that is that. The church―it might be more proper to call it the church of Asharohs―doesn’t openly reject the existence of other gods, but it may still take steps to ensure Alsharohs appears preeminent.

「Can’t they give out divine punishments?」

「The most they can intervene with the surface is by giving oracles, minor divine protections… and unleashing large-scale disasters capable of wiping out entire cities. I don’t allow the last one, so they probably won’t.」

「So they really can’t do much intervention?」

「At the end of the day, divine power is, well, powerful. And broad-sweeping. There would be significant consequences if this world accidentally gets destroyed, so I’ve exhaustively told them not to intervene too much.

Though I did practically give them the Job system in exchange.」

In exchange for not allowing them to directly intervene, they were given the Job system―does that mean that the gods have some level of influence on what Jobs would be granted to people? Rispelgia has proved that Jobs have a connection to divine power, so maybe it also goes both ways.

「I vaguely recall them giving Jobs like Saintess and Divine Envoy to mortals they favor. But I specifically forbid them from giving bad Jobs to those they don’t like.」

「If that was possible, it could be used to manipulate humanity as a whole. People could be threatened with bad Jobs for not worshiping them.」

「In the first place, they can’t really change the Jobs of mortals that frequently. Gods like Tyrnorus have their individual right to specify Jobs reserved for emergencies, you see.」

「Those are Jobs for like the Hero, right?」

「Exactly. It’s so they can choose an individual to resolve possible nation destroying threats in the future.」

「So you’re not intervening in those?」

「It’s not really in my interest. Unless a certain threshold is reached, it’s all theirs to handle.」

If, hypothetically, some major power were to aim for world conquest and start a great war, it probably wouldn’t matter to the Creator God. Acolytes praying for monsters to stop spawning due to their danger would probably be more troublesome for her.

Unlike animals, monsters can spawn even in wastelands, so if the surface was burned to ruin, this world would still be capable of serving its function.

「I learned a lot about taboos. By the way, do you know anything about the individual attempting to commit a taboo in the academy?」

「All I know is that they’re in the academy you’re in.」

「They are actually in the academy, right?」

「At the very least, their presence is near you whenever you’re inside the academy. That’s all I know, and since they’ll just get automatically eliminated after committing the taboo, I don’t really mind if you ignore them.」

「I suppose it feels that way from your perspective.」

Mother Fii used this as a reason to send us out, but it didn’t particularly seem like she needed us to resolve it. It probably was just a convenient reason to have us attend the academy. After all, without it, we wouldn’t really have any reason to go out of the way to attend school.

So for this matter, I guess we could just find the suspect to pass time and ask for their reasons.

「But let’s see. While it is merely a tiny tiny bud that could threaten the world, if you can resolve this issue in a way that the divine punishment doesn’t occur, I’ll grant a single wish of yours. Though as with before, there’s a limit to what I can grant.」

「Are you sure?」

「Despite appearances, I am a god who has observed many mortals, you know?」

I suppose she means that she has seen people losing motivation after losing their goals. While it’s true that I am a bit disappointed about my objective being reduced to a simple pastime, I’m surprised that she’s motivating us like this. There must be a catch―or so I assume, but I don’t think there’s really any reason for the Creator God to be scheming against me.

「Oh, that’s right. If the divine punishment does end up occurring, it’s impossible for you to block it no matter what. Keep this in mind, alright? At worst, you might end up dying, too.」

「―Understood.」

My power doesn’t even measure to the divine punishment―to the Creator God’s strength. I’m already aware of how wide our power gap is, but since she intentionally mentioned it, then she must think that there’s a chance that I’d protect the suspect.

Nonetheless, excluding Ciel, the people I would personally consider protecting would be Palra, Belltina, and maybe the princess. Even if it ends up being one of them, I’m unlikely to risk my life protecting them. Though now that I said that, this honestly applies to everyone except Ciel.

「Now then, shouldn’t it be about time for you to return?」

「That’s true. I’d rather not be away from Ciel’s side for too long.」

「Not even an hour has passed since you’ve arrived here, but things have gotten a bit interesting on her end; I’ll be enjoying it from here.」

For now, I’ve asked everything I wanted to know, so I obediently returned as suggested, but the Creator God’s last words were pretty ominous. _What does that_―before I could finish my thought, I returned to Ciel’s side.

+++

# **185: Return, Girl, and the Church**

Returning from the Creator God’s realm, Ciel was still on the chair at the temple. That’s not particularly weird; I mean, the date hasn’t changed, but I am surprised she waited for me here the whole time.

Still, I guess if she leaves the temple or a place that serves the same purpose, there is a possibility that I can’t return to her. In that case, I’ve done a bad thing to Ciel. I’ve made her spend a long time with nothing to do… Or so I mused to myself, but I immediately remembered what the Creator God said before I returned.

「Goddess Alsharohs is really wonderful, isn’t she!」

「… I see.」

A familiar-looking girl was talking to Ciel. Her attire was similar to the other sisters’, only somewhat more lavish-looking, and she seemed to be of Ciel’s age bracket. She’s shorter than our class average height―still taller than Ciel, though―with bright tawny hair and golden yellow eyes. She gives off the impression of a really cheerful girl.

The gap in her and Ciel’s enthusiasm is striking; while the girl is speaking with great excitement, Ciel isn’t even hiding her bothered expression. In a sense, her being able to talk to Ciel despite this is quite amazing, isn’t it?

『I’ve returned.』

『Welcome back.』

Saying so, Ciel chuckled in a voice audible only to me. If we were not in the temple―and if this girl wasn’t here for Ciel to hide her adorable expressions―Ciel might have greeted me with a beaming smile, and missing that chance has me feeling frustrated. That aside, I don’t know why she chuckled, so I’ll try asking her. The girl remains engrossed in her own monologue and doesn’t appear to notice any change.

『Did something funny happen?』

『I’ve never had to greet Ain like this, after all. So I’m feeling a bit happy.』

『Now that you mentioned it, that is true.』

We’ve previously exchanged welcome home greetings whenever we return to where we stay, but situations like this where we reunite after being separated don’t really happen very often. I think we experienced a similar situation two more times in the past? But we weren’t in any condition to calmly express ourselves back then, so this is the first time.

『By the way, can I ask what’s going on here? I can somewhat guess from what I can see, but―』

『It’s not that complicated; she just suddenly started a conversation, and I responded arbitrarily. So I honestly can’t remember much of the conversation. If I recall it correctly, I think she approached me because I was alone for so long?』

Ciel must have been sitting for a long time, so perhaps the girl thought that Ciel was deeply pious or that she was admiring the temple and must have had interest in it.

I don’t know if she approached Ciel by her own initiative or if she was instructed by someone else, but her starting a conversation without being prompted is quite troubling. It makes me hesitant about coming to the temple in the future.

『Do you know who this girl is?』

『She said she’s Sheleight from the same class. She seems to be one of the people around Juerd.』

『That explains why she looked familiar.』

Since we’ve been avoiding interaction with Juerd, I only have a vague recollection, but I sort of remember her being with him.

The reason Ciel noticed this is because the girl mentioned us previously declining the invitation to gather herbs together. She apparently heard it from Juerd, so she must be one of her followers.

Being affiliated with the church, she seems to value cooperation and helping one another, so she didn’t have a good impression of us due to the cold shoulder treatment. As such, she was surprised to see Ailneige coming to the temple, so she talked to Ciel out of curiosity.

After that, Ciel responded to her arbitrarily, so her personal assessment of us as of now is a mystery. Based on the current situation, however, she doesn’t seem to think badly of us. Since she seems to be quite pious, perhaps she’s reciting the teachings in an attempt to make us into better people. The reason she’s with Juerd could be because they share the same ideals, or because she found him to be pure and noble, I suppose.

『Since today is my day, would you mind if we switch places now?』

『… Understood.』

The reason Ciel was somewhat displeased was probably because she didn’t want to switch me into a bad situation like this. Otherwise, she would have gladly switched out.

Even after we switched, Sheleight continued talking, but I unconcernedly interrupted her chattering.

「I’ve been a bit curious about this for a while now, but are you different from the other sisters, Miss Sheleight?」

「—? Oh, yes! I am a saintess candidate.」

「Is becoming a Saintess something that one can work towards? If my memory serves me right, I believe that it is a Job…」

「While I would also love to have the Job, I’m referring to the occupational post of saintess.」

So it’s not the Job from this world’s Job system, but the actual work and occupation kind of job; perhaps something similar to a title, or as she said, an official position. After all, it’s not like Swordsman Job holders in this world can’t become farmers.

「To be granted the Job of Saintess, it’s said that one must help and be a guidance to many people. But only a very few people have become a Saintess that way. On the other hand, most of the Saintesses of history were granted the Job from the very beginning.」

Job changing, huh? Ignoring whether her methods are correct or not, I suppose that could be possible. Just as how children of royalty are born with the 「Royalty」 Job, there should be exceptions among Jobs. Due to that, being able to change one’s Job after already acquiring one shouldn’t be out of the question.

However, since people generally only take a Job assessment once when they reach the age of 10, it’s difficult to confirm. If changing Jobs is possible, it would probably require an experience of similar extremity as those that result in a significant increase in magic power.

「Then you must be working hard for other people’s sake.」

「Ehehe… It’s a bit embarrassing to admit, but yes. However, it’s not just because I want to become a Saintess… That’s why, Miss Ailneige, you too—」

「Miss Sheleight, what sort of people do you help?」

Since the conversation was getting bothersome, or rather because she seemed to be trying to rope us into helping people, I changed the topic.

Seemingly surprised, Sheleight opened her eyes wide but then had a knowing expression as she answered.

「I personally believe that we must be impartial to all, including those with Misfortunate Jobs.」

「So there are people who think otherwise, then?」

「… _Umm_, yes. There are factions who think that way.」

She answered in a low volume only after checking her surroundings. Perhaps she can’t speak too loudly about factional issues.

In that case, I’ll take the chance to ask in more detail. After all, Sheleight herself has confirmed that there aren’t any people nearby, and she was willing to answer. In truth, there is actually someone observing us, but I’ve put up soundproofing.

「Is there a faction of the church that doesn’t acknowledge Misfortunate Jobs?」

「… That’s right. Jobs were granted by the gods for the betterment of people’s lives. So they believe people with Jobs that can’t fight monsters or directly aid in people’s daily lives are people forsaken by the gods.」

I’m not sure if she’s supposed to share this much, but maybe it’s actually a popular belief that I just don’t know.

Actions made by that portion of the church could be part of why Disappointing Jobs are looked down upon. Anyway, this should be enough inquiry. If we continue talking, she might assume that we’ve gotten closer, which isn’t a welcome development.

「Thank you for the fruitful discussion. It’s about time for me to leave, so I shall excuse myself.」

「In that case—」

「Please keep up the good work. Now if you’d excuse me.」

Since we both live in the student dormitory, there’s a chance that she might want to return with us, so I quickly shut her down.

I don’t know how she took it, but Sheleight didn’t continue her previous statement but instead said, 「About helping people―」 Since Ciel only gave vague responses earlier, she probably wants confirmation. Well, I’m not giving her that, though.

「I’ll consider it.」

With a swift response, I left the temple. On the way back to the dorm, Ciel asked, 『Will you really?』 and I replied, 『It’s better not to lie, you know?』 With us becoming closer to Palra and Belltina recently, it might be a good opportunity to reassess how we should interact with them.

---

「To think such a thing happened… I should have come along.」

「The plan was to move around as Ainsel today, so there was no helping it.」

「I fully understand that, but still…」

While being cared for by Mia, I reflected on today’s happenings.

Mia is generally Ciel’s conversation partner, but since Ciel has also been talking with other people recently, I’ve also started talking to her more. We randomly switch things up to maintain impartiality. In general, it’s based on who is outside longer?

「If Mia is around even when we’re acting as Ainsel, then there might be people who would find it suspicious.」

「I understand that very well, but still―」

While she’s not expressing it explicitly, Mia must be feeling some discontent since we haven’t had much time with her ever since the start of classes.

I’m sure she’s bored during the day, and from our conversations, it seems like she doesn’t do hunter activities in her free time. While my first thought was, _‘Then why not just go for it?’_ it might still be difficult for Mia to complete requests by herself. She has a habit of getting tunnel vision when focused on a task, so considering that, it’s normal that she doesn’t act on her own.

『Ciel, about tomorrow…』

『Tomorrow’s a day off too, right?』

『Yes. For that reason, why don’t we do hunter activities with Mia tomorrow? In the end, we weren’t able to go out of the capital today.』

『Yeah, that sounds good to me.』

「With that said, why don’t we go do hunter work together tomorrow?」

「Is it truly alright?」

「We weren’t able to do any today. Since Mia will be coming along, we can’t really go as Ainsel, but we’re still free to take a look at the A-rank requests. Accompany Ciel in her hunter activities.」

「Affirmative.」

I spoke in a commanding tone so that she can’t refuse, but, well, I just can’t get used to it. Ciel is just better with this sort of thing, so maybe I should have switched with her. Anyway, we’ll be doing hunter activities―moreover, as low-ranked hunters, which makes it more likely for us to bump into other people―so I want to take some time to think over what we were discussing before heading home.

Since Ciel and I tend to have a biased way of thinking―or rather, we’re out of step with common sense―maybe it’s a good idea to have Mia, who still has the typical mindset, give her opinion as well.

「Mia, if there is someone in need of help, what do you think should be done?」

「Is it about what happened at the temple? Wouldn’t it depend on the circumstances?」

「Fair point.」

Helping everyone who may be in trouble really is a fool’s errand, and I personally would rather not get involved. I don’t need thanks or appreciation; I just want to live in peace.

「What you two―Lady Ainsel is most apprehensive about is the trouble that might follow after helping others, correct?」

「Generally, yes. There was an incident where we helped a carriage under monster attack, only to nearly be sold into slavery as a reward.」

「I don’t think I could ever forgive someone capable of that… but in that case, why not help only when you can do so discreetly, or when you believe it’s truly deserved?」

「That’s more lenient than I expected.」

「If you try to help everyone simply because you can, there will never be an end to it. That said, it’s probably best to intervene in situations involving life and death. If you turn a blind eye to those too often, others will come to see you as cold-hearted.」

With the way Mia said it, I can’t help but think that that should be good enough. Since we’ve decided to blend in with human society, we also need to meet other people halfway.

『So, in short, we help when it won’t be a burden on us—or when it’s someone we don’t mind being burdened for… I think?』

『That sounds reasonable, but can’t we also just not worry about things that don’t really involve us? Or is helping others something we actually need to do?』

『Ah… that’s a fair point. As long as we follow this country’s rules, we’re not doing anything that deserves criticism, and we’re not truly obligated to help anyone either. I suppose we can just decide when the situation arises.』

『And when it does, we can mull about what to do together! Yes, let’s do that!』

Putting aside why Ciel is so excited for now, it’s a fact that we aren’t obligated to help people. While helping would leave a good impression on the other party, it’s not absolutely necessary for us to help others.

That’s why we should just help those that we want to help and leave alone those that we don’t. That should be good enough. If Palra and Belltina are at risk of dying, we can help them out, but if they’re just having difficulty in completing a request they’ve chosen, we probably won’t help. After hearing Mia’s opinion on this, she said that it’s acceptable, so we’ll go with this line of thought.

+++

# **186: Sumiaria, Enrolled Students, and the South of South**

「Come to think of it, I don’t think I’ve seen many students from other countries in the academy; Mia, do you know why that is?」

As promised yesterday, we are doing hunter work with Mia today. We went to a spot with no people, and I watched over Ciel and Mia as they gathered medicinal herbs.

Out of the blue, a thought popped to mind, so I asked Ciel to switch out and inquired Mia. To be honest, I would have preferred if Ciel asked this question in my stead, but she probably doesn’t understand my rationale―it’s likely not even interesting for her―so considering the flow of the conversation, I decided to take control.

Hearing my question, Mia paused her working hands for a moment and turned to me, muttering, 「Let me see.」

「My lady, how much do you know about world affairs?」

「I barely know anything about it. Before arriving at Central, I didn’t have the leeway to be concerned about it, and ever since arriving at Central, it still didn’t pique my interest. While I do know that Estoque doesn’t recognize non-human races, I don’t really know why that is the case.」

「Then how about the church’s stance towards other races?」

「I know even less about the church, but I did hear that there are factions with different opinions of Jobs.」

Jobs were granted by the gods, so there are those that believe people with useless Disappointing Jobs must have been forsaken by the gods and those that believe otherwise.

Continuing that line of thought, it isn’t particularly difficult to guess how they might treat non-human races.

「In that case, are races that don’t possess Jobs a target of discrimination?」

「There are factions that discriminate, but the church as a whole considers them good neighbors. Even elves and dwarves can utilize church services like any other people.」

「So they recognize them, huh.」

「… That’s right.」

Was Mia’s reluctant nod due to her knowing that nearly all factions of the church don’t recognize Song Princesses, or because she feels bad about me knowing this fact? Or perhaps I’m just reading too much into it. Without answering my inner doubts, Mia continued her explanation.

「Returning to world affairs, Estoque holds ideals similar to those of the church. Like them, they are critical of Misfortunate Jobs. And much like the church, they view the other races as fundamentally different—but unlike the church, Estoque harbors outright disdain for them. While the church at least makes public efforts to build bridges, Estoque doesn’t even pretend to try. That’s the greatest difference between Estoque and the church.

Because of that, some people even refer to it as a kingdom founded by the church’s racist faction.」

「But Estoque isn’t actually acting against church doctrine, are they?」

「Apparently, the scriptures don’t specify how other races should be treated, so technically, no. Partly because of this, very few people from Estoque choose to study at Ausente, where other races are accepted and commonly seen, even in towns and villages.」

「Still, that doesn’t mean there are no students from there at all, right?」

If I recall, there isn’t much non-human discrimination in the rural areas. Besides, there should be people willing to turn a blind eye to the presence of other races in order to obtain technologies.

And it seems that I wasn’t wrong, as Mia nodded in agreement.

「True, having zero students from them is unusual. Not only are there none in your grade, there aren’t any in the other years as well; it’s unprecedented.」

In that case, should I assume that something has happened in the past few years? Maybe the relations between Estoque and Ausente have soured, or so.

There is one incident that I think could be related, but that should have happened a little more than a year ago, so while there being no students a year above us is understandable, it shouldn’t affect the students two years above us, should it?

That’s what I thought, but contrary to my assumptions, Mia brought up the said incident from a little more than a year ago.

「What triggered this was Royal Capital Estoque’s stampede. However, you may be more knowledgeable than I am on that topic.」

「That may be the case… but does it really affect all years?」

「It’s an affair that is concerned with their nation’s survival, after all, so their enrolled students must have rushed back to the kingdom.」

「Is that how it is?」

「That is how it is.」

When you put it that way, I guess that’s how it is. It’s been so long since I last felt any sense of patriotism, so while I can understand the logic, I can’t really relate to it.

Still, thinking about it more, most of the students abroad should be nobles; they probably have a stronger sense of duty towards their homeland compared to the people in my old world. At least, to the point that they feel the need to return home when there’s a disaster happening. They can surely provide some help in the reconstruction, no matter how small, and if they didn’t return home and simply ignored the chaos, they’d probably be criticized by their people. There’s even a chance that it could lead to other nobles taking advantage of their absence against them.

「Moving on to Eusreuk, for the past few years… no, few decades, their nation has been experiencing turbulent times, so they don’t really have children studying abroad.」

「In the south, right? Isn’t there also an empire further south of them?」

「Yes. This very turbulence is due to their conflict with that Empire.」

「I don’t really know much about that part; why did the conflict between the two nations happen?」

I completely forgot Eusreuk, but Estoque, Ausente, and Eusreuk are the three great nations. With the Empire included, they’re considered the great four, if I recall. I asked Mia for more information, and she provided me with more context.

「Estoque, Ausente, and Eusreuk were originally called the continent’s three great nations. Among them, the king’s ruling hand is most felt in Eusreuk, and it’s said that the burden on the commoners is far greater compared to other nations. Anguished by this, Marquis Digratoria of Eusreuk began a revolt, won the favor of the surrounding lords, and named themselves the Empire.」

「What was the other countries’ reaction?」

「Most simply observed. Marquis Digratoria’s frontier lands did not border any other nation. Instead, they bordered the wildlands—the monster-infested region south of Eusreuk. Not only were there no neighboring countries to contend with, but the territory itself lay deep within Eusreuk’s heartland.

Because of this geographical reality, no foreign power would intervene unless Eusreuk explicitly requested aid. Eusreuk initially believed the rebellion could be swiftly suppressed, but the Empire managed to amass enough influence to fracture the nation. Then, by publicly declaring that it had no intention of waging war against any country other than Eusreuk, the Empire effectively reduced the likelihood of outside intervention.」

In other words, the Empire wishes to take down Eusreuk’s foolish king and bring peace to the land. For some reason, being called the Empire gave me the impression that their goal was to unify the continent, but it sounds like they’re more like a coup or a liberation army. That’s if the Empire’s claim can be trusted, that is.

「Did they really believe that statement so easily?」

「It doesn’t particularly appear that way. Marquis Digratoria’s frontier lands―currently the Empire’s entire territory―are said to have strength tempered by the daily struggle with the bordering wildlands. When they sent messengers to the other nations, they sent powerful individuals, leading to the nations deciding to stay observers as they anticipated great losses if a battle broke out.

Based on the rumors, the messengers sent were around the strength of S-rank hunters.」

「That sounds dreadful.」

「An S-rank serves as enough of a deterrent by themselves, after all.」

『If it’s Munyechka as the messenger, I can understand. I wouldn’t want to fight her myself.』

『Munyechka can probably create an army by herself. If it’s someone at the same level as her, even if you defeat them, the damages would be too large to celebrate victory.』

Just as Mia said, an S-rank alone can serve as a strong deterrent. Even I can apparently bring a country to its knees by myself, so with messengers like that, there really isn’t much of a choice but to accept their claim. Otherwise, you could also deem the fact that they sent such a powerful messenger as a declaration of war instead.

If taken as a declaration of war, there’s a chance that the S-rank might thrash wildly in the heart of your capital, so in the end, you still have no choice but to accept them. The best way to avoid this is to not let them into your countries to begin with. Just because they’re a messenger, why did they allow what’s practically a human weapon capable of demolishing entire settlements inside their walls?

Regarding that, I do know of a similar situation having occurred, so I understand why it was probably impossible to stop on their end.

『The empire’s S-rank messenger could be the one Munyechka was talking about.』

『The person who defeated a dragon?』

『Likely so.』

In other words, the countries did not have prior information. That’s why they welcomed the messenger so easily. Considering that several countries received the messenger, the S-rank was likely not _a_ singular messenger but multiple individuals. So a full party must have defeated the dragon. Well, dragon slaying would normally be a combined effort, I guess.

I wouldn’t even dream of fighting a dragon alone. It’s only a possibility with Ciel by my side.

「They have that much strength, so why have they still not achieved their goal after all these years?」

「Since they’re also occupied with the wildlands, it’s likely that the manpower they can mobilize is limited. On the other hand, if Digratoria is defeated, Eusreuk will have to deal with the wildlands themselves. If left alone, it may result in the second coming of Estoque’s disaster, perhaps even worse than that, so Eusreuk and the other countries can’t tread lightly.」

And because of the recent stampede outbreak in Estoque, Digratoria’s importance has inevitably increased. I don’t know what kind of people live there, but since they have multiple S-rankers, they should be able to manage even a large-scale monster stampede. And in terms of compatibility, Ciel and I alone are probably capable of quelling one ourselves. As long as I can attract a majority of the monsters, Ciel can handle the rest on her own.

However, since the said wildlands are said to house strong monsters, perhaps there are S-rank monsters there as well. If that’s the case, then quelling it with zero casualties might be difficult.

Anyway, the situation in the south is currently in a delicate equilibrium that could tip one way or the other with the slightest push. It’d be great if they just keep the stalemate going―but that’s being too optimistic, so I’d prefer we don’t go anywhere near it. When will we ever see the oceans of the south?

「And that is why it has become difficult for the other great nations to send children to study abroad. However, there have been a considerable number of students from the small western nations.」

「Is that so?」

「It wasn’t particularly important, which is why you weren’t taught about them. Some of the famous ones are the Elf and Dwarf Kingdoms.」

「I did notice an elf student.」

「As long-lived races, they don’t particularly produce children every year, so just having students from them is rare enough. Anyhow, the high nobles of the smaller nations have around the same level of influence as the lesser nobles of the four great nations.」

Which is why we don’t need to be concerned about them. How cruel. But that’s just how the world is, I suppose.

「I understand it better now. Thank you, Mia. By the way, have you found the medicinal herbs?」

Giving my thanks, my next question then caused Mia to have a troubled look. It seems like she stopped searching while we had our conversation. While that may be normal to do, for Mia’s training, I really hope that she eventually becomes capable of looking for herbs while maintaining a conversation.

After that, I switched with Ciel, and we continued our tasks.

+++

# **187: Class Sparring and Chat with Palra**

With a sharp whistle, a practice-use longsword landed right next to Ciel. Before she could launch a counterattack, the male student holding it let out a sharp yell while forcefully swinging his longsword horizontally. I was looking at Ciel from a bird’s-eye view, and this took me by surprise, so it must have been scarier from Ciel’s perspective, but she didn’t appear to be fazed as she calmly avoided it with a back step.

This was a scene from today’s Combat Training. After several meetings and with many skilled individuals around, we’ve started to shift to sparring matches. However, this only applied to the top students; those with below-average performance have just recently become capable of finishing the running within the class period.

In our party, Belltina is considered an underperformer, while Palra, who has good foundations, is considered on the high end of the class average. While Palra does have an Advanced Job, since she’s training for both the bow and knife in parallel―and due to her natural disposition―she still hasn’t participated in the sparring matches.

Observing the proficiency gap, or rather the difference in progress among the students, you can roughly tell who has what kind of Job. The boy battling Ciel right now, his name is Grimid, I think, likely has a high-tier swordsman-aligned Job―possibly Advanced Swordsman―and the other students who are qualified for sparring likely have at least intermediate-level Jobs.

In contrast, the Jobs of those in the below-average group are harder to infer, since the activities they’re doing might not be aligned to their Jobs. A good example of that are the students who have sorcery-related Jobs.

Now then, it has been a month since the start of the classes, and compared to the first week, we’ve been having more relaxed days. Since the meeting at the temple, Sheleight has started talking to us in the classroom, resulting in Ailneige standing out a bit and gaining some of Mr. Hero’s attention; however, no one has attempted to squabble with us, nor have any nobles abused their status to get close.

While I sometimes wish that Princess Leshimiiya would do something about Sheleight and Juerd, I’m sure there’s a limit to how much she can do, and since there’s a chance that the church could get involved, she probably can’t act carelessly. I could still try asking, but the moment that happens, it could be taken as a _command_ to do something about them, so I’m holding back.

With us periodically having teatime together, I do wish to maintain our pleasant relationship with Princess Leshimiiya, so I want to avoid stressing her out.

「You’re done for!」

As the end of the period was approaching, Grimid, who had been on the offensive for most of the match, let out a rousing roar.

His shoulders rose and fell with ragged breaths until that moment. Then, the instant those words left his lips, his breathing halted and the trembling in his body disappeared as he swung his longsword with all his strength. He should have been worn out by now, yet this attack was faster than any before, enough to make me uneasy about Ciel.

Ciel attacks, and I protect. Considering our roles, I don’t think it’s good of me to think about Ciel possibly losing, but it’s alright to lose in this class, and Ciel is a sorcerer. This is a sword fight where Dance Princess is only at half-efficacy and the physical reinforcement used is only at Ailneige’s level. It’s undeniable that Ciel is at a disadvantage.

In fact, Ciel has been on the defensive for the entire match, and whenever they clashed, she was overpowered. At their age, sexual dimorphism shouldn’t have that large of an influence yet, but Ciel is arguably the smallest student in our class. In terms of pure physical difference, Ciel is at a disadvantage. But at the same time, I realized that Ciel has had a composed expression the whole time.

And it seems like her composure was not groundless, as she was able to parry Grimid’s sword. Swung by his own momentum, he lost balance and fell down with both hands to the ground, with Ciel then pointing her rapier at his nape.

「That’s enough!」

As Mr. Ishparht announced the end of the spar, Ciel sheathed her rapier. Even this simple flowing gesture was enough to charm the eyes of the surrounding audience.

While it isn’t the same for everyone, many of the students watching the spar stared at Ciel absentmindedly, while Grimid alone was scowling at her in frustration.

「I still haven’t…」

The words Grimid whispered behind gnashed teeth were awfully vivid to my ears.

Certainly, Grimid had the initiative for most of the match, so it must be hard on his pride to have lost to someone much smaller than him. Or maybe he’s just a sore loser.

While still unable to accept his loss, Mr. Ishparht turned to Grimid and asked, 「What are your thoughts on this match?」

「I was winning except for the last part,」 Grimid responded curtly, but it seems that he does understand that he was outplayed at the end. Still, for people with combat experience, it must have looked like Ciel had it under control the entire match. After all, Mr. Ishparht didn’t seem to be surprised about Ciel’s victory.

「I see. Then how about you?」

Mr. Ishparht lightly nodded to Grimid’s answer before then turning to Ciel. Ciel showed a contemplative expression for a moment before answering, 「The final yell was unnecessary.」 Hearing that, Mr. Ishparht laughed out loud.

「Still, as a hunter, it’s not necessarily bad to yell out. In fact, there are times when it’s important to do so. Do you know why that is?」

『Is it for party battle coordination reasons?』

『I think that’s a good answer.』

We don’t team up with people much―and when we do, it’s more as an experienced mentor rather than an equal collaborator―so we’ve never had proper battle coordination with others.

While Ciel and I are practically in sync all of the time, I can’t really communicate when I start singing, so communicating to coordinate isn’t really possible for us to begin with.

Still, I do have ideas other than what Ciel said. However, it’s just amateur guesswork, so I’m not telling Ciel. If you think about it, we are at a school, so there’s no need to teach her my uncertain ideas.

Instead of learning that, she can learn the correct knowledge from others.

「It’s important for making coordinated actions as a party.」

「That’s certainly one factor. Particularly for sorcerers and archers attacking from behind, it’s important to raise your voice; otherwise you might accidentally hit your companions. One more utility of yelling is to catch the attention of the enemy as a front-liner; this gives your other party members greater leeway to prepare their spells and can also help raise overall morale.

Even when you’re not up against monsters, it’s still useful to communicate during large-scale battles.」

After giving Ciel that explanation, Mr. Ishparht then turned to Grimid.

「With this information, reflect on why you lost until our next meeting.」

「Ugh… understood.」

Handed an assignment, Grimid nodded with a sour look on his face.

He can probably give an answer right now, but as expected of an educator, Mr. Ishparht wants Grimid to really contemplate about the match. He’ll remember it more than if he was simply told the answer, and more importantly, it’ll help train critical thinking skills.

Since hunters are free to choose their work, you encounter many situations where you really have to think carefully before you act. Even the act of choosing a request to work on requires you to think for yourselves. While hunters are mainly classified by rank, there are individuals who specialize in material gathering and ones who specialize in fighting.

Even among the battle specialists, there are those who have outstanding offensive capabilities and those that focus on keeping the value of the monster’s materials high by subjugating them with as little damage as possible. For your own future growth, you need to be able to reflect on your actions. Otherwise, becoming a high-rank hunter will be difficult―or so they say. We’ve skipped several steps in our promotion, so while Carol did teach us a lot, we lack common sense in a lot of stuff.

Which, I suppose, is why we’re here at the academy.

Not long after Grimid and Mr. Ishparht’s exchange ended, the teachers announced our class period was officially over.

From here on, we are to return to the dressing rooms to change into our uniform for the afternoon homeroom meeting. These days, we walk together with Palra (who we share homeroom with) and Belltina (who we don’t, but is in our party) to our destination. From the second week after the start of the classes, Palra would lend Belltina a shoulder after class since she’d be unsteady on her feet from the physical exhaustion.

The reason why we don’t help―while it’s also partly because Palra does it voluntarily―is because Ailneige can’t really support Belltina with her physique. While we do plan to help if Palra has difficulties, but compared to Ailniege, Palra is much more physically capable, particularly because of her Job. Even if we intervened, our contribution would likely be minimal.

And so today, while firmly holding Belltina’s hand, Palra came right before us.

「You were amazing today, too, Ailneige. I couldn’t take my eyes off of you. I think you’re probably the strongest in our year?」

「Not far in the future, that…」

『Grimid.』

「Grimid would likely be able to overpower me.」

「Really?」

Palra said while tilting her head.

「Really; I’m just a sorcerer, after all.」

「Oh, yeah, that’s right. But you still look really cool when swinging a sword, you know?」

「Thank you for the praise.」

Ciel answered in an obligatory tone, but Palra doesn’t seem to take offense from it at all. This patient nature of hers is probably one of the factors that kept us willing to interact with her.

Palra has gotten more friendly and easy-going than before, but she still never oversteps our personal boundaries. A certain church-affiliated girl could learn from her example.

While chatting here and there, we returned to the dressing room. Before, we changed clothes at our own pace, but recently we’ve been changing together more.

This is mostly to help Belltina change into her uniform, though. Unlike before, Belltina is able to recover enough to be able to change on her own, so you could say that is a vestige of that practice.

Belltina looks like Palra’s little sister when being helped into new clothes; it’s really adorable. It doesn’t happen much these days, but whenever Belltina is especially tired, you can see Palra taking care of her.

It appears that Belltina has really opened up to Palra, as even when she looks well enough to change on her own, she occasionally asks Palra to help her change.

As we finished changing, Belltina reluctantly returned to her class with the look of a calf going to the market to be sold.

While I’ve never actually seen a calf about to be sold before, her face is just filled with sadness. I really hope she can make friends in her own homeroom class. Though if that were easy to do, neither Belltina nor Palra would be suffering as much as they do.

「Ailneige, can we talk a bit after the teacher’s announcements?」

『How should I answer?』

『What do you want to do, Ciel?』

『I think chatting shouldn’t be a problem? No, it might be nice to have a chat with her.』

『In that case, let’s hear her out.』

If Ciel was not inclined to hear her out, I was thinking that I could listen in her place, but since Ciel is willing to go herself, there’s no need to complicate things.

I wonder if this is because Ciel has opened up to the two girls. If that’s really the case, I feel happy, yet also lonely; it seems like I’m never going to outgrow Ciel at this rate. Well, I don’t plan on doing so, though.

「It’s fine. While we’re at it, why don’t we have dinner at the cafeteria as well?」

「Sure, and thanks. Also, do you mean the academy one?」

「There will probably be fewer people, you see.」

「Good point. Okay, I got it.」

『Is that alright?』

『Yes, of course. In that case, however, let’s contact Mia as well.』

『Understood.』

Since bringing attendants is allowed in the academy, you can ask to send a message to your own room. With that, we can inform Mia that we won’t be needing dinner.

Mom might get angry if you eat dinner outside without prior notice, after all. Well, Mia’s not our mom, and she probably wouldn’t get angry, but there’s no need to needlessly inconvenience her.

And so, Ciel sent Mia a message before returning to the classroom.

+++

# **188: Palra, Sorcery, and Idle Chat**

「There really are fewer people around this time, huh.」

「There’s little reason to eat dinner here, after all.」

「Right, the students still need to go back to the dorm.」

It’s after class at the academy cafeteria; time-wise, it’s still early for dinner but a bit too late for tea time. In this awkward midpoint, the number of students in the cafeteria didn’t even reach double digits.

Just as Palra said, you’ll need to go back to the dorm after eating dinner, and while the buildings are on the same premises, the distance between the cafeteria and the dorm is fairly large. Students who would prefer to lounge around and relax in their room after dinner would probably never choose to eat at the school cafeteria. Well, Ciel and I barely use the dormitory dining hall either, though.

Anyhow, we bought dinner and sat at a fair distance from the other students eating.

Just on a whim, I tried looking if there’s someone under the table, but there wasn’t. It was just on a whim, so I’d honestly be shocked if there was.

That aside, the meal Palra purchased has clearly leveled up compared to her previous choices.

She seems to be doing hunter work whenever she finds time, so it must be the fruits of her labor.

「So, what did you want to talk about?」

As we sat down, Ciel questioned Palra. Palra was just about to eat her meal, and this caused her to lower her cutlery and look around restlessly. Moments after, mustering her resolve, Palra stared straight at Ciel.

「Ailneige, you’re skilled with sorcery, right?」

「Enough to make a living as a hunter, yes.」

「Is performing sorcery difficult?」

「There are individual differences, but it may be difficult for you to do sorcery.」

Commoners have less magic power, and her Job doesn’t particularly provide her with the ability to use sorcery. Palra might be able to use sorcery if she gains a deeper understanding of her Job, but it’s certainly not a path normally recommended.

Hearing Ciel’s answer, Palra didn’t appear discouraged but instead had a pensive look.

「Umm… Ailneige, over the course of your hunter career, were there any sorcerers who had difficulty with sorcery?」

「There have been some, but why do you ask?」

Hearing Palra’s question, Ciel tilted her head in puzzlement. I can vaguely guess Palra’s intent, but I want to entrust Ciel with matters relating to Palra and Belltina as much as possible, so I’ll keep to myself. It’s not as if we’d immediately switch if I speak up, so it’s not really a big issue.

「Do you know how that person stayed a hunter despite that?」

「I see… Give me a moment to think.」

Ciel paused the conversation and asked, 『Can I answer this?』

Honestly, it’s a bit complicated. While sharing another hunter’s abilities is a breach of etiquette, it’s not as if you absolutely can’t talk about it. After all, information gathering is a necessary part of a hunter’s repertoire, and the feats of famous hunters are included in the said information. It’s important when you’re searching for party members or collaborators, and if you have hostilities with someone for whatever reason. If you don’t have information about what weapons or sorceries people are proficient with, it’s hard to plan the next move.

Besides, telling others that someone who generally uses a broadsword is a front-liner that uses a broadsword doesn’t count as a breach of etiquette. On the other hand, that’s basically as much as you’re allowed to tell.

Information that anyone can get, or that is easily inferred if you work with that hunter, like one’s general fighting style, should be fine to share. For example, people knowing that I’m proficient at barrier sorcery isn’t really a problem.

『Let’s see… Sharing that the said sorcerer was skilled at consecutively shooting attack spells should be fine enough. Viviana didn’t seem to particularly hide that.』

『I see. I’ll try that then.』

「Alright. Let’s see, what I can say is that she was skilled at performing sorcery quickly.」

With our discussion over, Ciel looked up and relayed the information. For some reason, Palra had an uneasy look on her face before sheepishly responding.

「_U-um_, was I wrong to ask that question, maybe?」

「It concerned a hunter’s tool set, so I was just contemplating how much of it I can speak about. We don’t really share much about things like this, you see.」

「I see, that’s a good point. I’m sorry.」

「Well, it’s not a problem. What I said was just general information, after all.」

「Okay, thank you.」

Ciel was confused about why Palra thanked her, probably because she thinks the thanks is about the sorcery discussion.

That said, Palra should have gained the information she wanted, so this should be good enough. If Ciel asks about this later, I’ll share my opinion.

「So, I’ve been doing more hunter activities recently.」

「Is that so? Please take care to not die.」

「It’s mostly errands done within the neighborhood, so I’m still alright for now. But thank you.」

Achieving her goal, Palra changed to a more casual topic. Since she plans to live as a hunter, there’s nothing to lose from being as active as she can. Even without leaving the walls, she can learn about the Hunter Guild’s framework and general workflow, and the guild branch here is very accommodating to students.

Still, I can’t say that there aren’t any troubles at all, but if we’re nitpicking, it’s not as if there aren’t any troubles between students within the academy either.

「There are some requests that require going outside the walls, but students aren’t allowed to do it alone. Only parties consisting of at least 3, preferably 4, students can do it.」

「Do you plan on taking requests like those?」

「Right now, nope. I’d probably start panicking if I encountered any monsters.」

「That does seem likely. It’s best you avoid it until you gain enough confidence.」

「Though even if I had enough confidence, I don’t really have anyone to go with.」

Palra sheepishly smiled. If it’s only 3 students, then we could go as long as Belltina is on board with it. In the first place, if the active hunter Ailneige is with her, then 2 people should be fine. If not, we could just invite Mia to fill the numbers.

Palra doesn’t seem eager to go outside yet, so we’ll start thinking about it when she starts mentioning the idea.

「Ailneige, you’re also active as a hunter, right?」

「I generally only gather herbs, though. I barely deal with monsters; it’s mostly just me accompanying my party member.」

「Party member?」

「She’s a maidservant that came with me to the capital.」

「… So you do have one.」

We weren’t really hiding Mia at all, but I guess Palra didn’t know, huh. Still, she probably understands that Ailneige is a noble child at this point, so she wasn’t really that surprised.

Perhaps she simply didn’t pay attention to Mia since she’s simply not used to people having attendants with them.

「Is she an adult?」

「An adult, yes. She became a hunter after becoming my attendant.」

「Because you were a hunter… right?」

「That’s right. It’s more convenient that way.」

「Is she the only one who came with you?」

「That’s right.」

If we invited Mohsa and Luna, they’d probably come along; honestly, it did sort of look like they wanted to. I’m not really into walking around with multiple people following us, so I’m glad that it was only Mia.

「That reminds me, they say an A-rank hunter recently arrived here at the capital.」

「I’ve heard the rumors talking about it.」

Perhaps realizing something, Palra changed the topic. This new topic sounds awfully familiar. At the same time, we really haven’t heard about the news ourselves, but Ciel managed to tie into the conversation.

「However, is it that rare for A-rank hunters to be in the capital?」

「Who knows? I heard that there aren’t that many of them, though. Apparently, there are always a few around, but most of them are somewhere else handling different requests.」

「Now that you mentioned it, there don’t seem to be many A-rank requests around here.」

To be exact, even if there are high-rank requests available here, their objectives are at a different location. For example, requests to subjugate monsters in a more remote area, or requests from rural villages for aid.

The former generally come from nobles or research institutions and have low urgency, so you can accept the request at the capital, go to the designated area, and go straight home.

「Yeah. And they say that the hunter in question is small, like student small.」

「Other than being small, is there no other information?」

「I heard the A-rank hunter wears a hood and a mask, so no one knows her true appearance. But some did say that she had a girl’s voice, and the hair peeking from her hood was black.」

「Perhaps she’s an elf? If not, a dwarf?」

If we ignore the fact that it’s just us, the information almost certainly hints at the hunter being from a different race. Well, it’s not like I know much about dwarves and elves, so it can’t be for certain. Palra nods in agreement to Ciel’s words.

「Rumors believe that’s the case, but if she actually turned out to be human, that’d be so amazing.」

「That’s… true, yes.」

I guess that’s the only way Ciel can respond. After all, it’s practically about herself, and Ciel doesn’t really think of herself as particularly amazing.

But the fact that she still agreed with it, albeit awkwardly, might be because she vaguely understands the level of the other people around her.

And Palra’s words seem to be not out of suspicion that Ailneige is the rumored hunter but just her honest opinion. She appears to believe the part about having black hair, after all.

「You could probably become an A-rank hunter, right, Ailneige?」

「Who knows? I don’t really wish to proactively raise my rank, so reaching D-rank would be good enough for me.」

「Really?」

「D-rank is enough for herb gathering, after all, and I already earn enough just from that.」

Well, Ailneige can’t reach A-rank, after all. If we perform enough to reach that far, that’d just be Cielmer or Ainsel, which defeats the point of us even getting a low-rank card.

It’s possible to reach D-rank strictly through herb collection requests, so that’s the finish line for Ailneige. I do hope that Mia aims for A-rank, though.

「Is herb gathering really that good?」

「I know a secret trick to it, you see. I’m not going to share it, but I don’t think there are many that can perform it even with the information anyway.」

「You’ve also subjugated monsters, right?」

「That’s right, but I generally go for subjugation requests that have low compensation and have been long neglected; I don’t really prefer it.」

That’s how Ailneige would be. Ciel’s story is starting to sound a bit inconsistent, but it’s not like it reveals anything significant about us. Adding to the explanation, we also mainly choose low-paying herb collection requests.

We’ve been completing the so-called pickled requests, but the main difference between now and our Estoque days is that we also assertively defeated monsters back then. At Estoque, we defeated monsters that are relatively strong for their rank, resulting in our battle prowess being recognized, and this was probably why we were able to quickly rise in ranks, but we haven’t done that as Ailneige.

Even when we accept subjugation requests, we generally make it appear as if Mia defeated the monsters on her own.

And that’s why our rank has stayed the same. Also, there’s the matter of our age. Cielmer is a different story, since she was abnormally strong, while Ailneige only appears to be fairly capable of fighting for her age. Though I don’t really know other people’s actual opinion of us.

「In the first place, why don’t you proactively want to raise your rank?」

Hearing Ciel’s story, Palra tilts her head in confusion. It’s quite rare for her to show so much interest in a certain topic. Still, Palra aspires to be a hunter. Being her senior and already E-rank, I suppose she wants to hear more about Ailneige’s thought process.

Especially since rising in rank tends to be seen as the goal for a hunter, and not many really settle for D-rank just because it’s enough to pay living expenses.

Rather, there are many that can’t quite rise to C-rank but could have still continued living an above-average lifestyle that instead ruined their lives in desperation.

「What does rising in rank get you?」

「_Umm_, the permission to accept requests with better rewards, I guess?」

「I don’t particularly need the better rewards, you see. I already earn enough from safely gathering herbs, so there’s no need to do dangerous activities.」

「_Hm_… That’s a good point.」

「If A-rank can secure safer hunter work, then I’d find it to be a good goal to aim for.」

Hearing Ciel’s statement, Palra’s eyes went wide open before she nodded with understanding.

+++

# **189: Sound Spirit, Play, and Chat**

「In the end, why was Palra so curious about sorcery?」

Now in our room after the dinner with Palra, Ciel seems to have recalled something that bothered her before. Mia is diligently caring for her right now, but this question is most likely for me. Still, Mia appears to be listening, curious about this topic as well.

『It was probably for Belltina’s sake.』

「Ah, I see. In that case, Viviana’s example might end up being useful for her. Still, why didn’t Belltina ask us herself?」

『I believe she secretly consulted us without Belltina’s knowledge. She seems to be a caring busybody to people she’s close with, you see.』

「So just like Ain, right?」

『I can’t deny that.』

After all, up until now, I have done many things for―or rather, most of what I do is for Ciel’s sake.

I can’t really deny being called a caring busybody at this point. Still, I like doing things for Ciel, and without Ciel, there’s no point in me living in this world. There’s no denying that I don’t have much care for anything other than being with Ciel.

Hearing my response, Ciel let out a graceful giggle, and it seems that Mia finally couldn’t take it anymore, as she spoke to Ciel.

「May I ask what your conversation is about?」

「Do you recall Belltina?」

「The classmate who you formed a party with, yes?」

「Belltina has a similar condition to Viviana, so Palra came to me to gather information, it seems.」

「I see, is that so? Just to validate, Lady Ainsel should be able to resolve her issue, correct?」

While Mia does not necessarily know everything I’m capable of, she does know a lot. She also knows that I was the one who resolved Viviana’s issue, and she probably also knows that Ciel and I have gone to the lowest strata of the den.

「I think so.」

「As to be expected.」

Mia replied with a look of respect, but she didn’t ask whether we would treat Belltina or not. I don’t know if many can perform the same treatment, but most people can’t, so this isn’t something we should do carelessly.

It was a different situation in Viviana’s case, and back then, it was also an experiment to confirm my own capabilities.

Besides, Belltina is also making her best effort, so I don’t want to risk raining on her parade. She’ll probably start training her fundamentals after hearing Palra’s information, and that would only serve to help her regardless of the future.

Besides, I honestly still need time to be able to trust Belltina. Being school friends is different from being actual close friends. In the end, Belltina and us―and frankly Palra―are not very good at socializing.

While I was contemplating to myself, Ciel and Mia continued conversing.

「Still, I’m personally rooting for her.」

「Really?」

「She reminds me of Viviana in the past, you see.」

「Come to think of it, Viviana also has a childhood, huh. Mia, too, and everybody else.」

「And eventually, yours will also―」

Mia was about to say something, but, 「Never mind,」 she held her tongue.

---

It’s late into the night. I previously asked for Ciel’s permission to use the body after she fell asleep, so I took control and sat up on the bed.

Most of the world is fast asleep at this time, so Mia has returned to the attendant’s quarters.

Now for what I plan on doing this late: just a little fun. And while I’m at it, I’ll be playing with the other spirit that’s always with us, the sound spirit. To be honest, there’s no need to do it this late at night. It’s just that I usually borrow Ciel’s body at night.

In fact, there’s even a possibility that doing this so late would make my objective harder to achieve. In that case, this’ll just be a fun time with the spirit.

「Now give it a good try.」

After I said that, the spirit cheerfully started floating around me. Soon after, the sound of knocking on hollow wood echoed to a steady beat.

Following this relaxed percussion, I started to sing.

About the sound spirit, this little one is now capable of producing a good variety of sounds. At first, it could only mimic sounds. Still, it was capable of learning, so I got a bit carried away and made it listen to so many different sounds. As time went by, it eventually became capable of arranging the sounds it memorized, so then I tried to make it produce sounds closer to ones played by musical instruments.

The sound spirit can produce sounds, but it can’t talk to me. But since it can respond with sound, it became relatively easy to communicate with it.

Spirits of Lisyl’s level would try communicating in ways that I would have an easier time understanding, but the little ones don’t make that much of an effort. Rather, even the thought of doing so probably hasn’t crossed their minds.

And with that, I’m currently having a small concert. Now that I’m actually singing alongside its sounds, this surprisingly sounds like proper music. Come to think of it, people do sometimes clap when they sing. I originally only saw the cajon as a plain wooden box, but thanks to recalling it, I have the sound of wooden percussion now.

Only when I sing do I use languages from my old world. There’s no deep reason for it, but it’s not as if I don’t feel sentimental when singing these songs.

As I was singing, I could tell that someone was approaching.

The presence headed to the kitchen and shuffled things around before heading towards me. A steaming teacup was then placed on the table by our bedside, and the figure stood stock-still.

With her arrival, I stopped singing, and the sound spirit let out a displeased tooting sound. Witnessing this, Lisyl started soothing the spirit, so I’ll leave that issue to her.

「It appears that it’s already over.」

「Would you like to listen?」

「If I may be so indulgent, yes.」

「In that case, we’ll need another cup and a chair.」

「That’s…」

In other words, I’m telling Mia to sit down, but perhaps due to her pride as a servant, she showed disapproval. I believe that everyone should be able to behave as they desire regardless of social status… Well, not really, but that’s a different issue.

「I personally want my audience to be comfortable listening, you know?」

「I understand. And please forgive my thoughtlessness.」

「I don’t really mind.」

While seeing Mia off, springing into motion, I informed the sound spirit that I’ll be singing one more song, and it quickly turned from sulking to playful, approaching me with cheer.

After waiting with the impatiently excited sound spirit, Mia returned. She put down the cup in her hand, carried one of the expensive-looking chairs next to the bed, and gracefully sat down. She looked so majestic despite her maid uniform, likely a result of her good upbringing as a former noble.

With Mia’s preparations finished, I signaled to the sound spirit to play the accompaniment. It’s just the same thing it did earlier, so I don’t really know if accompaniment is the right way to describe it.

It’s evening, so I chose a song associated with the night. Even if my words aren’t understood, I pray that the song’s meaning and mood reach her.

Ever since I started singing, Mia closed her eyes and focused on listening. As the song progressed, her body gently swayed to the rhythm of the song.

I generally sing similar songs to Ciel as a lullaby, and she would quickly fall asleep, so having someone listen like this makes me feel a bit happy.

As the song finished and the accompaniment stopped, Mia, who seemed fully immersed in the song, gave an applause.

「Splendid, Lady Ainsel. Whenever I hear your singing, I can’t help but question why I’ve barely heard songs until now.」

「So it’s also the same in your case, Mia?」

「Unfortunately so… The songs that praise the beauty of nature and extol and give thanks to the gods are considered differently, but I was raised educated that songs for amusement are uncouth.」

「Is it only for singing? Were dancing, drawing, and playing music allowed?」

「Those are considered acceptable hobbies. However, if that’s all you do, people will eventually start to look at you coldly. As long as they remain hobbies, though, such activities are sometimes even welcomed. It shows that you have the leeway to indulge.」

So they’re fine as hobbies, but singing, even when treated the same way, clearly wasn’t. Setting singing aside, I feel like someone should be able to make great success through these ‘hobbies’ eventually, but perhaps that’s actually difficult with the strong influence of religion.

Still, there do appear to be religious factions that are against the discrimination of all Jobs—except for the Song Princess—but there are also those that support it, and the common knowledge seems to be that the church is harsh against Misfortunate Jobs.

Well, certain hobbies being considered good or bad isn’t particularly unique to this world; perhaps humans just have a primal urge to put everything in ranks and hierarchies.

「Mia, did you do any of those as a hobby?」

「Researching sorcery is just so enjoyable, so…」

Ignoring how Mia obviously averted her gaze, I decided that it’s about time to get to the main topic.

「Incidentally, Mia, there is something I’ve been wanting to ask…」

「What might it be?」

From how she answered without appearing particularly surprised, it seems like she expected me to ask a question. In that case, it should be fine to be frank about it.

「You know that we will eventually stop aging, correct?」

「Yes. Before leaving for Ausente, Mistress Fiiyanamia briefed us three personal attendants about it.」

Meaning Mohsa and Luna are also in the know. Maybe Mother Fii thought that it would be better to inform them that we’ll stop aging rather than for them to discover it over the course of time. Since the servants of the manor already serve Mother, I don’t think it’ll be that hard for them to accept, so the explanation probably went smoothly.

And while I don’t know how much they were told, I’d feel bad if I happened to ask a question that’s difficult for her to answer, so I’ll refrain from probing further.

Since I know that Mother Fii was the information source, it’s not really a problem, and even if Mia had figured it out on her own, the most I’d do is hush her. As long as her attitude towards us doesn’t change, it’s not an issue. As long as Ciel doesn’t get distressed, all is well.

Now that I think about it, I feel like I’ve been the one that has caused most distress for Ciel… Let’s forget about that for now.

「That’s good to hear. Still, it’s not as if I don’t want Ciel to grow into adulthood, you see.」

「Is it something you can choose?」

「I don’t know how much you were told, but we can choose to some extent. However, no matter how we stall, her growth will stop when she’s just about to fully mature.

Ciel wants to stop aging as soon as possible as well, and it isn’t like I can’t understand her sentiment.」

「But at the same time, you also wish to see Lady Cielmer as an adult, yes?」

「Naturally. After all, whether she reaches adulthood or even well into old age, I’m sure that she’ll be beautiful still.」

I have confidence that even if Ciel grows old, my feelings for her won’t change. Though Mia responded with a troubled, 「I see.」

「I would love to witness Lady Cielmer’s growth as well. I’m certain she’d mature beautifully. And while she is short now, she may even have a growth spurt in the future.」

「That’s a fair point. After all, Ciel’s small size might primarily be the result of being malnourished in childhood.」

Hearing my nonchalant tone, Mia’s expression grew stern. I can even feel something similar to murderous intent emanate from her.

「Well, anger can’t take the past back, so why don’t we just rest for the night? I won’t be sleeping, but I want Ciel’s body to have a good rest.」

「Understood. May you have a good night.」

「Yes, may you have a good night as well.」

After seeing Mia off, I lay down and relinquished control.

+++

# **190: Sulking, Puppet, and Munyechka’s Past**

「_Umm_… Ailneige, is there something wrong?」

「Not at all.」

Palra sheepishly asked the sulking Ciel. I’m really sorry; I’m the one who caused Ciel’s bad mood. Long story short, my exclusive performance for Mia yesterday was apparently unacceptable. Certainly, I haven’t sung in front of Ciel with the spirit’s accompaniment yet, so I’m completely at fault here.

And so, Ciel has been in a bad mood since we entered the class homeroom. Recalling that I borrowed her body yesterday, she asked me what I did last night, and I honestly answered, resulting in her displeased 『It’s unfair, unfair, so unfair!』 in a voice only I can hear.

『Next time, I’ll sing it without anyone else.』

『I don’t want the same song, alright?』

『Of course.』

『It’s a promise, okay? Swear?』

『I swear. However, please give me some time to prepare.』

『Yes, yes! Of course! I’ll wait no matter how long.』

And so I managed to better Ciel’s mood, but now I feel like her expectations were raised really high.

It’s probably just going to rise higher and higher the longer I make her wait, so it’ll be best to fulfill my promise early on.

「If there’s something on your mind, I’m all ears, you know?…」

Contrasting Palra’s modest tone, Ciel was suddenly chipper―relative to how she usually acts as Ailneige―and answered, 「I’ve just resolved it; it’s fine now.」

The difference in Ailneige’s expression should not be easily noticeable, but Palra appears to have recognized it, as she responded, 「Then I’m glad to hear that,」 with a smile.

「So you’re not going to ask what happened?」

「Can I ask about it?」

「For now, I don’t plan on answering.」

Despite Ciel’s curt response, Palra didn’t show any sign of displeasure. On the other hand, Ciel has opened up to Palra enough to specify that she doesn’t intend to answer _for now_. In that case, perhaps we should try to speak in a more amicable tone.

『Ciel, can we have a moment?』

『Sure, of course.』

『If only you’re alright with it, could you try showing appreciation when people do something for you?』

『That’s what Ain does every now and then, right? I don’t really mind, but is it for everyone?』

『That’s fine too, but it’s also fine if you only do it with people you don’t think badly of.』

『I’ll think about it.』

From the tone of Ciel’s voice, she seems to be positive about the idea. Well, she’s generally receptive to most of my suggestions, though. Honestly, I feel like she tries to fulfill them whenever possible. That’s not really a good thing, but considering that this shows her trust in me, I can’t help but feel happy. It’s really complicated.

After that, Ciel continued listening to Palra until homeroom started. The topic of Belltina didn’t come up at all.

---

「Come to think of it, what category of sorcery is Puppet Sorcery considered to be?」

「Ainsel asking me sorcery questions—now that’s rare.」

「I’m just personally curious about it.」

It’s Puppet Sorcery period. We’re the only student attending, and the lecturer, Munyechka, knows much about us already, so we can actually relax and act natural.

Princess Leshimiiya doesn’t know of me, so this is the only place other than our dorm room where I can spend time as Ainsel and change into my colors.

I’m used to disguising myself, so it’s not particularly uncomfortable, but for some reason, having black hair feels a lot more relaxing.

Perhaps I’ve started thinking that this is the natural state of Ainsel.

「Puppet sorcery’s category, was it?」

「Is it combat sorcery, supportive sorcery, or something else? Is what I mean. Which one is it?」

「If I had to choose, probably combat-use sorcery. After all, it’s said that Puppet sorcery was originally devised to kill people.」

「Is that so?」

I personally thought that it was supportive. Babysitting and childcare are supportive acts, after all, and I’m able to perform this sorcery.

But that’s right, it’s not that I can’t use combat sorcery, it’s that I can’t use magic power to attack. It’s not that Puppet sorcery is an exception; I can still use all kinds of sorcery. I can manifest the spells. But they simply don’t have any destructive power. In that case…

I borrowed a practice doll and operated it. Moving the doll isn’t hard by itself, but making it move like a person is difficult. It’s different from my own body―which I’m not sure still exists.
