When operating a doll, Ciel has greater proficiency than I do. While I’m better at manipulating magic power, Ciel has a better understanding of how the human body moves.

Putting that aside, I tried making the doll hit the desk. I made it punch as hard as possible, but the empty desk that even a baby could probably move didn’t budge at all.

Seeing this, Munyechka examined the doll with great interest before slowly turning her gaze to me.

「It doesn’t seem like you meant to stop the attack from connecting.」

「Yes. My intention was to hit with all my strength.」

「I see, I see… So this is Ainsel’s sacrifice for magic, I suppose?」

「That it is.」

Since I promised before, telling her my sacrifice for magic isn’t an issue. As long as I keep my side of the promise, Munyechka should keep hers as well.

「To be more precise, I cannot cause any damage even when using combat sorcery. I can invoke combat spells, but they vanish into thin air on contact.」

Saying so, I promptly made a knuckle-sized fireball and slowly moved it towards Munyechka. She curiously examined it before grasping the flame. The fireball then disappeared as if devoured by her hand.

「That does appear to be the case. I can feel the flame’s warmth, but it didn’t burn me at all. Well, it’s not like this body would burn, but the point stands.」

「Even a scorching wind’s heat is adjusted to be incapable of damaging a strand of hair.」

「And you have no clue why it’s like that, right?」

「The sacrifice itself is probably in the realm of magic.」

「True. Even I have no idea why I can still exist like this, after all.」

It’s called magic exactly because it’s beyond human understanding. So while I do at least understand the mechanics, I have no idea about things like, for example, where the kinetic energy from the doll’s attack dissipated to.

Maybe it’s better to accept that not knowing how magic works is the norm. In the first place, even sorcery was unknown back in my old world.

「Still, was it really alright to tell me about your sacrifice?」

「It’s fine; as long as you keep your side of the promise. Besides, just because I can’t use attack sorcery, that doesn’t mean that we don’t have any means of attack.」

「Your magic is wholly dependent on Cielmer’s existence, isn’t it?」

「It was born from me thinking only of protecting Ciel. Back then, combat sorcery didn’t really seem to be helpful for the situation, you see.」

The good old days of the Rispelgia mansion. Looking back on it is enough to make my blood boil, so I’d rather not remember, but since it was also where I met Ciel, I can’t forget about it either.

It must be so liberating to get over it like Ciel did, but unfortunately for me, I’m too mature to be capable of that. Now it’s an awkward question if I’m actually being mature about it, but I’m certainly not young enough to easily forget.

「Let’s not touch on your past, then. It doesn’t sound like a pleasant time.」

「Our past is simply a slightly unique misfortune among all misfortunes of this world, but it may still be better not to hear it. After all, last time I tried sharing, I was refused.」

When I was about to share how we got covered in spiders, Shusii backed down on the spider silk idea.

I wonder how she’s doing these days. And when will we ever get the opportunity to wear the dress Lisyl made?

Among the dresses made for us, only Ciel’s party dress has been worn so far, but maybe that’s just how it is.

At this rate, we might as well wear it when active as Ainsel, but the mask and that dress don’t really match well, so that’s a nope.

That get-up would make us look like a noble that just left a masquerade party.

「Now then, you’re concerned about how the doll will turn out, are you?」

「Yes. Even if it ends up being the same quality as your other dolls, how will it be on my end?」

「Honestly, there’s no telling until we try. You and I are different, so I’m not even sure if it will succeed.」

「Just to confirm, do you have all five senses?」

「It might be duller compared to a real human body, but it’s there. Including this body, I create my dolls to be as human as possible. It moves through muscle-like internals and has blood-like fluid flowing through it.」

It’s awfully curious how she emphasizes the “-like” part, but it certainly sounds like it mimics the human body very well.

Still, while she does love dolls, she doesn’t necessarily seem to love humans, and I feel like the charm of dolls should be their difference from actual humans.

「Munyechka, you said before that you love dolls, so I’m surprised that you went to great lengths to make them look so human.」

「I was troubled by that same dilemma in the past. A doll is an imitation of the human form. If so, shouldn’t the goal be to make them look as human as possible? However, can dolls that can’t be distinguished from humans really be considered true dolls?」

Munyechka started speaking with a nostalgic tone, so I listened to her while giving adequate responses.

「I was traveling the world while searching for an answer when I first met Fiiya.」

「Really!?」

Hearing a name I didn’t expect, I was taken by surprise.

Her having met Mother Fii isn’t particularly a surprise at this point, but I just didn’t expect her to bring it up now, so I couldn’t even prepare myself. I still have much to work on, I guess. Seeing my reaction, Munyechka showed a meaningful smile as she continued speaking.

「When I was able to get on speaking terms with Fiiya, I mustered the courage and asked her, as she seemed so detached from the world, about my plight. And her answer was, “If it was made to be a doll, then it is a doll.”

Her response figuratively melted my worries away. Whether one is made to look more like a human or not, it doesn’t change the fact that it is a doll.」

And from then on, she apparently felt indebted to Mother and started associating with her more.

It was quite interesting to hear of Mother’s history on such an unexpected occasion.

+++

# **191: Sparring and Palra’s Feelings ※POV Shift**

「Ei!」

With a lethargic yell, Palra thrust her dulled knife forward. In response, Ciel turned her body a half-step back and nimbly smacked down Palra’s knife.

「Hii!?」 Palra shrieked out of surprise.

It was Combat Training time; since Palra is now permitted to participate in sparring, she is currently challenging Ciel. Grimid was unable to give the teacher a satisfactory answer, so now he’s not allowed to fight Ciel until he gains proper understanding.

Since he brilliantly concluded that he lost because Ailneige was a coward unwilling to tank his final strike, he probably won’t be fighting Ciel for a while.

While he might have wished for a fair and square knightly spar, what Ciel did probably wouldn’t be criticized even in an actual knightly duel.

In the first place, forcing Ciel, someone who’s absolutely weak in raw power, into a battle of pure strength is far from being fair and square.

Nonetheless, Grimid will go on to continue improving from here on, so Ailneige may not be able to win by the time they face each other again. If that happens, Grimid’s attitude might not get properly corrected, but the teachers will surely work to amend that. At the very least, it’s not our problem to resolve.

To begin with, it’s not good to exclusively spar with the same opponent, which is why today it’s Ciel and Palra fighting. The teacher also mentioned that it’s convenient since we’re part of the same party, though.

「First of all, are you taking this seriously?」

「I am! I am, but…」

Ciel grilled Palra for dropping her knife, and she averted her gaze, tongue-tied.

Even I could vaguely tell that Palra was holding back, so it must have been extremely obvious for Ciel. Usually when she’s asking, she’d have a tone of pure curiosity, as if she just wants her questions answered, but today, Ciel’s voice had an uncharacteristic hint of irritation.

Seeing Ciel’s reaction, I nodded to myself contemplatively like an unrelated observer and awaited Palra’s response.

「As I thought, I really can’t attack Ailneige.」

「It’s part of our class, you know?」

「I know, but still…」

「I’m not as slow to be hit by your attacks right now.」

「_Ugk_… That might be true, but…」

『I’m troubled, I’m so troubled, Ain.』

『Why so?』

『I have no idea why Palra is reacting this way.』

As Palra fell silent, Ciel spoke to me with an extremely troubled tone.

I really want to give her a definitive answer, but the most I can do is guess Palra’s thoughts.

『I think it’s because she doesn’t want to injure… or even just hurt you, Ciel.』

『But it’s unavoidable when fighting, you know? Besides, this wouldn’t be enough to injure me. Right?』

『There’s something I’m a bit curious of; please ask Palra if she can do it with other people.』

『? Understood.』

Can she just not fight against Ailneige, or does she not want to fight people at all? There’s even a slim possibility that she also finds it difficult to harm monsters.

It’s best to make it clear first.

「Can you fight if it’s with other people?」

「Y-yeah. I’ve sparred with the teacher before, and I was fine with others too.」

『But she can’t with Ailneige?』

『That seems to be so. In that case, why not show her that she can’t injure you at all? I believe your barrier should be enough for that.』

『Are you sure?』

『It’s not a barrier for protection, after all.』

Protecting us is my role. However, this time, the barrier’s purpose is to make Palra fight, so it’s fine for Ciel to use one. It’s just like my rationale for fighting before.

Perhaps convinced by my reasoning, Ciel chanted a barrier spell. How do I say this? It’s been forever since I last heard that chant. I can cast it chantless, after all, and other people generally use magic circles to cast it.

「I’m using barrier sorcery. Please attack this barrier with all your might. You can do it if you aim where I’m sure to not get hit, right?」

「Yeah.」

Nodding in affirmation, Palra took a few deep breaths and attacked Ciel’s barrier wall. Palra’s strike is still quite light, and Ciel’s barrier is adjusted to easily endure an attack of E-rank force.

It was still difficult for Palra to break through, and her attack was easily deflected. Experiencing Ciel’s barrier firsthand, Palra was astonished, her eyes jumping between her practice knife and Ciel’s barrier.

『Can I leave the next one to you, Ain? I can’t manipulate it as freely as Ain, after all.』

『Understood. I’ll shrink the range of the barrier, then.』

After making an exact copy of Ciel’s barrier underneath the existing one, Ciel’s barrier disappeared. I then slowly transformed the remaining barrier to envelop Ciel’s body. It was now an ellipse spaced around 30 cm away from the body. This is something that even Ciel is capable of doing, but it’s difficult for her to maintain it subconsciously. After all, it’s my fault that she hasn’t improved in barrier sorcery.

「With this, there shouldn’t be any need to worry about me getting hurt, right?」

「Y-yeah. Thank you, Ailneige.」

「Now then, let’s continue, and this time, please fight properly.」

Saying so, Ciel readied her rapier. Palra was stanced with her knife as well.

Since this is a spar, the lower-ranked Palra gets the first move. Otherwise, it’ll end up being a one-sided battle, defeating the whole purpose of sparring.

Now, the knife, as a weapon, is far from the most practical against monsters.

Having a short blade forces the user to draw close to the monster, and that already makes it a difficult fit for Palra. However, if we consider her Job, it’s more adequate than having her use a sword or spear, and most importantly, Palra’s main weapon is the bow, so the knife is more of a self-defense weapon in her case.

Besides, as long as she gets into her ideal range, it’s not impossible for her to overwhelm the enemy. In interpersonal combat, getting extremely close to the enemy can limit the utility of lengthy weapons.

However, against monsters, who have sharp claws as weapons and hides too thick for a knife to fatally pierce, it’s not much of an advantage.

With our spar restarted, Palra took a deep breath before rushing in as ideally prescribed. She was faster than expected, much faster than Ailneige’s hypothetical maximum movement speed. But since she’s moving in a straight line, Ciel should be able to handle her easily even with our restrictions.

After waiting for Palra to reach her ideal range, Ciel avoids Palra’s knife thrust at the final moment. Palra was taken by surprise, but she remained close to Ciel and continued attacking.

Perhaps growing impatient after Ciel avoided everything, she hastily tried attacking from an awkward stance and was countered by Ciel.

It’s more of a mentorship than a spar, but this was our plan to begin with. Ciel—even when fighting as Ailneige—tends to use tricky movements even when fighting fairly. It’s not a problem when the sparring partner already has some fighting experience, but when sparring with someone who just started out, they might develop weird habits.

Anyway, I want Palra to have a proper foundation first, and Ciel adjusted in turn. It’ll serve as good training for Ciel as well, and this coaching period shouldn’t last too long, so it’ll be a good experience.

She’ll probably overtake Ailneige soon, since we can’t just easily make Ailneige go beyond E-rank in terms of mastery.

From my observation, Ciel’s sword skill without my support should be around upper D-rank. She should be much stronger than the recently promoted D-rank boy that we battled a long time ago. However, it won’t reach C-rank.

For swordsmanship, Ciel hasn’t made much effort in learning things outside of the basics, and she isn’t as powerful as she is with sorcery. Honestly, compared to when we were training sorcery with our lives on the line at Rispelgia’s, we haven’t grown as much.

「I’m not particularly well-versed with knives, but I think it’s generally important to build a solid foundation.」

「R-right. Gotcha. Thanks.」

While Ciel’s breathing had only quickened slightly, Palra was breathing with her whole body and looked like she might collapse from even a light push.

She had a composed look up until the end of the spar, but it’s probably to keep her exhaustion from showing.

「Why don’t we take a break for the time being?」

「That sounds good. Ailneige, you can go ahead without me.」

Since the class period has finished, the students are gradually leaving. After a short contemplation, Ciel said, 「Well then,」 and left the area.

---

「Hah— It’s so frustrating—」

As Ailneige left, I attempted to sit down, but unable to support my body, I lay down on my back.

I know this will get my hair covered in sand, and my roommate Tietta will scold me for it. But still, I wanted to fight until I couldn’t move.

At first, I held back, not wanting to hurt Ailneige, but just as she said, there was absolutely no need to worry; she showed me the undeniable gap in our abilities.

Even if I make the excuse that I’m just more skilled with the bow, Ailneige’s specialty isn’t the sword either; it’s sorcery.

Besides, I was matching her in terms of speed. And yet, my attacks couldn’t even graze her.

It’s like I was just hit with the reality of what an actual hunter is capable of.

I’m not frustrated because I felt envious of Ailneige’s power compared to mine.

With my current capability, I’m far from standing equal to her. That’s what frustrates me.

「She’s so far away—」

She’s just so far. Ailneige is apparently just an E-rank hunter. In that case, how much further away are A-rank hunters?

In the first place, can someone like me even become a hunter?

My thoughts were starting to spiral into negativity, so I shook my head and stood up.

At the very least, I kept up with her speed. That’s why… I’m sure that I’ll be able to match her someday. Ailneige has had a variety of experiences as a hunter, while I’ve only been assisting my father up until now.

There’s no way catching up would be easy.

That’s why, during my stay in the academy, I want to at least gain something that will let me stand next to Ailneige without feeling shame.

For that reason, I need to return to the classroom and chat with Ailneige as I always do.

+++

# **192: Magic Cores, Stampede, and S-Rank**

Roughly 2 months have passed since the academy classes began. It’s been getting hotter as summer is steadily approaching, but it doesn’t seem to be as hot as summer in my old world. While I can measure the atmospheric temperature, I can only make vague estimations based on the season, my bodily sensations, and my past experiences. The old world had Fahrenheit and Celsius, and my estimations are probably closer to the former.

And so, while the temperature itself isn’t as high, it doesn’t make much of a difference. Hot still feels hot. I just might not be used to it, though. Still, there are sorceric tools that keep the temperature down in this world, so it doesn’t get uncomfortable indoors.

The said sorceric tool is by no means cheap, so the common household can’t afford it, but each classroom in the academy has one, while the dorm also has at least two installed per floor. Apparently, even just having one in the hallway can cool the rooms down considerably.

Meanwhile on our floor, each room has one installed. Considering how much we paid, it’s not particularly surprising. It does require magic cores to maintain, but each room is provided a supply. It’s roughly worth around 10 hours of use, which I guess is long enough to stay comfortable from after class until the next morning.

In our case, we could probably substitute it with a barrier, but as we know the purpose of magic cores, we make use of it as much as possible. Honestly, we generally have it turned on the whole day.

Mia spends most of the day in our room, after all, and we have an excess of magic cores in stock. Frankly, a single S-rank magic core could probably last us the whole summer and some.

We’re hoarding because we’d rather not be seen with these, but is there any way for us to dispose of magic cores? Even if we were to dispose of them through the Hunter Guild as Cielmer or Ainsel, we’re still limited to up until A-rank cores, and it’s hard to find use for S-rank cores.

「Incidentally, there seems to be a magic core deficiency this year.」

「Is that so?」

「Indeed. I heard that there are fewer magic cores gathered compared to last year, which is quite troubling.」

「I wonder why.」

Wouldn’t a magic core deficiency be a major problem for this country? With sorceric tools being so commonplace, there should be a high demand, and it’s likely that they also rely on sorceric tools to survive through summer and winter.

While the summer heat isn’t particularly bad, what about winter? Still, the nobles probably have enough stock to last at least one winter.

「Apparently, small-scale stampedes periodically happen near the royal capital of Ausente. While one just broke out recently, it seems to be smaller than usual.」

「I see.」

Ciel responded with indifference, but a certain incident suddenly popped into my mind. And looking at Mia’s expression, she seems to be thinking the same.

「Still, I haven’t heard any news about a stampede.」

「The public was likely not openly informed. There seems to be an effort to keep it secret from the students as well.」

「There must’ve been a troublemaker before, right?」

「Yes. Though the said troublemaker simply overestimated their abilities and died.」

Plausible story. For this year, the thunder sorcerer Alcrei or the hero Juerd might just stick their necks into something like that. Mr. Hero would probably survive one way or another, though.

While their reasons may be different, like testing their own mettle or helping people in need, I can easily imagine them diving headfirst into a stampede.

「To begin with, the nation is able to quietly quell the stampedes without the aid of students. They simply don’t occur on a large scale here, you could say.」

「Well, small-scale ones are manageable. After all, Ain and I could handle one.」

「Only you two can treat it that lightly, I believe.」

If you ever hope to resolve a stampede alone, the first problem is not your own strength but how to get the whole monster swarm to focus solely on you. Being capable of large-scale attacks so they can’t run past you might be enough, though.

Either way, only a small few are capable of either.

Even if it’s only a stampede of F-rank monsters, it’s still normally impossible for a single person to handle. In our case, we might have a difficult time if there are monsters that can’t hear leading the pack. I have no idea how the Song Princess interacts with deaf targets, so I probably need to get more familiar with my Job’s abilities.

I’m sure that the Song Princess at the chapel has greater Job mastery than I do.

Since only Ciel can hear me, all I think about is how many positive effects I can provide to Ciel, so I’m honestly not very skilled outside of those.

First of all, the chapel Song Princess appears to have a different audible range than I do. So perhaps Song Princesses can expand or narrow down the audible range of their voices.

Finally, if they can become capable of making only the people they choose hear their songs, then Song Princesses could be crowned as the most powerful Job ever. Well, it’s probably impossible, though. Whether you judge it by its abilities or its reputation. Unless the discrimination stops, no matter how much power the Song Princess Job may have, it will probably continue being called a Misfortunate Job.

「With that said—」

While I don’t see where we’re going from here, Mia moved the conversation forward.

「This would be the perfect situation to expend magic cores, wouldn’t it?」

「That’s true, but why ask?」

「You do have an acquaintance who you could entrust to covertly utilize magic cores, yes?」

「Right, you’re absolutely right!」

Ciel raised her voice in realization. Now then, will this action serve to give relief to that certain acquaintance, or will it only ail her with stress? It will undoubtedly be of great help, so let’s just meet up for now.

---

「So, what do you wish to discuss about?」

On the floor above our own, we arrive before Princess Leshimiiya after sending a letter in advance. While she likely won’t get mad even if we come without prior warning, the princess will still be troubled if we don’t.

Considering the topic of discussion, only Princess Leshimiiya and Fithuille are allowed to hear it. She probably needs to make preparations regarding that, but if not today, then we could just ask her for a more convenient date.

Still, it seems the princess puts great importance in her conversations with Ailneige, as she replied that we can come any time.

And so, after having a short idle chat, the time for serious discussion came; only Ciel, the princess, and our upperclassman (on the inside) remained in the room.

「I hear that magic cores are in low supply; is that true?」

「That’s… that is correct.」

「The stampede this year was apparently small, was it?」

「That’s what I heard. I was only told about the periodic stampedes recently, however…」

So it was also hidden from the princess? Perhaps there simply was no need to tell her until now. The princess doesn’t seem to be one to resolve stampedes, and she probably isn’t in any position to command.

Besides, even hearing about the monster stampede might be stressful for the young Princess Leshimiiya. And with it happening periodically, at worst, she might not be able to feel at peace living in the capital.

In short, just because she’s the princess doesn’t mean that she knows everything.

She surely doesn’t tell us everything she knows either, and it’s not like we want to know everything. Nonetheless, I told Ciel to ask a leading question just for good measure.

「That they are being triggered on purpose, you mean?」

「… T-That’s…」

Shaken, Princess Leshimiiya turned her eyes towards Fithuille. Perhaps she’s thinking that it would be bad for Fithuille to learn this.

She immediately concealed her panic, but when the princess couldn’t find her next words, Fithuille spoke in a curt tone.

「Thuille already knows, so no need to worry, princess.」

「I… I see. I understand.」

Somehow forming a response, the princess then took a silent but deep breath before showing a look of understanding. I’m sure she has complicated feelings about Fithuille knowing this when she was not informed until recently, so it’s impressive that she could quickly compose herself.

Fithuille being a bodyguard directly assigned by the king and an individual capable of seeing through Ailneige’s abilities might have a part in it, though.

「That’s right. Officially, Ausente triggers stampedes to periodically cull monsters and minimize the potential damage if a naturally occurring stampede ever breaks out.

However, the truth is that it is done in order to keep up with the enormous magic core demand.」

Stampedes certainly do occur periodically if left unattended, but it takes years of neglect. So it’s certainly strange that this occurs practically every year.

It was why I suspected this to be the case in the first place, and it seems like my hunch was correct.

「And because of the stampede that ambushed you, there are fewer monsters this time.」

「That’s likely the case…」

The one to benefit most from this issue is probably the Elbert family that Princess Leshimiiya previously warned us about. We don’t plan on getting involved with the politics of things, so I won’t ask for confirmation.

Carelessly touch on politics, and the next thing we know, there’s already war on the horizon.

Even our smallest requests can be practically taken as an order. So there will probably be people asserting that a foreign ruler’s daughter is intervening in their politics.

「For the main topic, would you, as a representative of Ausente, like to purchase magic cores?」

「Purchase magic cores? But―」

Princess Leshimiiya was about to say something, but her words were cut off. Normally, an individual offering to sell magic cores would not be able to withstand the demand of a whole country. That’s probably what she was about to comment on, but because we were the one making the offer, she held her words.

「This is the magic core I hope to sell.」

Saying so, Ciel put a towel on the table, on which she then carefully placed a large magic core on top of. Because the core might roll off otherwise. Seeing this, the princess’ eyes were wide with shock, and she was at a loss for words.

Fithuille’s eyes shimmered for a moment, but she quickly returned to her usual expression.

Monsters of every shape and size possess a magic core, and you can roughly identify their rank by the size of the core.

The sizes can range from small ones, which can fit on your palm, to big ones like these that need to be carried with both hands. However, the most important thing is actually the magic power contained within, as there are small magic cores that hold a lot of magic power.

When utilizing it for a sorceric tool, you can use it as it is, or, if it’s too large, you can process it to shrink in size while still retaining the same amount of magic power.

After all, small cores that can hold a lot of magic power exist, so this is basically creating that artificially. As for the details of the actual process, I have no idea.

「Is this… an A-rank monster’s magic core?」

Finally returning to reality, the princess inquired with a hushed tone.

「Likely an S-rank monster’s magic core. The monster was beyond A-rank in strength, but classification gets fuzzy above A-rank.」

S-rank monsters are creatures of the same level as true dragons and, excluding the den, do not appear anywhere near human habitation. Even in the den, the strata they start appearing in are physically far from human habitation.

The S-rank monsters on the surface are not creatures that just any mortal can defeat, and defeating them would make you something beyond normal mortals. S-rank monsters are just those kinds of creatures. And since they can use magic, they’re generally doing things beyond mortal comprehension by default.

Anyway, the gap between A-rank and S-rank monsters is a large valley that includes this as one factor, and the magic core Princess Leshimiiya is seeing right now is from a monster generally considered to be just between A and S-rank in strength.

It honestly could be around S-rank, but since I don’t actually know, it’s just a hypothetical for now.

「This monster, where did you…?」

「There are many in the lower strata of the den.」

「But the monsters appearing in the den should be only A-rank at most…」

Princess Leshimiiya sounded as if she couldn’t process the reality in front of her. Is it really shocking that this is from an S-rank monster?

No, I suppose it should be. After all, in terms of pure strength, an S-rank monster is much more devastating than a sizable monster stampede. An army that can quell a stampede could be annihilated by a single S-rank monster.

+++

# **193: Magic Cores, Wholesale Delegation, and Royal Discussion ※POV Shift**

「A-rank monsters are the limit to what can be found in the lowest strata regular hunters can reach. After all, there appear to be no S-ranks challenging the den.」

The official report is that the other hunters have only progressed through half of the den’s area. Still, there might have been hunters that traversed beyond the 50th strata without reporting it, so who knows if this is reliable. Come to think of it, if people were to actually reach the deepest strata―Tur’s area―what would happen? They’d fight Tur… and probably lose. And will they die there, or will they be returned to the surface?

It’ll likely take centuries for mankind to actually reach Tur’s area, so we can just ask before then.

「Then is it different for you, Miss Ailneige?」

「I’m E-rank, you know?」

「Oh, right, that certainly is. My apologies.」

「The information you desire should be identifiable with your resources, is it not?」

Cielmer’s actual hunter rank; it should be easy to know with a quick inquiry. We don’t really hide how we’re A-rank. But we do hide the fact that we’ve defeated S-rank monsters.

「I understand. Now, about the magic core, if this is true, then I cannot make the final judgment on my own. It doesn’t appear to be within my financial means to begin with…」

How much money does the princess have access to? While royalty, she is low in the succession line; however, her standing should be relatively important still.

Additionally, I have no idea how much an S-rank monster’s magic core is priced. I could use the price of an A-rank core as a reference, and since we’re the ones selling, we can probably inflate the price a fair bit, and they’d still buy.

However, we’re not particularly doing this for profit, so we don’t plan on selling it at an expensive price. Still, we don’t plan on giving it for free either. We could just give it to the princess and count it as a debt of gratitude. However, there are conditions I want to set with the princess.

Since it might be better to discuss those in advance, I instructed Ciel to do so.

「Allow me to present the conditions for this transaction in advance.」

「Is it to keep the fact that this was purchased from you a secret?」

「That’s also included, but please only utilize the magic core for sorceric tools that are not exposed to anyone’s eyes.」

「Understood. It will be difficult to keep it completely away from the public eye, but we will make sure to utilize it in places only a limited few are allowed to witness.」

「I shall trust your words.」

In the end, if they use it at places accessible to more people, there’s a chance that it might get stolen, so I’m glad that she accepted.

As royalty, there should be one or two hidden contraptions they can use it for, and honestly, they can probably replace the palace’s existing energy sources with these magic cores instead.

「Now then, since you may need a sample to make an appropriate decision, I will hand one magic core over in advance. You do have a magic pouch on hand, right?」

「…! I do, but… you have multiples of that magic core?」

Princess Leshimiiya asked with a tone of bewilderment. She should understand that the fact that we possess multiple S-rank magic cores means that we are powerful enough to procure them. Well, there wasn’t any specific mention of us defeating monsters alone, so she might believe that we gathered them with multiple people. Either way, the fact that we’re at least a member of a party that can subjugate multiple S-rank monsters should hint that we’re quite capable.

I’m sure she hasn’t really doubted the power of Ailneige—of Fiiyanamia’s daughter—but it should feel more tangible with physical evidence like this.

Humans are creatures that can still get surprised even by things they should already know as information.

「I won’t divulge the exact number, but I certainly do. As such, I don’t mind if you wish to purchase as many as I have in stock.」

『What should we do about the price?』

『It might be best to have them decide the price. We don’t really know how to assess the value, and even if they end up under-pricing, it won’t be particularly painful for us.』

『Fair point.』

With a nation as the buyer, even if they under-price, they probably won’t haggle it down that badly. But now that I think about it, we should probably make things clear just in case—we’d rather avoid making this a transaction between the kingdom and Central.

We don’t want them to think that they are indebted to Central or that they are doing Central a favor.

「I’ll leave the pricing to your end. However, please remember that this must remain a private transaction with me. It will become a complicated matter if Central gets involved.」

「Understood. I’ll make sure to relay the offer exactly as you have said.」

Anyway, we’ve achieved our goal for the day, so Ciel was about to leave when the princess halted her.

「Thank you very much for your consideration.」

「It was simply a good opportunity on my part, so please don’t mind.」

_It seems like the magic core issue has been a really big problem for them_. With that thought in mind, we left the princess’ room.

---

The magic core Miss Ailneige has shown me—one larger than any I’ve seen in my life—was left sitting on the table.

I hurriedly stored it in my magic pouch as Miss Ailneige exited the room, but this familiar magic pouch I’ve always used now feels like a priceless article that must not be touched lightly.

The truth of the matter is, it’s not as if we are immediately at risk of running out of magic cores due to the unusual stampede this time. We have reserves stored in the palace, and the establishments handling magic cores should have a fair number of stock remaining. This issue is only a problem for the royal capital area, so while it takes time to gather enough magic cores, we do have the option of purchasing from nobles with their own fiefdom.

Even so, Miss Ailneige’s offer is greatly appreciated.

That’s because, regardless of how we resolve it, it will be difficult to maintain the current living standards of the populace without great burden in our current situation.

There are even rumors of nobles using the magic core situation to steer the public sentiment against the royal palace.

To avoid that, there has even been discussion of turning off several sorceric tools used in the palace’s operation to at least mitigate the decrease of the magic cores being circulated in the market.

It would lower the palace’s defense, but we have judged that it’s more dangerous to allow the rumored noble to gain the influence of the public opinion.

There is a possibility of it being a trap, but for the royal family, that noble―the anti-Central Elbert family―cannot be permitted to gain more power.

If it truly is a trap, then there’s a fair chance that I will be targeted, but that won’t be different whether they gain power or not. In that case, the best option for the pro-Central royal family is to prevent the Elbert family from rising in power.

However, there is now a way for us to prevent Elbert’s rise and circulate more magic cores in the market without undermining the palace’s defenses. That’s only if my kingly father accepts this offer, however.

The servants waiting outside were quick to return to the room, so I immediately arranged to request a clandestine discussion with Father.

---

It’s the first holiday since I sent the letter, and now I finally have the opportunity to discuss it with Father. As it is a sensitive topic, I could only give limited detail, but perhaps the lack of detail might have hinted at the gravity of the topic.

As for why this day was chosen, perhaps it’s out of consideration for me.

「Now, Leshimiiya. I’ve been told that you wanted to discuss the magic core supply issue… However, there is no need for you to feel responsible for this matter to begin with, you know?」

「While the responsibility may not be mine to uphold, I am still a Royal; I hope to help in what little ways I can.」

Certainly, this magic core shortage may not be my responsibility, but since I was indirectly involved with it, I want to help in some way. After all, had it not been for my presence, this would not have been a problem to begin with.

That’s why I had been thinking of how I could possibly help, but―

「Besides, I haven’t made any particular move this time. I simply received an offer.」

「An offer, you say… You haven’t gotten yourself into anything dangerous, have you?」

「I have not actively done anything to put myself in danger.」

If I were honestly asked if what I’m doing is dangerous or not, I’d say it’s dangerous. After all, I am chatting with someone in an enclosed room with only one bodyguard instead of the many I usually have.

Moreover, the said bodyguard even admitted that she cannot win against Miss Ailneige. If I had to describe the danger level if things ever go south, standing right in front of an A-rank monster would probably be less dangerous.

However, ignoring her―ignoring Miss Ailneige―is much more dangerous, and there’s no assurance that she will not harm Ausente.

Incurring her wrath and getting into an openly antagonistic position with Central is much more terrifying. And so to explain all of this, I decided to immediately inform Father about the matter at hand.

「The said offer was raised by that personage. She wishes to sell us magic cores in her possession.」

「That personage―The Princess of Central, is it? In that case, it shouldn’t be a bad offer. We will be incurring a debt to Central, but a good price should be able to offset to an extent.

However, it’s hard to say if a few magic cores will be enough for our dilemma…」

「A few conditions were raised during our discussion, but it would be best to see it with your own eyes first. This is the magic core that she has in stock.」

From my magic pouch, I took out a large magic core the size of an armful. Seeing this, Father displayed a rare expression of shock, but he quickly returned to his usual look.

「This is…」

「I’ve been told that it may be an S-rank monster’s magic core. If we are to purchase, the source must be kept―」

As I was about to share Miss Ailneige’s conditions, there was a knock on the door. That sound made my heart shrivel, but then the voice saying, 「Dear Father, I’ve heard that Mii has returned,」 immediately after gave me instant relief.

Not knowing how to handle this, I turned to Father for answers and saw him looking at me with the same concern, so I said, 「I leave the decision to you.」

Hearing that, Father answered 「Enter,」 to the person behind the door with a short but clear voice.

The one who entered shortly after was Ausente’s crown prince, my dear eldest brother, First Prince Arclain.

Being more mature, Brother Arc was lean yet already as tall as Father. He is awfully affectionate of me, but when it comes to his royal duties, he is capable of making difficult decisions.

「It’s been so long, Mii. I’m glad to see you doing well.」

「I’m glad to see you doing well, too, dear brother Arc.」

After a short exchange with Father, Brother greeted me with a smile. And then, upon noticing the object on the table, he had a serious expression.

「I was hoping to have a pleasant chat with Mii, but it seems like now is not the best time.」

「Indeed, which is why I permitted your entry here.」

「It sounds like anyone else would not have been allowed. Is that an A-rank monster’s magic core? It looks considerably bigger than what I can recall.」

My dear brother tilts his head in contemplation, but he probably has an idea of the magic core’s true identity. Hearing Father say, 「S-rank,」 he reacted with a light sigh.

「That on its own should give great progress on our magic core issue, but… where did such a monster come from? It should be hard to miss the news of an S-rank monster’s appearance.」

I see, so that’s how Brother Arc assumed this was procured. In fact, I also had a similar question in mind when I first saw it. If such a monster has appeared nearby, then it must be subjugated no matter the cost.

Besides that, the Hero’s appearance also came to mind. I thought, perhaps, the monster that is to ruin Ausente or its heralding omen may have finally appeared.

But reality had stranger things in store.

While Brother was a bit anxious, Father spoke out.

+++

# **193.5: ※Leshimiiya POV**

「Regarding that, Leshimiiya shall explain in detail.」

「Certainly. First of all, please keep even the very existence of this magic core a secret.」

「Right, understood.」

After Brother nodded to my preliminary caution, I continued speaking.

「As for the origin of this magic core, it apparently comes from the den in Central. I was told that this was procured from the monsters appearing at the strata further beyond those that are currently identified.」

「An S-rank from the den… How authentic is this information?」

「I believe it to be almost certain. For better or for worse, news of an S-rank monster appearing near human habitation would spread quickly, so if that isn’t the case, the den would indeed be the most reasonable source.」

「I see.」

Brother deeply nodded, not with the expression of a family member, but as that of the crown prince.

There indeed are other possible sources, but Miss Ailneige has yet to be absent from the academy ever since. In that case, the only time she has to defeat a nearby S-rank monster is during the end of the week.

She would need to secretly find unreported S-rank monsters and fight and defeat them without anyone noticing during the holidays. Achieving all of that within the span of two consecutive days would surely be difficult even for an S-rank hunter.

As such, her having defeated monsters in the den as she said is the more realistic prospect. Moreover, craftiness of that sort is not her strong suit.

「This by itself would greatly help with our magic core shortage, but surely this wasn’t given to you for free, was it now?」

「Yes. This was merely lent to me since the other party thought it would be better to have a sample.」

「… Mii, who provided this sample?」

Hearing Brother’s inquiry, I turned to Father for confirmation, and he nodded in response. I already suspected it when Brother was given permission to enter, but it appears that Father intends to entrust the decision-making to an extent.

With Brother Arc being the next in line, this certainly is a rare and valuable experience for him. In that case, I couldn’t help but think this matter should have gone to Brother to begin with.

Still, considering Miss Ailneige’s personality, she is unlikely to go out of her way to propose this offer to the palace, so had she not come to me, this offer likely wouldn’t have reached us to begin with; it can’t be helped.

「The other party is the one called the Princess of Central: Lady Cielmer.」

「Why is such a major player here in Aus―… I see, the academy.」

「Yes. Lady Cielmer enrolled with an alias and stated that she did not want to be known, so only our dear king father and a small few know about her. Brother Arc not being informed was…」

「By Father’s judgment, surely. Still―no, let’s continue with the magic core first.」

Brother seemed to have further inquiries, but he held his tongue and returned to the topic at hand.

「Her conditions are to not divulge the source of the magic cores, to strictly use them where they cannot be seen, and to treat it as a private transaction, not as a transaction with Central. For as long as she has stock remaining, she is willing to sell to us at our asking price.」

「I see. Then, Crown Prince, what do you believe the course of action should be?」

As I thought, Father wishes to have Brother decide. Father will still have the final decision, but he probably wants to witness his choice as the next king.

「Before making judgment, Mii, may I ask a few questions?」

「As long as they are questions I can answer.」

「Why does the Central Princess wish for it to be a private transaction?」

「She exclaimed that it is because making it a transaction between nations would complicate things.」

「From your observation, is there no lie in those words?」

「That’s… yes. She seems to dislike troublesome matters, so I’m certain about it. In particular, she doesn’t show any strong sense of ambition.」

From our interactions, that was the impression I got. Despite having the position of being Central’s Princess, making her no inferior to the kings of other nations, she doesn’t wish to do anything with that status.

However, if need be, I believe that she will not hesitate to wield her authority. She has a mindset similar to that of a commoner, yet not exactly. Now that I think back, she’s such a strange personage.

「_Hmm_… In that case, how about we purchase as much as we can at the market price? It sounds like the Central Princess would not be pleased with attempts to curry favor or otherwise, so making a fair trade may be the safest option.

Even if it ends with us being indebted, it’s still better than having the kingdom in chaos.」

Brother shared with Father the conclusion he reached from the information I shared.

And to his words, Father responded with a satisfied nod.

「In that case, I shall contact a trustworthy appraiser. Leshimiiya, that much should not be an issue, yes?」

「As long as the appraiser keeps silent about the magic core, it should be fine. I was also told that it’s fine if only a chosen few witness the magic cores being used.」

「At worst, we might need to use a contract, but no matter.」

「Now then, please allow me to excuse myself.」

「Of course, you did very well.」

Staying here will only make me a nuisance, so with our discussion over, I decided to leave. While I did not work for this achievement, I was giddy from Father’s praise, and my cheeks curved into a smile the moment I exited the room.

Just as I noticed Brother exiting right after me, he called my name.

「Mii, if you have free time, why don’t we have a short chat?」

「Of course, dear brother.」

It’s been a long time since I’ve had a relaxed chat with the busy Brother Arc, so I gladly obliged. The choice of venue is either my room or Brother’s room, so after some contemplation, I chose his room.

My dear brother’s room had plenty of sorceric tools, which―from his own admission―is because sorceric tools are both a hobby and work for him. _He likely enjoys them more as a hobby, though,_ I thought to myself as I was led to the table by the window side.

「I really love drinking tea while looking out of the window from here.」

「The scenery is quite wonderful.」

While it doesn’t have the whole view of the capital, a large portion can be seen from here, and you can easily imagine how the people are living their lives.

There is also a good view of places I’m familiar with, which almost brings back memories of my experiences there.

For a while, we observed the royal capital, pointing at curiosities here and there and chatting, but as we were finished being served tea, Brother had all of the servants step away.

「Incidentally, how has your academy life been? I’ve never studied at the second academy, so I’m genuinely curious about it. I have heard stories, though.」

「It’s quite enjoyable. Learning alongside many people has been a stimulating experience, and it allows me to objectively assess my capabilities.」

For the lesson contents, there’s only a few I do not know about. I have been given prior education, after all, and I believe that I should have a good understanding of things. Still, learning once again, and from new teachers, was more interesting than I expected.

I’m taught the same topics, but the difference in teaching styles has been very illuminating. The problem is that while there may not be much of a gap in knowledge level, there are still major differences on the technical level.

And while style differences are not an issue, there are situations where there is conflict between old and new information, so the problem is what to do then.

Should I fall back to what I was taught before, or should I instead adopt the new techniques taught here?

「So what do you do when that happens?」

「I discuss it with Runya―the Hausen family’s Rulinia. She has experienced the same kind of education as I have. And―」

I hesitated on whether I could talk about it or not, but since I suspect that this is part of what Brother wants to know about, I mentioned another name.

「I’ve also inquired about Miss Ailneige’s opinions of this. And her thought process is to set her existing knowledge as the foundation, incorporate all that has value in learning about, and simply ignore the rest.」

「How do I say this? She’s an interesting individual.」

「She is, indeed. Miss Ailneige doesn’t appear to put much importance in having high grades, you see.」

When Miss Ailneige is at the academy, she is quiet, doesn’t cause any problems, and normally maintains good grades like any good student. However, due to her appearance and her status as an E-rank hunter, she stands out considerably and is one of the individuals that everyone in the class knows the name of.

However, the way she stands out is different from others―from us, as it’s better to describe us as not merely conspicuous but more as renowned.

「How is her reputation in class?」

「Mostly good, I believe. There are many who are intrigued by Miss Ailneige, but most of them seem to be satisfied simply observing from afar.」

「I see… While it appears to be alright so far, there’s no telling how things will develop if a problem were to occur…」

Brother Arc’s concern is most valid; if Miss Ailneige were to get involved in an issue―if she were to be bullied by a classmate, for example―we can’t simply ignore the risks. It may lead to a deterioration in our relations with Central, and to begin with, if Miss Ailneige were to take any sort of action, the only ones that could possibly stop her in the academy are the rumored near S-rank in power headmistress and the rumored high-ranked hunter in hiding.

Right now, Miss Ailneige is hiding her true identity. If it were known that she is the Princess of Central, there would be no one daring to test her patience―or at least I want to believe it to be the case―but right now, there is a high chance that someone may unwittingly cause her problems.

「Miss Ailneige goes to great lengths to remain incognito, so I believe she shouldn’t act immediately. Concerned about this, I once asked her possible course of action, and she said that she’d give a warning first and only act if all else fails.」

「In that case, we should be fine as long as nothing disastrous happens.」

「That’s right. I’m sure no one would perpetrate such a mess of disastrous proportions… But even if someone does, she stated that she would consider it a personal matter with the perpetrator.」

「So that no matter what happens, the damage will be kept minimum, huh―For now, I’m glad you’ve become friends with the Central Princess.」

Hearing Brother’s words, I was a bit troubled.

As I was contemplating on how to reply, Brother asked, 「Is there something wrong?」

「No, I’m just not really sure if Miss Ailneige and I can be considered friends…」

「She was willing to tell you that she is the princess of Central, wasn’t she?」

「That is true, but rather than telling me because we’re close friends, she mostly did it because it would be less troublesome that way.」

「Ah, I see… She seems to be quite a resilient individual. Mii, what do you personally think of her?」

「Me?」

What do I think of Miss Ailneige―of Lady Cielmer? Thinking back on my exchanges with her, we always had trivial conversations. It’s only a short time before she heads to the roof, but we would talk about how the class was that day or which food in the cafeteria tasted delicious.

While it is partially for formality, I do find chatting with her comfortable since she doesn’t have interest in political prestige.

While there are times like today when she would bring up very stressful matters, they are generally matters that I’m grateful to learn of in advance rather than when they are already a problem, or ones that I do benefit from, so it’s difficult to hate her whimsy.

Most of our classmates are only observing her, but I know that many hope to talk to her. Though the reasons may vary from wishing to learn from her experiences as an active hunter or simply wanting to befriend a lovely girl such as her.

I can’t deny that being someone who has had plenty of chances to speak and learn from her has brought me some sense of superiority. And besides, I feel a small sense of affinity with her.

As I was deep in thought, my brother suddenly muttered an important revelation.

「Perhaps it’s just difficult making friends with someone older, huh.」

「… Dear Brother Arc, what did you just say?」

「Hm? She is a year older than you, isn’t she?」

「Is… that so. I’m surprised you know.」

I nearly fell speechless from the shock, but I somehow managed to respond.

「Lady Cielmer doesn’t hide any of her private information about her hunter activities, you see. After hearing that Central got a princess, I did a quick investigation.」

「I couldn’t really risk carelessly investigating on my end.」

Besides, unlike Brother, I don’t have the connections to investigate Central. Additionally, ever since meeting Miss Ailneige, I purposely avoided gathering relevant information just to be careful.

As Brother was convinced by my answer, I added, 「If possible, I do want to be her friend,」 and nothing more.

+++

# **194: Sorceric Tool Class, Kotatsu, and Napping**

「I’m sure some have already learned this from experiencing failure firsthand, but sorceric tool creation is not simply about drawing neat magic circles. The compatibility of the medium you chose is also an important factor.

For example, should you wish to craft a sorceric lamplight, you will need material to be illuminated; should you wish to create a sorceric waterspout, you will need a part where the water will emerge.」

We’ve already had a lot of activities in the Sorceric Tools Course at this point, yet Mr. Liens started with this. It must be because he wants us to learn what we can from failure. Or perhaps to warn us against neglecting the physical part of the sorceric tools, or to teach us the difficulty of crafting new sorceric tools.

I’m also included in team failure. At first, I thought of making a hair dryer for my project, but since I couldn’t get the drying part working, I had no choice but to give up on it. In the end, I even consulted with Mr. Liens, but he told me that it’s still difficult at this stage.

I still remember what a hair dryer looks like, but I don’t know what material to use for it, and it’s an annoying silhouette to shape.

You can easily create a water-producing sorceric tool by drawing a magic circle on a random plank with the necessary ink, but the water would just flow everywhere nonstop, and it won’t be as strong. This is why both the material and the shape of the medium are important.

You can take an existing, already established sorceric tool’s design and put your spin on it to make your own original, but there seems to be no existing sorceric tool that’s similar to a hair dryer.

To be precise, if there already is, then its design has not been released to the public.

This country apparently has some form of patent system, but there are technologies still kept top secret.

And so, my first sorceric tool attempt ended in failure, and I decided to make a kotatsu instead. There are publicly released designs for heating implements, so I just need to attach it to a table, put a futon on top of it, and then add a countertop as weight; it should be achievable.

I am questioning my choice of making a kotatsu with summer right around the corner, but since I’m only making a small sorceric tool that can sit on my desk, I’ve stopped being choosy.

If I start with a miniature, I can just enlarge it into a proper kotatsu in the future, and with it being smaller, it’s easier to bounce back from failure.

With a large one, just making the table part is challenging enough.

「Depending on your Job, it’s also possible to only create the magic circle and outsource the physical parts of the magic tools to other craftsmen, and the opposite is also true. However, in this class, I will have you go through the entire creation process, so please decide on a feasible project.」

「In that case, using accessories would be difficult, huh…」

Beside me, Tietta muttered to herself. While the plans and designs for creating accessory-type sorceric tools are publicly available, they’re still quite difficult to make. While not as difficult as a magic pouch, what you can make is almost practically dependent on your Job. As far as I know, Tietta should be capable of making those, but just because her Job is compatible doesn’t mean she can craft those immediately.

Also sitting next to me, opposite of Tietta, is Belltina drowsily nodding off. Is she going to be alright?

If not, I can teach her about the lesson content later, though.

「Professor, isn’t there anything we can do with the magic core’s size?」

「There are techniques that can make large magic cores smaller or change their shape. However, only individuals with crafting Jobs can perform those, and the techniques themselves are quite sophisticated, so it’s not easy to resolve.」

「Then would it be better off to give up on the magic core’s size at this point?」

「No, stores that handle magic cores sell pre-processed cores of different sizes, so you can purchase from there. There are also places where you can order custom sizes, and our class has a supply of standard market-sized magic cores.」

Mr. Liens thoroughly answered the questions a student raised. Then, he lined up magic cores of different sizes on top of the lectern. While they vary in size, they all seem to be E-rank magic cores based on their magic power.

「I originally wanted to have the Job holders try to process magic cores, though…」

「Was there an issue with that?」

「The supplies are currently low, you see, so we don’t have the leeway to use some for practice.」

The students seem to be aware of the supply issue, as many nodded in understanding.

How do I say this; I really have no luck. My Job doesn’t allow me to process magic cores, but I at least wanted to see how it’s done.

Side note: if you want to make an accessory-type sorceric tool, you’ll need the ability to process magic cores. You could just purchase a small magic core, but it’ll be difficult to draw a magic circle on it.

That’s why common practice is to directly draw a magic circle on a magic core and then shrink it down to size.

In other words, they’re generally disposable. Since magic cores disappear after use, some are difficult to use even just as accessories.

As the discussion part ended, the teacher instructed us to start working on our projects.

---

『So, what does this sorceric tool do?』

『It warms you up during the winter season, I suppose.』

As I completed the kotatsu magic circle, Ciel spoke up.

The two beside me are currently struggling with basic magic circles. Yup, about this course, since there are students who don’t have prior knowledge of magic circles, we are given sample designs of basic sorceric tools with guides for drawing magic circles included. Like one for illumination, or for a flask that boils water. Still, for people who have never studied magic circles before, it’s still difficult to draw.

Even students that are attempting to make their own originals are given the choice to just make the sample sorceric tools if they get stuck. At the same time, there have been students who immediately chose to craft one of the basics to satisfy the course requirements as soon as possible.

There is even one student who has already finished his own original sorceric tool. Apparently, he has the Artificer Job.

『How is it used?』

『You install it on a table and drape a comforter over it so the heat can’t escape. Even if this ends up being a success, it probably won’t be that popular.』

『Is that so?』

『This sorceric tool is made to be used without footwear, you see.』

In this world, people wear their footwear indoors, so even if I made a kotatsu, not many would probably utilize it.

I’ve heard that showing feet is considered immodest among aristocrats as well.

I think it’ll be difficult for people to accept something that could result in bumping into another person’s feet when your legs are outstretched.

So why am I making this, then? It’s because it seems easy to do.

『It should be fine to have one for personal use, right?』

『It will probably need a dedicated room for storage, you know?』

『In that case, that won’t be a problem for us. By the way, this is an object from Ain’s old world, right? What’s it called?』

『It’s a kotatsu』

『Kotatsu? Say, can I use it with Ain?』

With her mentioning it, I tried to imagine sitting with Ciel. Not a bad idea; rather, I’d like to do it in the future, and I kind of want to see the bed-loving Ciel not wanting to leave the kotatsu.

As a fellow bed lover, we’d probably end up sleeping next to each other in the kotatsu, though. Other than that, messing around under the table is a common cliché.

Depending on the size, there are cases where only one person can stretch their legs out, and even if it’s large enough to accommodate multiple outstretched legs, it’s still tempting to pull a prank on someone’s outstretched feet. Now I don’t know if I’d have it in me to do that to Ciel, but she’d probably mess with me like it’s nothing. She had previously professed that she enjoys troubling me, after all.

As I told all this to Ciel, she replied, 『I’m really, really looking forward to it!』

Since class is still ongoing, I ended our chat here for now and brought the finished magic circle and the kotatsu design outline to Mr. Liens.

---

「I see. By using a thick blanket, it can provide plenty of warmth with only a small amount of heat, yes?」

「That’s right. Still, since the heat source is only by the feet, it necessitates the removal of one’s footwear, making its practicality is a bit questionable…」

「While it certainly would be difficult to popularize it, the idea itself is not bad. We do have colored lights consisting of a sorceric lamplight enclosed in tinted glass panels, which I think is conceptually similar. If we craft a chest built from effective heat-retaining materials, food transport could――Additionally, if we consider the cost-effectiveness of using low-grade magic cores――」

After showing my work, Mr. Liens entered his own world. The same thing happened with the hair dryer consultation, but whenever he gets excited by something, he apparently has a tendency to ponder to himself.

While that’s a bit of an issue as a teacher, I think it’s a good thing as a craftsman and a researcher. As a fellow researcher who pondered about barrier and detection sorcery―actually just straight-up magic―by my lonesome, I felt a sense of kinship, so I let him talk a bit until he was satisfied.

Still, since it was starting to take a bit too long, 「Mr. Liens,」 I called to him, causing him to snap out of it. He then looked my way and awkwardly scratched his nose.

「My bad, it was such a good idea; I couldn’t help myself.」

「I’m glad it left an impression, but our class time is limited.」

「Oh, yes. With that, you should be able to deliver a work that’ll pass with no issue. You can go ahead with that design.」

「Understood.」

「Incidentally, are you――」

As I was about to return to my seat, Mr. Liens spoke. However, after I turned to him, he said, 「No, never mind,」 while scratching his cheek.

It sounded like it’s something important, but if he doesn’t want to continue, then I won’t poke my head into this one.

After all, he probably has a reason for holding his tongue, so forcing it out would be troublesome.

Returning to my seat, Belltina was napping with her arm as a pillow. At first, I thought that she might just be feigning it to avoid speaking with Tietta, but she seemed to be really deep in sleep.

Tietta is seriously undertaking her work. It’s all nice and peaceful right now, so I decided to continue my mini-kotatsu as well.

---

The class period ended, and the people have started thinning out, so I started jolting the sleeping Belltina’s shoulder.

「Ye-Yesh!」

She appears to be surprised about being woken up, as her voice was a bit hysteric. This attracted the eyes of the remaining people around. Noticing this, Belltina turned bright red and curled into a ball.

Still, their gazes only stayed for an instant, so no need to worry much about it. Honestly, though, I can understand her feeling.

「The class period has ended.」

「R-right! Thanksh for waking me uap!」

「It’s not a big deal, but are you alright?」

「Ah, umm. Bell is alright, yes.」

True, she does look alright, probably since she was just asleep, but still――After some deliberation, I decided to convey my sentiment.

「If you need an ear, I’ll at least hear you out.」

「Thanks… But I really am alright.」

Belltina replied with a slightly troubled smile. Considering how Palra asked us about sorcery some time ago, I’m really doubtful about her ‘alright,’ but I decided to step back for now.

「Understood. In that case, shall we have lunch then?」

Saying so, I started walking、 and Belltina toddled behind me. No, considering how we’re actually smaller in size, I’m probably the one toddling, to be honest.

+++

# **195: The Capital’s Magic Cores, the Princess, and the Promise**

If I was asked which place I feel the most familiar with in the academy, I’d have to say that, outside of our room, it would be Princess Leshimiiya’s room.

We come here regularly, after all, and while I don’t know how she truly feels, the princess always gives a warm welcome, so we never feel like we’re overstaying our welcome. Palra aside, we’ve probably spoken with the princess more often than we have with Belltina.

And since she knows about Cielmer, we’ve also talked about pretty personal stuff with her. For my sensibilities, I feel like I can comfortably consider her a friend at this point.

How do I describe it? We’re close at school, but we don’t really hang out after classes or on the weekends. She’s that kind of classmate, I feel.

And in the most familiar room of Princess Leshimiiya, after being welcomed as always, the servants were made to leave, and we―Ciel, who’s in control, and Princess Leshimiiya―started talking.

「In short, the supplies are now alright?」

「Yes, all thanks to you, Miss Ailneige.」

「It’s a fair trade, so there’s no need to act that way.」

「But―Alright, then I shall oblige.」

Regarding our trade of S-rank magic cores with Princess Leshimiiya, they ended up purchasing 10 cores. It turned into quite a lot of money―I don’t know if it’s the market price, though―but as expected of a great nation’s royalty, they were able to pay with no problem.

It was a price that we could afford if we needed to, but it would definitely burn a hole through our wallet. All I can say is that, once again, we’ll never have any issues with money.

The only times we had to be concerned about money were when we started out and before that, though.

In regard to the public impact, I have heard voices of relief about magic cores starting to circulate in the market once again. Many people probably still need to be more economical compared to last year, but now it won’t be an extreme burden. With this, the problem is now much more manageable.

「By the way, what will the purchased magic cores be used for?」

While Ciel has gotten used to Ailneige’s speech pattern, whenever she’s straightforward like this, I can’t help but go, _‘Yup, that’s Ciel.’_

While I’d probably end up being straightforward eventually, I usually dance around the topic for some time first. Still, I don’t intend to say that a certain way of interacting with people is better than the other, so I just kept to myself and watched over their exchange.

The question could be taken as an inquiry about state secrets, but the princess will surely tell us if she can’t answer it, and Ciel isn’t really the type to get upset from not getting answers.

「We’re using it to replace the magic cores powering the palace. I can’t go into the details, but while each of the palace’s important sorceric tools are normally powered by their own magic cores, they can all be sustained by a single, highly powerful one instead.

Only certain individuals are authorized to replace the magic cores used by the palace’s infrastructure, so no one should find the change unusual. They are also bound by contracts that forbid disclosing any information related to the royal family’s sorceric equipment, so there’s no risk of information leaking from them either.」

『It’s like the palace is one big sorceric tool, isn’t it?』

『Now that you mentioned it, you’re right. Still, that probably makes it more convenient to live in.』

『It must have been a challenge to build, though.』

Just how complicated must the palace’s magic circle be? Still, designing a house that uses a single core to start a fire, illuminate a room, heat a bath, and maintain a comfortable room temperature should be possible even for me.

The magic cores used day-in-day-out would need to be from high-ranking monsters, though.

「Also, the magic power within the purchased magic cores is being transferred into lower-ranking cores, which are then circulated in the capital.」

「You can transfer the magic power from a magic core?」

「I heard that it’s only possible to transfer from a higher-ranked magic core to lower-ranked ones, and that the resulting transfer also decreases the total magic power available, but apparently people with certain Jobs can perform this.」

Where does the decreased magic power go? Since it isn’t considered a taboo, then it probably hasn’t vanished or returned to being miasma, though.

Thinking about it normally, maybe it’s treated the same as expended magic power? In that case, wouldn’t it be efficient for this world to just transfer magic power around to expend it? Though I do think that it might be a bit overkill. Still, if need be, to resolve an urgent world-ending threat, then I’ll gladly give all our magic cores away.

In our course of work as a hunter, I only thought of magic cores as a little more than glorified exchange coupons, but there is a surprising amount of use for them. That drug that drives magic power berserk should also be made of it, so I guess I’m just not paying attention.

「Taking the opportunity, I also investigated the flow of magic cores within the capital, and it appears that magic cores of undisclosed origin are being brought into the second academy.」

「Is it really alright to tell me this?」

This should be a national problem or something at that level. At the very least, I don’t think this is a topic to bring up to outsiders like us.

Besides―

『Bringing this up, I wonder what she wants us to do about it?』

『I don’t think we can do anything about it, but what do you think, Ain?』

『I agree with you about that.』

It doesn’t sound like the princess spoke about the mysterious flow of magic cores to have us investigate it. If that was the case, then I’ll have no choice but to lower my opinion of her.

If she wanted us to do something for her, she should just tell us what to do and how we’ll be compensated; no need to be so roundabout. In the first place, this isn’t something to entrust an outsider to handle.

「Honestly, I really shouldn’t share this matter, but since the Elbert family appears to have involvement, I decided to inform you about it.」

「Thank you very much.」

With the anti-Central faction involved, I now understand her wanting to inform us. After all, it’ll be too late if we only learn this after something already happened.

If we’re not expected to do anything in exchange for this information, then I’m honestly grateful for it. As I was pondering, the princess then started to say, 「By the way…」 in a somewhat awkward tone.

「Miss Ailneige, are you older than me?」

「That’s right… Is there any issue with that?」

「No.. I mean…」

While Princess Leshimiiya sheepishly scanned Ciel up and down, Ciel tilted her head in confusion.

『What’s going on?』

『Setting aside where she learned of our age, she must be wondering why we’re so short.』

『Are we really that short?』

『We are the shortest in our class, so yes, we are relatively short. Still, there’s nothing we can do about it.』

We were malnourished, after all. It seems like 3 years’ time is not enough to compensate for 10 years of deficiency. We’ll probably continue being smaller than our peers in the future, but we are experiencing proper growth.

I’ve repeatedly mentioned wanting Ciel to grow to adulthood, but I suspect she’s probably going to stop aging around high school age―as early as 15 years old.

「You just seemed so adorable, I thought.」

It was a painful excuse, but I wonder what her _‘adorable’_ truly meant here.

Even ignoring her small stature, Ciel’s appearance is objectively―I’m not sure if I can confidently assert this, but still―adorable. However, I believe she should look more beautiful than cute, but am I wrong?

「So I am adorable even from your eyes?」

I’m not the one to say this after pondering adorableness, but I’m surprised that Ciel reacted to this topic.

While it may sound like sarcasm from how she spoke, Ciel doesn’t have that in mind at all, and the princess is also quite the pretty girl herself.

「Of course, it’s acknowledged as a fact within our class, and you do have things I feel envious of. Your smooth skin, for example…」

「Yes, yes! Great effort has been done to maintain this complexion, you know?」

Ciel said boastfully, probably because I was being praised. Lately―or rather since we started living at Mother Fii’s manor―we have been using actual expensive skin care, but my barrier is the main protector of Ciel’s skin against all external factors.

That’s why, despite the recent change, she has the tendency to associate praises to her skin as praises to my barrier.

Now then, either because Princess Leshimiiya is a familiar acquaintance by now or due to her excitement, Ciel smiled―something she rarely does in public.

Witnessing this, Princess Leshimiiya’s pupils slightly dilated in surprise, and she whispered, 「You truly are so charming.」 Then, with resolve filling her eyes, stared at Ciel.

「Um, if it would be alright with you, how would you fancy going downtown with me on our next break?」

『Seems like we’ve been invited to a date.』

『So this is the ‘date’ thing, huh.』

After hearing that unexpected invitation said with such a serious expression, I couldn’t help but mutter to myself, which Ciel overheard.

Now, it would be nice to have time to contemplate, but since it won’t be good to make the princess wait in silence, I had Ciel say, 「The next break… please give me a moment,」 for now. Then, I had her take out an appropriately sized notebook, so it looks like she is checking her journal. Does this world even have a journal-taking culture?

To begin with, it would be unthinkable for any regular noble to mull over a princess’ personal invitation, but since the princess knows the truth of Cielmer, it should be alright.

While Ciel pretends to check her schedule, we start discussing.

『For now, it’s probably less a date and more of an outing.』

『Is that so? But why the sudden invitation?』

『Hmmー… Perhaps she simply wants to become closer to us, but there might be something more to it.』

It’s completely possible that she just wants to be friends, but there’s also a chance that isn’t the case. However, personally, I don’t feel it’s necessary for us to keep a high alert for ulterior motives. Whether she purely wants to be friends or only hopes to gain a connection with Central, it’s not a problem; if she has a malicious intent, then at worst we can literally stomp it down.

『What should I do?』

『I’ll leave the decision to you. However, if you aren’t particularly against the idea, I think you should try it at least once.』

And besides, if you keep doubting someone’s intentions, you’re unlikely to ever make friends, so I vote for going on the outing.

After mulling for a moment, Ciel seemingly found her answer.

「I wouldn’t mind, but can I bring someone else with me?」

「Of course. Even I can’t truly go by myself, after all.」

Meaning she needs bodyguards. She actually is a princess, so it’s only natural. If she brings another friend… That would be troubling. The people Ciel is almost willing to open her heart to in the academy are only Munyechka, Palra, Belltina, and Princess Leshimiiya. If someone else comes, then at worst, Ciel might avoid talking altogether.

_If our relationship with the princess fails to deepen, then that’s fine, too,_ I thought, but that would defeat the purpose of going to the academy to begin with, so I’ll keep it to myself.

After all, I do find the idea of quietly living in the forest with Ciel nice, too.

「I’ll relay the exact meeting time through later correspondence, but let’s meet before lunch in our next break.」

「Understood.」

And so the outing plan was settled, but now I just realized that there was no mention of our itinerary.

Well, we don’t really know much about Ausente, so I suppose we can leave it to Princess Leshimiiya. She invited us, after all, so she should at least have some places in mind, right?

Thinking about it this way, maybe I really was just overthinking the date thing.

---

『Come to think of it, who are you planning to bring along?』

As we returned to our room, I asked Ciel. I was wondering if she plans to bring Palra or Belltina along, but they’re unlikely to come willingly. And even if they do, they probably won’t be able to say a peep.

I recall Palra having talked with the princess before, but I’m not even sure if Belltina has had a conversation with her.

「It’s Mia. Having Mia along would be reassuring, after all.」

『I see.』

She knows how nobles interact, after all, and being an attendant, it won’t be unnatural to bring you along.

「Lady Cielmer, did you call for me?」

Having no context about the conversation, Mia asked in confusion.

「On our next break, we’ll be going on an outing with Princess Leshimiiya, and I want you to come along.」

「Affirmative. Do you know where we will be going?」

「No. Princess Leshimiiya is probably going to plan the whole thing.」

「Understood. I’ll make sure to be fully prepared by then.」

「Thank you, I’ll be depending on you.」

Hearing Ciel’s words, Mia was surprised for a moment before composing herself and firmly answering, 「Please leave it to me.」

+++

# **196: Clothes, Rendezvous, and Nicknames**

And so it was our next break, the appointed day of our outing with Princess Leshimiiya. After our meeting, we had some back and forth with Mia to iron out the details, with the general agreement being to meet in front of the academy gate and then leave the rest to the princess.
