The princess wanted to come pick us up at first, but, as expected, having a nation’s princess do that wouldn’t be a good look.

While the princess doesn’t find it an issue since she knows that we’re Central’s princess-ish figure, only a small few should know that information.

Based on how she always makes her servants leave, the attendants and bodyguards she has at the academy, at the very least, likely aren’t in the know.

If it looks like we’re calling her to get us, the number of people who don’t think well of us will increase. And there should be a good number of them already.

On the other hand, the princess apparently finds it unacceptable for us to go and pick them up as well.

Because of that, we decided to rendezvous. Personally, it feels very student-ish of them. Still, meeting in front of the school gateーagainーfeels really date-like.

Ciel’s outfit is the image of an incognito disguise. A pea-green one-piece like those usually worn by commoner girls, but with excessive ornaments. It’s adorned with frills, ribbons, and gems, made to suit Ciel wellーand I do think it looks cuteーbut it really makes you question the status of the one wearing it.

A commoner wouldn’t wear something this over-the-top. Children from prominent merchant families or fairly wealthy commoners would choose one with a more elaborate base design, and nobles wouldn’t wear this to begin with.

It’s as if the outfit is screaming _“I’m a noble in disguise.”_

There’s actually some logic behind it: if you wear the exact same clothes commoners wear, then people might start an altercation without knowing you’re an aristocrat. While it might not be intentional, that can possibly escalate into real trouble.

That’s why nobles wear such extravagant clothes, ostensibly displaying their status; so that the people keep their distance. And since our intention this time isn’t to completely blend in with the people but to enjoy commoner pleasantries as nobles, this was the end result.

While there are also people who’d target disguised nobles instead, there’s no need to hold back against them, making the bodyguard’s work easier.

「And that’s the last of it.」

「Really? Thank you.」

All preparations were entrusted to Mia, and now she just announced the completion of her task with satisfaction. Mia will be carrying our luggage, so Ciel will only be carrying one magic pouch, the one that only we can use due to my tampering.

It has money inside, but Mia will be paying in most cases. We’ve already handed her money for that purpose, so it should be alright.

The remainder becomes Mia’s pocket money. Mia is our employee, after all, so we pay her wages. In that case, I guess it’s more bonus than pocket money?

「Mia, are you fine going like that?」

「I’ll change into something more appropriate. It won’t take too much time, so no need to worry. Please excuse me for a moment.」

Seeing Mia off to change, Ciel sat on a chair.

「Come to think of it, isn’t it rare for us to wear a hat like this?」

Saying so, Ciel caressed the hat on her head.

It’s like a short-brimmed sun hat, tawny in color and woven from plant fibers. We usually wear a hood, so a hat certainly is unusual.

『It looks great on you.』

「Is that so?」

『Anything looks good when you wear it.』

「Is that meant to be a praise?」

『Ahー, uhhh…』

Depending on the interpretation, it can sound like I’m saying that what Ciel wears doesn’t matter to me, which can then be taken as me not caring about whatever she’s wearing.

That’s what got me choked for words, but I quickly responded, 『It’s a praise.』 Ciel chuckled in response, so I’m sure she understands my intent, I think.

「I think you also look great in anything, Ain.」

『Really? My eyes and hair are black though.』

「You say that, but my hair is white. If I wear a white one piece dress, I’ll be white all over.」

『A completely white Ciel is cute, in my opinion. And your blue eyes would accent it greatly.』

「A completely black Ain is sure to be adorable.」

『I’d probably seem gloomy.』

「You think so?」

Ciel tilts her head, but unlike her bright colors, dark clothes combined with my already black hair would only make me exude a gloomy aura. My eye color can’t accent it like Ciel’s eyes can either.

『Well, in conclusion, there are clothes that would suit us better than others.』

「Let’s leave it at that for now.」

Since it was turning into an unproductive discussion, I forcefully ended the topic, and Ciel teasingly giggled in response. Yep, I’m glad I ended it early.

As this happened, Mia had returned. Her outfit looks easier to move in than the average feminine garb. It’s casual wear but looks quite snappy. She’s wearing pants, so she gives off the impression of an occupational fighter.

Skirts are the standard ladies’ bottoms in this world, after all.

That reminds me, even female hunters were mandated to wear skirts in the past, weren’t they? I’m not sure if it was only an Estoque custom or continent wide one, though.

On that note, we also wear skirts a lot. We’re generally fine with wearing whatever, and I’m doing my best so that the skirt stays down even with extreme movements. These days, I can even create a field of darkness within our skirt if I want to.

「Sorry for the wait.」

「So you’re going with that attire?」

「I do also play the role of bodyguard, after all.」

Mia doesn’t sound convinced of her own words, probably because she’s generally the one being protected. While this may sound insulting, she should serve the role of a scarecrow well, and that’s something to be proud of.

Having an adult along will lead to less trouble than if it’s only us children, and if trouble that we can’t handle ever occurs, that’s already an existential threat for the Royal Capital Ausente.

For example, disasters at the level of an impending meteorite collision or the arrival of a Tur-level threat.

That reminds me, Princess Leshimiiya did previously talk about the kingdom’s prophecy of destruction: that since one with the Hero Job appeared, a powerful monster might attack the kingdom or something.

If the threat is at the level that the current Juerd can handle, then there’s no need to worry about it.

「Now then, it should be about time for us to leave.」

「Yes, I’ll be depending on you.」

Cheering up, Mia extends her hand to escort Ciel, which she naturally takes.

As we left the room and gradually approached the gates, Princess Leshimiiya was already there, silently waiting. Munyechka’s Fithuille and two others seemed to be observing the surroundings nearby. Likely her bodyguards.

Princess Leshimiiya was staring at empty space, seemingly lost in thought, until one of the bodyguards whispered to her ear, which resulted in her jerking her shoulders and looking our way.

She then modestly, but delightedly, waved us hello.

While finding it quite unusual for the princess to show this much emotion, we arrived before the gate.

「We’ve kept you waiting.」

「No worries, I just arrived a moment ago myself.」

Starting with such a date-like exchange, the two exchanged proper greetings.

I know it’s a date cliche, but is this also a common interaction in this world? Well, to be honest, I don’t even know if the “Did you wait long?” “I just came,” back and forth actually happens for real in my previous world.

With their greetings done, I informed Ciel of something I want to ask the princess before we get started.

『Please confirm if there should be 5 in total.』

『Understood.』

「First, there’s something I want to ask.」

「What is it?」

「Are there 5 in total?」

「Um…」

It appears that Princess Leshimiiya didn’t understand my intention at first, as she displayed confusion. The princess’ group consists of 4 people, and there are 2 (3) in our group; it doesn’t exactly add up to 5 people.

And that is because what we mentioned is the number of people watching us in hiding.[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-121464) After a moment, she seemed realize this, as she answered, 「That’s right.」

In other words, if someone else outside of these 5 starts following us, we can apprehend them.

I’m not capable of wide-range detection scan sorcery―magic―like Mother Fii, so I can only sense those that approach near. As for the people outside my range, let’s trust that the 5 hidden protectors do their best. It’s their duty anyway.

「Can I leave today’s plans to you?」

「Of course. After all, I believe you’re not very well-acquainted with Ausente, Miss Ailneige.」

「Are you well-acquainted, then, Princess Leshimiiya?」

「I occasionally come for inspections, so I’m relatively well-informed.」

I had the impression that the princess isn’t allowed to leave the palace much, but it seems like I was wrong. Though she called them _inspections_, the princess is 12 years old, so it’s probably more like observational studies to show her how the common people live while she’s still at a young age.

Now it’s difficult for me to judge if it’s for better or worse, but as a commoner myself, I’d prefer if the people above knew about the average lifestyle.

So if any policy changes are made, they should at least have some consideration for common folk, and they might give reparations for necessary decisions that place great burden on the populace. There are probably kings that still turn tyrant despite knowing, though.

While I rejoiced at the fact that I wasn’t born a noble, Princess Leshimiiya shyly, but resolutely, turned her gaze our way.

「Um, Miss Ailneige!」

「? What is it?」

Perhaps nervous, she spoke in a higher tone, causing Ciel to tilt her head. As I thought, today’s Princess Leshimiiya is acting somewhat out of character. Well, her inviting Ciel for an outing was already out of character for her.

With the gap from her usual, collected demeanor, she’s honestly very cute. While incomparable to begin with, she’s probably only second to Ciel in cuteness right now.

「Um… It would be problematic to be called by my real name, so let’s use a different―…would it be alright if we called each other by nicknames?」

『What do you think?』

『If you’re not against it, then it should be fine. Even with nicknames, it’s Ailneige’s nickname in the end.』

『Well, that’s true.』

「Understood. In that case, please call me Ail.」

We did make this alias so we would have less hesitation about letting people call us by nicknames, so it’s fine to follow through. However, even if it’s a false nickname, it still feels complicated to have more people addressing Ciel by nickname.

Still, I don’t have a negative opinion of Princess Leshimiiya either, so it was honestly a matter of time that this happened. We’ve put the princess through a lot of stress, after all.

In contrast to my conflicted feelings, Princess Leshimiiya showed a reassured and joyous expression. Despite knowing that Ailniege is only an alias, it seems like she’s still happy about this. That’s so pure.

「Thank you very much, Miss Ail. In that case, could you call me Miiya?」

「No.」

Ciel’s immediate answer caused Princess Leshimiiya to have a shocked expression. It seems like the princess is taking a break from being royalty today. Also, the bodyguards have scary glares. Doesn’t bother Ciel and me, though.

「―May I ask why?」

「That nickname is too close to Fii’s.」

I have no idea what the princess thought of it, but she looked mortified. For some reason, the nickname being similar to Mother Fii’s name probably doesn’t sit right with Ciel.

It’s not just nicknames; people having similar names happens a lot. In fact, in my previous world, there were times when I’d have three classmates with the same surnames or given names.

But in Ciel’s mind, having similar names is a very unusual thing, making her uncomfortable about it. Especially since Mother Fii is one of the few people Ciel can fully open up to.

This is all conjecture on my part, though, and judging from Princess Leshimiiya’s reaction, she must be having some weird misunderstanding. So in the meantime, I decided to lend her a hand.

『How about Princess Leshy―no, Miss Leshy?』

『That’s much better.』

「For that reason, will it be alright to call you by Leshy?」

「O-of course! By all means, please call me Leshy!」

「Well then, I’ll be depending on your guidance, Miss Leshy.」

With her face blooming with cheer, Princess Leshimiiya―Miss Leshy puffed her chest and proclaimed, 「Leave it to me.」

+++

# **197: Boutique, Black, and Test Fitting**

Guided by Miss Leshy, we headed to the capital’s town center. Unlike the streets hunters regularly pass through, the streets here are vibrant and sanitary.

There’s still some pedestrian traffic, but not enough to feel cramped and congested. It doesn’t have the liveliness of the market area, but it’s by no means dead silent.

The stone pavings draw organized patterns, and the people walking wear good-quality fabrics and seem to be enjoying themselves. We occasionally pass by benches, with some occupied by people taking a break, so the atmosphere here isn’t bad at all. It’s probably an area where the more affluent people gather.

Miss Leshy confidently led the way but stopped right before a certain establishment. On closer inspection, it appears to be a boutique. 「Miss Ail, over here.」 Urging Ciel, she entered the store ahead of us.

Ciel soon followed after, and inside was a spacious interior with rows of various clothing.

There were shop assistants present, but they only gave their greetings without approaching us. Is it just shop policy, or were they instructed to behave unobstructively beforehand?

Either way, as long as they keep their distance, it’s fine by me.

『I know that girls love clothing, but still…』

『Oh? But isn’t Ain a girl now, too? The Creator God said so, after all, since Ain is a Song Princess.』

『Well, that’s true, and I do have more interest in it now than in my previous life.』

I frequently think about what would look cute on Ciel. And while it’s embarrassing to see myself dressed up in front of a mirror, I don’t really hate it. I look similar to Ciel, so I want to look pretty, too.

『However, what I meant to say is that both we and Princess Leshy should have a near excessive amount of clothes, and most of them tend to be custom-made.』

『Hmm, that is a fair point.』

While having a suggestive smile, Ciel answered with a contemplative tone before then speaking to Miss Leshy.

「Miss Leshy, do you frequent shops of these sorts?」

「I almost never get to go inside one. Whenever we need clothing, we simply call a tailor to the pala―no, our home. Those clothes don’t necessarily suit my liking either. While my preferences are considered, the overall design is already settled in most cases. That’s why… it’s actually a small dream of mine to―」

She hung her head in embarrassment. Come to think of it, being a princess probably doesn’t give her much freedom in fashion as well. Perhaps the most she could do is pick out what fits her preferences the most from a prescribed assortment of royal garbs. While a selfish princess might demand for beautiful dresses of her liking, I don’t find Miss Leshy to be the demanding type.

For that reason, it must be a dream of hers to freely pick clothes for herself, regardless of them being pre-made goods.

While pondering over the princess’ peculiar predicament, as though to gloss over her embarrassment, Miss Leshy then asked, 「How about you, Miss Ail?」

「It varies. There are times when I buy pre-made garb, times when I go to a boutique to have something designed, and times when we call a tailor to the manor.」

「That―sounds quite enjoyable.」

「Yes, it is.」

The part that Ciel enjoys is brainstorming the design of my clothes with everyone in the manor, isn’t it? Or thinking about what kind of clothes would pair well with mine. While we have a princess-like position in Central, it’s completely different from Miss Leshy’s situation.

Though perhaps that is part of why Princess Leshy wanted to meet Ailneige halfway.

「Miss Ail, what colors do you like?」

「Black and whatever complements it.」

「Umm, would it be alright if I picked an attire for you?」

「I don’t really mind, but…」

「Then let’s get to it!」

While Ciel couldn’t seem to understand her sentiment, Miss Leshy excitedly went deeper into the store. Ciel saw her off, and Mia could only watch with a troubled smile.

『I wonder what happened.』

『She probably wants to have fun picking clothes for you. You like picking out clothes for me, so you should understand how she feels, right?』

『Is that so? But I enjoy it because it’s with Ain, you know?』

『I enjoy choosing clothes for you as well, and I believe the servants of the manor feel the same way. We picked out clothes for you in hopes that you’d be happy.』

I’m happy enough seeing Ciel wear my choice of clothes. And while it’s just a hunch, as long as they aren’t absurd-looking, Ciel would probably be happy just knowing that I picked them.

I have absolutely no intention of making Ciel wear anything bizarre.

Also, while I fully expected this, Ciel doesn’t plan on returning the favor and choosing clothes for Miss Leshy. But that’s fine for now. It just means that Ciel doesn’t find it worth doing.

Still, since we’re already here, let’s take a look at the shop offerings.

Boutiques that sell pre-made clothing are actually quite few. I assume it’s because not many can prepare enough equipment for a full-on production line.

There might be sorceric tools specialized in goods production, but if it’s for something large-scale, it would probably end up being expensive, and the magic core upkeep is going to be proportionally as costly. In general, shops will only have handmade stuff displayed as samples. That was how it was at Shusii’s place, too.

As for what they’re selling here, with the current season, many of them are summer-oriented outfits. Actually, it’s mostly summer dresses. The other choices are also all skirts; no pants for sale.

This is probably the norm for boutiques aimed at the average female customer. The only other boutique I can think of is Shusii’s store, but their shop is aimed at hunters, so the atmosphere is pretty different.

The general prices don’t seem to be that different, though.

Anyway, this establishment mainly sells summer dresses and outerwear to pair with them, like cardigans or jackets. Though as expected, there aren’t any coats. No cloaks or capes either.

It crossed my mind when people passed by us, but there was barely anyone who wore only a summer dress. It seems like their culture is to hide as much skin as possible.

Wearing at least a three-quarter sleeve and hiding up until the elbow is common practice for the upper class. You generally don’t expose your legs.

Miniskirts and sleeveless shirts are no good either. Though among commoners, there are people who wear short sleeves.

And so, Miss Leshy is currently looking at the black summer dresses with an extremely serious expression. She doesn’t need to be that serious―but that’d be difficult for her personality, I suppose. She probably wants Ciel to be happy with her choice, though she doesn’t know that picking anything black would already put Ciel in high spirits.

Also, her eyes frequently wander towards the lighter-colored dresses. She must think that those colors would suit Ciel more. I completely get her.

『Wouldn’t this look great on Ain?』

『I think you’d look better in it.』

『Then how about this one?』

『That one’s still preferable.』

Before I noticed it, Ciel had started choosing clothes for me to wear. It seems like Ciel is in the mood to make me wear adorable and frilly clothes today. While I’m not very enthusiastic about wearing those sorts of girly clothes at this age, I personally think they’d suit Ciel.

Watching Ciel mull over the clothes she just picked, Mia―who knows about me―silently watched over us with a knowing smile.

---

「How about this?」

Miss Leshy nervously handed over a choice of clothes. Accepting it, Ciel then inquired, 「Can I try it on?」 which reached a shop assistant through a game of telephone, and the assistant’s approval was relayed in a similar manner.

I’m not really sure if this establishment actually allows test fitting, but since we were given permission, then it should be fine.

We’re probably being given the VIP treatment. If that’s actually the case, then we’ll gladly oblige.

「Mia, can you assist me?」

「Understood. Shall I set your hair differently as well?」

「That… Let’s see. I’ll leave it to you. Miss Leshy, allow me a short moment.」

「Of course, take your time.」

Being seen off by the somewhat restless Miss Leshy, we were led to a different room. Once we were left alone with Mia, I enveloped us with a barrier so that our voices couldn’t be heard outside. While there shouldn’t be anyone eavesdropping and it isn’t particularly troublesome if we get overheard, Ciel would probably feel more comfortable speaking with a barrier up.

「Now then, let us change your clothes.」

With Mia’s help, Ciel takes off her clothes.

『Mia went through so much effort choosing this outfit, and we probably won’t be wearing it again today.』

『Changing again is bothersome, yes.』

『Well, that’s true…―But Ciel, if you want to change back into it, then feel free to do as you want.』

If we want to make Miss Leshy happy, then buying this on the spot and wearing it for the rest of the day would be the best option, but I’d prefer that Ciel follow what her heart desires. It’s not good to backseat other people’s friendships anyway; and if Miss Leshy can’t respect Ciel’s decisions to begin with, their friendship won’t last long.

Nonetheless, I’m sure Ciel prefers the outfit Miss Leshy chose to the one we wore on the way, so there’s probably no need to say this out loud.

「You chose these clothes for me, but I might not wear them for the rest of the day.」

「You’ve worn it on the way here; that’s more than enough.」

「Really?」

「There are even cases where outfits would never be worn again after being used in public; there are even people who have clothes in their closet that would never see the light of day.」

「There are clothes treated like that?」

Ciel raised her voice in surprise. We only carry the bare minimum amount of clothes when traveling, so her reaction is understandable, but don’t we also have a lot of still unworn clothes in our closet at the manor?

Well, we’ll probably end up wearing it sooner or later, though.

Now, for the outfit Miss Leshy chose, it consisted of a white blouse and a black high-waist skirt. It seems like she gave up on the summer dress. They’re made of thin fabrics, making them feel breezy, but not thin enough to be translucent.

There’s a moss green ribbon at the chest area, and it also came with a yellow-green cardigan and a necklace with a yellow gemstone.

It looks expensive overall, which probably shouldn’t even need mention, and the colorful additions can be seen as Miss Leshy’s small act of resistance.

She probably wanted to dress Ciel in yellowish clothes.

As a whole, if not for the necklace, it could be mistaken for a school uniform. Not this world’s academy uniform, but my previous world’s―specifically the type you’d see in creative media.

The skirt is long, but not too long. One thing for certain is that this isn’t something a normal student can afford.

「Lady Ainsel, if you may excuse me.」

Responding to Mia, I undo the hair barrier. As I wondered how she’d style Ciel’s hair, it looks like she’s going with a simple braid on the back. With the length of Ciel’s hair, it’ll take a long time to make tight braids, so I guess that’s understandable.

With the hair interlocking into place, it resulted in a cute hairstyle I couldn’t possibly pull off, which Ciel then checked by swinging her head left and right.

「How does it look?」

「It suits you nicely.」

『How do you like it, Ciel?』

「Great! As I thought, black really is wonderful, wonderful, you know!」

While I’m glad to see Ciel overjoyed, I don’t really know how to respond. In my place, Mia answers, 「It’s Lady Ainsel’s color, after all.」 Seeing how pleased Ciel is, I’m sure Miss Leshy will be very relieved.

+++

# **198: Outing, Matching, and Question**

「Mia, can we buy this outfit?」

「I’ll have it arranged so that you can keep wearing it.」

「Alright, I’ll leave it to you.」

As I randomly mused about how the clothing in this world doesn’t have price tags on them, I listened to the conversation.

『That reminds me, how about your mobility?』

「Hmm, I can’t really say. It’s not particularly difficult to move in.」

『Then it should be alright.』

「Compared to this, dresses are harder to move in.」

Now that she mentioned it, that is true, but unfamiliar clothing should be a bit difficult to move in. But apparently, that isn’t the case for Ciel.

As I finished that line of thought, there was a light knock at the door.

At first I thought, _Mia’s quite quick_, but then, 「How is it, Miss Ail?」 I heard Miss Leshy’s voice.

『I’ll undo the barrier now.』

『Understood. But what do I do?』

『You could let her inside. She likely wants to see you wearing the clothes.』

「Please feel free to enter.」

Employing my advice, Ciel turned to the door and replied. The door slowly opened, and Miss Leshy, with her attendant, was now visible.

Her clothes are different from before, now looking similar to what Ciel is currently wearing. The main difference is that she has a wine-red ribbon and a pink cardigan. I suppose being able to easily coordinate matching outfits is one of the advantages of pre-made goods.

I can understand why she wanted matching clothes, but I’m a bit envious. I want to go on an outing while wearing matching clothes with Ciel, too. I want to be led around by the hand, guided by Ciel’s whims and curiosity. Walking around while holding hands would be embarrassing, though.

「So you changed too, Miss Leshy? It looks similar to this outfit…」

「Umm… is it no good?」

Miss Leshy anxiously cast down her eyes. In contrast to the anxious princess, Ciel wasn’t bothered at all, replying, 「It’s alright.」 Seemingly relieved, Miss Leshy raised her head with delight.

「It suits you as well, Miss Ail.」

「Wearing black really makes me feel happy.」

Ciel was a bit excited and couldn’t keep a proper conversation, but Miss Leshy didn’t appear offended by it. If they’re fine with this arrangement, then alright, I guess.

Perhaps happy that Ciel is wearing the outfit she chose, Miss Leshy’s eyes were glued to Ciel, but then her gaze suddenly turned to Ciel’s head. Ciel took off the hat while changing; is she curious about Ciel’s white hair?

「Miss Ail, you always wear that hair accessory, don’t you?」

「That’s true.」

It looks like she’s curious about the hairpin-turned-spirit’s resting spot. That reminds me, I completely forgot that we always have it on. We haven’t been with spirits as much lately, but is that alright? Well, it’s probably fine. Lisyl hasn’t really acted differently, after all.

「Is it a precious belonging of yours?」

「I suppose it is important, but―」

『How should I respond? It’s best to keep the spirit stuff a secret, right?』

『That’s right. As long as you don’t mention that, feel free to describe it in any way you like. No, if you do think it’s fine to tell her about it, you can do that, too. But in that case, I’ll have to use a barrier so it’s only audible to Princess Leshy and Mia.』

『I’ll keep quiet about the spirits.』

『Understood.』

It’s not like they can do much with the spirit-related information, and even if this is stolen from us, it merely absorbs magic power―while it can also conveniently change its shape, but it isn’t really something worth the effort of stealing.

Still, I won’t allow it to be stolen in the first place, and if it does get stolen from us, the spirits might get angry.

「This is an accessory that absorbs magic power.」

「Is it a type of sorceric tool?」

「No, it doesn’t appear to be one. I’m wearing it as part of my disguise, but I really can’t recommend it to other people.」

「Ah…―So it was that sort of thing.」

It seems like Ciel decided to make it so the hairpin has magic power suppressing capabilities, and Miss Leshy accepted that explanation.

Certainly, it shouldn’t attract too much interest this way. It would also explain why Ailneige’s magic power is only around a noble’s average, and if we say that it was given by Mother Fii, whatever we say about it should sound somewhat legit.

Mia returned soon after, and we decided to leave the establishment.

---

After that, we had lunch at a somewhat expensive-looking restaurant and went to the park where Ausente’s largest sorceric tool, the clock tower, stood.

I don’t really know if it’s only officially the largest sorceric tool in Ausente, or if it’s physically the largest one, but with it looking as impressive as the clock towers in my memories, it’s undoubtedly amazing.

It appears to be a popular tourist attraction, as the place was bustling with people, and there were also other sorceric tools and contraptions in the nearby area. Like the water fountain, the contraption that makes flowers bloom as desired, and the clock tower’s elevator. The fountain, for example, occasionally has its water forming the shape of birds or flowers, making it even more impressive than the fountains in my old world.

There were also food stalls at the park, and we even ate as we walked around, but Miss Leshy seemed quite experienced with this, so maybe she actually does this regularly.

Being a food lover, Ciel enjoyed it greatly, but as expected, they couldn’t try all the stalls, and their stall tour ended shortly.

And as the sun began to set, we leisurely had tea at a fancy cafe.

We ate a lot on the way, so the two only had black tea with no snacks.

「Thank you for keeping me company for the whole day.」

「It was fun seeing various new places.」

「I’m glad to hear you enjoyed it. However, this is all for today. There still were other things I hoped to show you, but…」

# **※POV Shift**

Saying so, Miss Leshy turns her gaze to the view outside.

I have no idea how much she actually enjoyed herself, but from the subtle loneliness seeping from her expression, it must have been a relatively satisfying day.

「Miss Leshy, you really love Ausente, don’t you?」

「Yes, it’s my beloved kingdom that I wish to protect. And if possible―」

Staring at Ciel, Miss Leshy was about to say something, but, 「Never mind,」 she retracted her words.

I can guess what she wanted to say, but since she decided not to continue, I won’t tell Ciel about it. I’d answer if she asked, though.

「Say, Miss Ail…」

「What is it?」

「May I invite you out again?」

Miss Leshy anxiously asked Ciel.

『Can I make the final decision?』

『Of course.』

『Just to be sure, could you make us inaudible to the surroundings?』

Since Ciel appears to have something in mind, I decided to keep to myself and leave everything to her. And as she requested, I then enveloped the two of them within a barrier.

Miss Leshy’s attendants might notice something out of place, but she’ll probably handle the aftermath well.

Even if they can’t hear anything, it’s not like Ciel is planning anything malicious.

In contrast to Miss Leshy’s nervous countenance, Ciel stared at her and spoke with a seemingly carefree expression.

「Miss Leshy, what is your opinion of songs?」

「Songs?」

---

Miss Ailneige―No, Miss Ail, who was wearing an outfit similar to mine but differently colored, posed a question about songs.

This sudden question, seemingly unrelated to our conversation up until now, caught me dumbfounded, resulting in me only being able to parrot her last word.

However, by the time Miss Ail had replied, 「Yes,」 my mind had finally started to process it, so I quickly examined my surroundings―particularly my attendants. Regardless of what I say, I must tread on the topic of songs carefully.

Noticing the movement of my eyes, Miss Ail told me, 「No one else can hear us.」

Miss Ail’s favorite soundproofing spell. It’s highly convenient, but she can invoke it without others noticing. Considering how I’ve never seen her chanting, she must have it on a magic circle she keeps close.

If not, it could be the effect of a sorceric tool.

Regardless, the fact that it was of great help remains unchanged, so I gave my thanks. In hindsight, Miss Ailneige was simply resolving an issue that she herself caused, so perhaps my gratitude was unnecessary.

More importantly, I must answer Miss Ail’s question.

_What is my opinion of songs?_ If I want to play safe, 「Other than the hymns and church songs, they don’t have a very good reputation,」 should be my answer.

While we haven’t had the same experience as the Estoque Kingdom, we know of its history, and, with the part that a Song Princess played in it, songs do not have a good image by any means.

There is a faction in the church that champions equality for all Jobs―salvation for the Misfortunate Jobs―but it’s said that there is a tacit agreement that the Song Princess is exempted from their vision.

In truth, I’ve heard various different whisperings, but if I have to answer as the Princess of Ausente, then the previous answer is the only one I can speak. I cannot risk making statements that may put us in opposition to the church and the other nations.

However, I don’t believe that it’s simply all bad. I cannot forget the song of the one that saved us on our way back to the Royal Capital.

The song had a melody different from those sung at the church; it was my first time hearing such a tune, and it stole my heart. And, while this is mere speculation, I believe that song actually saved us.

Certainly, a Song Princess once destroyed Estoque’s royal capital, but why exactly did she do such a deed? This information is not known to the public.

There has only been a vague implication that it was done out of malice and, previously, that answer was satisfactory enough.

Even if the truth was the opposite, I alone―perhaps even with my Father’s aid―cannot do anything about it. Rather, it is because we have the responsibility to govern a kingdom that we cannot do anything about it.

It would be ironic if only we kept on unraveling hidden truths, but anyway, I personally have a good impression of songs.

「I personally have positive feelings towards songs.」

I didn’t want to make Miss Ail wait nor, did I want to lie to her, so this was my response. I know that if I answer this wrong, I may risk my relationship with Miss Ail―with Lady Cielmer―but I still didn’t want to lie.

「I see. Then please continue calling me Ail from now on.」

「Are you sure?!」

If Father were to ever hear my emotive, shrill voice, I hope he could excuse my reaction.

I was just so overjoyed, you see.

「Yes. Also, if the opportunity allows it, please guide me around Royal Capital Ausente again.」

「Of course.」

As though to reaffirm Miss Ail’s acknowledgment, I relayed my words of acceptance.

I don’t know if we can be considered friends now, but at the very least, we should be closer than we were before… I hope.

_Still, I wonder why she brought up songs_, I thought, before realizing something very important. In fact, I can’t even believe that I couldn’t connect the dots up until the end. It is without a doubt that the one who rescued us is connected to Miss Ail, and she greatly treasures that individual. That is why she asked me for my opinion on songs, and had I given an unfavorable response, our relationship could have ended then and there.

And although the issue has been resolved for now, this means that my foolish brother has previously acted discourteously towards the Central Princess’ precious individual.

If that’s truly the case…―I might have to meet with Father again soon.

+++

# **199: Sorceric Tools and Secret Room**

Ever since the outing with Princess Leshimiiya―with Miss Leshy―she has been more openly talkative to us at the academy.

It’s mostly short exchanges, so it isn’t too conspicuous, but there may be some people who view it differently. The young lady Rulinia of the Hausen family, for example, is quite conscious of Ailneige when we chat with Miss Leshy.

Incidentally, I’ve also started addressing the princess as Miss Leshy when there aren’t people around. It’s only natural since I am also Ailneige, but it personally feels complicated for me since Ciel is the one who actually got closer with her.

Due to this, I did try calling her Miss Leshimiiya once, but she looked so sad about it, so that was the last time as well. It could end up being bothersome if other people hear us calling each other by nickname, but since Ciel regularly calls her Miss Leshy now, there’s nothing else I can do.

That said, while the princess has started talking to us more, Palra is still the one who talks to us the most, and just like every other day, I’m currently keeping her company.

「Bell and I talked about going to the Hunter Guild sometime; would you mind coming along with us, Ailneige?」

「The Hunter Guild, huh…」

「… I guess that’s a no?」

Perhaps due to my unsure response, Palra asked with a sad tone.

Belltina has also become relatively fit lately, so they should be able to complete beginner requests now. Even if they end up being a burden, they’d be safe as long as I’m with them.

That’s why I’m not particularly against it… But I should consult with Ciel first.

『What should we do?』

『Well, it should be fine, right? Or would you rather not, Ain?』

『I was just thinking that it’ll be troublesome if we bump into Alcrei when going to the guild with Belltina.』

『Hmm… Oh, that’s true.』

It took a few seconds for Ciel to recall him, but it’s already impressive enough that she actually remembered. In my previous life, I couldn’t even remember the names of all my classmates.

『Well, making them go by themselves is also worrying, so let’s accompany them.』

After saying so, I told Palra, 「It’s alright.」

「Thanks. Once we decide the details, I’ll update you again.」

「Please inform me as soon as possible.」

「Ah, yeah, that’s right. You have your own plans too, right? Ailneige.」

We could just discuss when we’re all present, but it seems like the two of them are training without me, and that’s when they decide things together. Since they went out of their way to do it in secret, it’s probably best not to force myself between them, so I’ll keep this idea to myself.

I’m sure they have their own reasons for practicing in secret; maybe they’re shy about being seen training hard?

And yet she invited Ailneige, so they must be a bit confident about their abilities now. If not, maybe they want our advice about something.

Reasons aside, since we’ll be going to the Hunter Guild, there’s one thing they’ll have to keep vigilant of.

「Since we’re going with Belltina, please make sure to keep the possibility of bumping into _him_ in mind.」

「Ah, yeah, gotta be careful.」

Directing her gaze to Alcrei, Palra quickly understood my warning. After that, we reverted to the usual idle chat.

---

In summary, the second academy’s first semester starts from April and ends in August, and we’re given a month-long break. The second term lasts from October to February, with March being another break. The cross-academic athletic meet with the first academy will be held during October, so we apparently won’t have proper classes during that time.

In other words, since summer divides the first semester from the second, many of the current classes are gradually approaching their end.

And for the Sorceric Tool course, it’s around this time for the students to finish their first sorceric tool.

Tietta managed to finish hers early, so she’s currently seeing if she can apply what she learned into making protective gear. Belltina still hasn’t finished her project, and I suspect that she’ll be cutting it close to the deadline. She does frequently doze off in class, but I guess that’s fine as long as she finishes in time.　

And just now, a student who seems to be already finished with their project asked Professor Liens about the sorceric tools he has made.

「I’ve crafted many sorceric tools, but most of them aim to measure and examine. There are those that assess magic power quantity, spells, physique… and marriage compatibility, I guess.

I wanted to make a sorceric tool for identifying one’s Job, but it seems like it’s only possible for those with the Artificer Job. There hasn’t been much progress.」

He then started explaining the various difficulties he’s faced, and it was pretty enlightening.

Sorcery is capable of a wide variety of things, but it isn’t suitable for examining something and providing results in numerical value. In fact, it’s plain impossible.

No matter what spell I use, I can’t tell how many centimeters tall Ciel is. I can sense people with detection, but I can’t tell their weight and mass. Because of this, creating sorceric tools that function as measuring devices is, apparently, very difficult.

Since it can’t be measured in numerical value, a different indicator becomes necessary; for example, magic power capacity can be roughly measured by how brightly the sorceric tool glows when magic power flows through it. And so, how you turn your ideas into viable results will depend on your skill and creativity.

That aside, how do you even assess marriage compatibility between two people? Unless you can see the future, it’ll be hard to say, if you ask me.

Well, ignoring that, I honestly think that Professor Liens is very talented as an artificer.

He probably wasn’t included in Princess Leshy’s list due to the reputation he built in time as a former imperial sorcerer and because his Job isn’t related to sorceric tools. After all, if you only judge him by his history, he doesn’t really appear that competent.

But because of that, it’s possible that he currently doesn’t get proper acknowledgment as well.

『After this period, let’s investigate Professor Liens for a bit.』

『I don’t mind, but why is that?』

『It’s just a hunch, but he seems suspicious.』

『Understood. What should I do?』

『For now, I’ll only observe his movements, so please continue as normal.』

If it’s only one person, I can monitor their movements through detection. I’ll have difficulty staying alert against other people if I focus on a single individual, but I don’t really need to be on high alert inside the academy.

Hypothetically speaking, even if someone does happen to stab Ciel in the back because I have my guard down, it’s not like I’ll undo our barrier anyway, so, for the moment, I decided to stalk Professor Liens’ presence.

---

As I continued following Professor Liens’ presence, despite not leaving my detection range, he suddenly disappeared. That’s when I also noticed that there’s apparently a mysterious room that my detection can’t perceive. It’s probably being obstructed by a sorceric tool or something.

If we were closer, we could forcefully investigate it, but since I’ve spread my detection range thin in following his presence, the fidelity is pretty bad. In this state, if I didn’t focus on following Professor Liens from the start, I would’ve immediately lost track of him in the crowd.

In exchange, my range can be spread to the point where it could envelop the entirety of the royal capital. Having the royal palace within my detection range is probably more trouble than its worth, so I didn’t stretch it that far.

Well, while I did lose him, this does lead to one possibility.

『Found a suspicious room.』

『Oh, that was fast.』

『He most likely wasn’t expecting anyone to search for him.』

If he had been vigilant and avoided going to that room for several days, it would have taken a long time for me to discover it. Even if we assume that the headmistress informed him about Ailneige, it’s already been several months since then. Staying vigilant for that long should be difficult… I think. Well, it should be doable if you really put your mind into it, but I even probably couldn’t do it if it isn’t for Ciel’s sake.

『Shall we go right now?』

『We’ve confirmed the location, so let’s head there at another date. Even if we go now, there’s no assurance that we’ll find Professor Liens there; it would be better to book an appointment today so we can meet with him for certain.』

『Is that really okay?』

『It’s fine. The hidden room is apparently inside a regular room.』

If Professor Liens isn’t present, we likely can’t even enter the room connecting to the hidden room. Our goal isn’t really to expose the hidden room, but that’s probably the best way to corner him. After all, without firm evidence, he could still talk himself out of admitting the truth.

---

The next day, we successfully secured consultation time, so we arrived in front of Professor Liens’ laboratory. The laboratories are located in a building separate from the lecture building, and every teacher is granted their own.

While we’re free to go to their laboratories for walk-in consultations, it would be a big waste of time if you went and the teachers weren’t available, especially with it being a fair distance away. Because of this, you can request an appointment at the dormitory reception desk.

Valid reasons are required, but since we have a course with Professor Liens, I was able to secure an appointment without any questioning.

「Professor Liens, it’s Ailneige.」

With a knock, I gave my name, and he responded, 「Come inside,」 from behind the door. Minding my manners, I bowed upon entering the room while also tapering with the room a bit.

「I see, it’s you. I was informed that you had inquiries; what would you like to know?」

It looks like he hadn’t matched my name to my face. Well, I’m sure we’re not the only students he’s handling; memorizing each of his students’ names and faces must be a difficult task.

「I do have a question, but I was also hoping to see the sorceric tools you’ve made for inspiration. Would it be alright to ask after seeing them?」

「Sure, feel free to examine all the sorceric tools in this room.」

「Thank you very much.」

Since there were a number of sorceric tools displayed, I made that excuse on a whim, and it turned out well.

Nonetheless, there are so many sorceric tools. This personally tickled my interest, so I put aside our original goal and examined the sorceric tools, asking Professor Liens for explanations from time to time.

There were some so intricately made that I―a beginner who only started crafting sorceric tools a few months ago―could only marvel at his high skill level.

「That reminds me, what does the marriage compatibility sorceric tool assess for?」

「Ahhー… I’d prefer you pretend not to have heard that.」

「Understood.」

He was about to say something, but it’s probably not something he could openly state in public. At the very least, it isn’t something he can say to a student.

I was just a bit curious, so this isn’t really an issue, and after going around the whole room, I stood at a certain spot and returned to our actual purpose here.

「Thank you very much. It has been quite educational.」

「I’m glad to hear that. Now, have you finished formulating your question?」

He spoke with a smile, but I felt a hint of suspicion from him; maybe I was prying too much earlier.

At any rate, since he appears to be willing to answer, I decided to go straight to the point.

「Professor Liens, are you attempting to commit a taboo?」

Hearing my question, he responded, 「What are you talking about?」 with an unchanged expression. Him playing dumb is within expectations. I turned my back to where the hidden room should be connected to before interrogating him again.

「Since you insist that you’re innocent, then it’s fine for me to enter the room behind me, right?」

The instant I said that, Professor Liens’ face jerked.

+++

# **200: Sorceric Tools, Madness, and Resolve**

「Feel free to do as you like.」

「I see. Then I shall feel free to do so.」

Professor Liens is uncannily compliant. There must be a trap or something. Probably the type to activate if a proper procedure isn’t followed, but, unfortunately, while I know something awaits us, I have no idea how to avoid it.

Nonetheless, things will probably go smoother if he’s shown that I didn’t figure out the hidden room by pure guesswork, and I am confident with my defenses, so forcing our way through is an option.

『It seems to be a trap, but would it be alright to go?』

『As long as you switch out with me.』

『Naturally. After all, if anything ever happens, Ciel will have an easier time dealing with it.』

Whatever happens, I’d never do something that would risk our lives. With Ciel in control, at worst, we can just completely demolish the room. Even if there are a variety of traps, Ciel will be able to handle them safely.

Nothing I do really needs me to be in control to perform in the first place.

And so I switched with Ciel, and she then touched the shelf in front of us. There is a shelf displaying sorceric tools near the corner of the room farthest from the entrance, and there seems to be a small gap there. This gap is wide enough to accommodate one person. Two, if around Ciel’s width.

If this shelf is pushed aside, it should reveal this hidden gap. Based on Professor Liens’ activity yesterday, there might be a stairway leading underground.

Ciel used physical reinforcement and moved the shelf aside. Hidden under the shelf was what seemed to be a hatchway, and when Ciel approached it, I sensed a sorceric tool inside the room activate.

And I just noticed it now, but several sorceric tools displayed in the room are actually arranged in a way that points towards the hatchway.

Ciel quickly noticed it as well, so she jumped to the ceiling.

Seeing the thick vines from all directions converging right below us, it must have been a sorceric tool for capturing intruders. Bumping into each other, the converging vines rolled into a ball-like lump.

The reason Ciel escaped to the air was because that was the only viable escape.

However, Professor Liens naturally understands this as well, and immediately after Ciel jumped, a pitfall opened up underneath Ciel. It doesn’t seem to be too deep, but it most likely leads to a prison, and we’ll be captured if nothing else is done.

『Ain.』

Ciel called my name, so I immediately sang in response.

We’ve already fallen inside the pitfall, but there’s still an opening above, so it’s not an issue. Like a fawn prancing in the plains, Ciel spirals in the air with light steps. And after landing a few steps away from the pitfall, she switches with me.

Professor Liens was apparently captivated by Ciel’s movements, but he then came to his senses and acted as if nothing happened.

「I was warned to be vigilant against you, but to think you’d be this capable.」

「Amazing as always.」

Ciel did great, so regardless of what Professor Liens thinks, I praised Ciel. Ignoring his confusion, he mentioned a detail I couldn’t disregard, so I pressed for an answer.

「By the way, was the headmistress the one who warned you about me?」

「I can’t answer that.」

Professor Liens shook his head without giving a yes or no answer. If he had said yes, it would have confirmed that he’s doing something related to the taboo. Considering the lengths he took to protect this room, it’s practically enough of a confirmation for me even now, but there’s still a chance I’m wrong. He might just be hiding a top-secret sorceric tool unrelated to the taboo.

I’m neither a detective or a police officer, nor am I even particularly skilled in gathering information. That’s why, if possible, I want direct verbal confirmation regarding taboo-related things.

「Incidentally, what is your objective?」

I honestly thought that he would run, but Professor Liens didn’t even make an attempt, though he’s apparently changing his tactics. He’s actually asking us our objective.

I enveloped the room with a barrier just to make sure that he can’t escape, but it seems it was for nothing. Still won’t undo it, though. Now, our objective, huh. It’s not like we’re here to make enemies, so it should be fine to just answer. After all, unlike earlier, it’s not like we can play ignorant at this point.

In the extremely unlikely event that he actually isn’t our taboo guy, there is a chance that he’ll tell other people that Ailneige is looking for someone committing the taboo, but we can just hush him when that happens.

At the very least, it’s certain that he’s up to something in this secret room, so it shouldn’t be difficult to hush him.

「If I had to say, it’s to warn people attempting to commit a taboo and, I suppose, try to persuade them against it.」

His eyes went wide in surprise, but shortly he muttered, 「I see,」 and began contemplating.

「So you’re saying that you did not come to eliminate or capture me, nor to plunder my research?」

「The first one is the closest answer, but I won’t be the one to enact it. I’m just the prelude.」

「… Divine punishment, huh.」

Hearing his conclusion, I responded with a smile.

Even without us doing anything to the people attempting a taboo, divine punishment will eliminate them from the world the moment it becomes a problem. Our goal is to give a warning so that doesn’t happen. And just because we’re warning against it, the occurrence of divine punishment isn’t really a problem for us or the Creator God.

「Now, I’ll ask once more. Professor Liens, you are attempting to commit a taboo, aren’t you?」

「… Yes, that’s right.」

Professor Liens answered in a resigned tone. It would be great if he also gave up on continuing his taboo research, but that’s probably impossible. Still, with his admission, we can consider the first phase done, and now, as previously discussed with Ciel, I’ll reveal our identity.

Rather than the words of some mysterious first year, the words of someone connected to Fiiyanamia should hold more persuasive weight. And it’s a chance to test something else, too.

I retrieved the long-neglected pendant with Mother Fii’s white dragon crest from our magic pouch and showed it to Professor Liens.

Shown the pendant, Professor Liens was befuddled at first, but then his eyes opened wide in shock. Finally, with difficulty, he opened his mouth.

「To think you were Central’s princess.」

「I’m not actually a princess, but I was indeed adopted by Mother Fii.」

「Pedantics aside, you are still the princess of Central.」

「I do understand that.」

Which is why I don’t refute it often; besides, there are times when it makes things easier for us. Having “princess” even just as a title also makes it easy to relay how much influence we have.

That aside, it’s safe to consider this experiment a success. People of certain positions at least know what this emblem signifies. In other words, it can function as material proof that we’re Mother Fii’s daughter.

If the time comes when we are forced to reveal that we’re Central’s princess-like figure, it’s easy enough to assert it, but there’s no assurance that everyone we meet will take our words at face value.

There’s no point in revealing our identity if it can’t serve as a deterrent. The people I’ve revealed myself to, like the royal family and heads of major organizations, were probably required to know the meaning of this emblem, so I wanted to see if it works on teachers and other middle-level professionals as well.

And since it worked on Professor Liens, commoners aside, it should have some influence on nobles.

「With you being the princess of Central, I suppose it’s no wonder that you knew I was researching a taboo, huh.」

「So you understand that much.」

「It’s commonly said that it shouldn’t be a surprise for the mistress to have knowledge of everything, after all. Besides, it’s speculated that she’s connected to the divine.」

She has occupied Central for several lifetime’s worth of time, so there’s sure to be speculation abound. Speaking of which, no one can keep secrets from Mother Fii within Central’s domain, but without this context, it’s not surprising if people to think that she just knows everything.

Regardless, I’m glad this conversation’s going smoothly.

「Since you already know that much, I will be carrying out my task, then. Please stop your taboo-aligned research immediately.」

「… That’s something I can’t do.」

「Is it because you’re under orders?」

I asked, hoping that this was the case, but considering how firm and resolute his response was, it’s probably not―even if he was, he’s probably a willing accomplice anyway.

And it seems like my suspicion was correct, as Professor Liens shook his head and gave a firm denial.

「No, it’s personal research.」

「Suspected as much. However, if this ever bears fruit, you’re going to die, you know?」

「I’m well aware of that.」

「The divine punishment erases your results without any trace for the world to remember, you know?」

「…―That is a bit sad. Still, not a problem with me dead by then.」

「Not even death would stop you?」

「Unfortunately so.」

Seeing Professor Liens answer with a carefree tone unlike before, I’m inclined to think that nothing can probably sway him.

He’s aware that he’ll die and won’t even stop even if his final product is destroyed without a single trace, and we don’t even know what motivates his research.

『Why is he so adamant about committing the taboo?』

『Let me try asking.』

「Why are you so adamant about continuing your taboo research?」

「Well… It’s because I want to create the greatest masterpiece I can, I suppose. A masterpiece so great that no one can refute its greatness. A masterpiece that no one can ever top even in the future.」

「And so, the taboo.」

「Precisely. Receiving divine punishment for your work would mean that you have crafted something acknowledged by the very gods themselves.」

Professor Liens responded with a weirdly excited tone, which is a bit scary.

No one can blame me for thinking that he has several screws loose for wanting to create something that would trigger a divine punishment just to get the recognition of the gods.

Still, it’s not like I’m any better considering how I previously planned to erase my very existence for Ciel’s sake. So it’s not like I can’t understand having something you deem more valuable than your life.

That aside, that did give me something to persuade Professor Liens with, so I’ll try it out.

「I was told that you will successfully achieve the taboo in the near future. Knowing that, there’s really no need to put your life on the line, is there?」

「There’s no assurance that you’re speaking the truth. Besides, if that is true, then that would confirm that I’m currently on the right track.」

「I thought you would say that.」

Persuading people like him is far too much for me.

Talking him out of this isn’t our goal anyway, so I guess we can go home now.

「Since it’s meaningless to persuade you any further, I’ll consider my task done and return home.」

「You think I can just let you freely leave with the knowledge of my research?」

「You have learned my true identity, so isn’t that enough?」

Since we know each other’s secrets, there shouldn’t be any concern that one of us will speak out, but Professor Liens seems unconvinced.

「Even if that secret of yours becomes known, it’s unlikely to be a fatal problem. Quite unfair, don’t you think?」

「When you put it that way, that is quite troubling. Still, you can’t really stop me from going home, you know?」

「If you do that, you might just lose your place in the academy.」

True, our secret isn’t necessarily life-ruining even if revealed. It might result in certain weird people approaching us, but it’s not unmanageable, nor does it negatively affect our social standing.

In that sense, it’s certainly not fair for Professor Liens, since his secret could ruin his life and even have him marked for death.

And while I don’t know if he actually means the _‘losing our place in the academy’_ part, Professor Liens is a teacher and we’re just a student. We are under him in the academy hierarchy, so I can’t deny the possibility of us being forced to drop out.

In other words, he probably wants a secret that we actually want to be kept hidden, but… _hmmm_…

『Ain, can we switch places?』

『Of course.』

_‘I really wanted to avoid using force as much as possible…’_ I thought to myself, but since Ciel requested it, I switched with her.

「In short, we just need to tell a problematic secret, right?」

As we switched, I was wondering what Ciel was planning when she suddenly gave that daring response.

+++

# **201: Revelation and Temporary Resolution**

Ciel spoke without changing her natural speech pattern, making Professor Liens freeze in surprise. The sheer difference from how I spoke must’ve given him whiplash; I feel for him.

Still, perhaps thinking that he can’t stay stunned forever, he pulled himself together and replied, 「That’s right.」 It looks like he’s elected to ignore the change in tone.

「In that case, I’ll give two. Before that, right, nice to meet you, Liens. I’m Cielmer.」

「Nice to meet you…?」

Professor Liens’ confusion was obvious for anyone to see. Meanwhile, I’m shocked myself. I never expected Ciel to ever reveal herself on her own accord.

She must have felt something in the professor that made her think it’s fine to tell him, but… Wait, now that I think about it, Professor Liens is undoubtedly the kind of person that would attract Ciel’s interest.

And it feels like her reason for telling him is different from when we shared our secret with Carol and Munyechka.

「Yes, it’s our first time meeting. I didn’t take the sorceric tool course, after all.」

「You’re talking as if you’re two different people.」

「We are. She was just talking to you until now, right?」

「In that case, what’s her…」

The instant the professor asked for my name, Ciel glared at him with a cold, piercing gaze.

Her magic power surged to the point where even people with magic power but can’t perceive it would feel something amiss.

「That’s not something you need to know. There is another person inside me. That should be enough, no?

If you ever tell anyone else about this and cause her trouble, I will eliminate you without hesitation, alright?」

Saying that with a flat tone, she then knocked on the ground twice with her toes. The contact point started freezing, and from it, a frozen path with the width of Ciel’s foot crept towards Professor Liens before sprouting an icicle pushing against his neck.

「I-I understand. I won’t inquire any further.」

Hearing the professor respond while raising his chin away from the sharpened point, Ciel knocked at the floor again, dispersing the icicle.

That should be enough to know how serious Ciel is. In truth, my existence is critical in Ciel’s eyes. Even people who can’t understand this should realize that she’s not playing around after receiving this treatment.

「I’m glad you understand. As for the other thing, my Job is Dance Princess.」

Ciel then unceremoniously revealed her Job.

Hearing that, 「Wha―」 Professor Liens was at a loss for words.

「It’s not a lie. You’ll know if I lie about it anyway. After all, Aineige’s Job isn’t really well concealed. There seems to be a lot of speculation, though.」

「To be capable of so much while being a Disappointing Princess…」

The professor mustered in disbelief. We’ve actually heard that there are various speculations about Ailneige’s Job.

Since we’re a sorcerer and active hunter, many think that it might be a sorcery-related Job; meanwhile most of the students taking combat training with us think that it’s Swordsman-related.

Furthermore, anyone witnessing Ciel cast sorcery through dancing could probably reach the conclusion that she’s a Dance Princess.

Finally, the fact that she is a Disappointing Princess is something that should normally be kept secret. For the upper class, having such a Job is enough to drag you down in life, and that’d be even worse in the case of Fiiyanamia’s adopted daughter. From an outsider’s perspective, at least.

_But in that case, she could’ve mentioned my Job instead…_ I thought, but I guess the shock would be too much. Considering how he reacted to the Dance Princess revelation, saying she’s a Song Princess might just cause Professor Liens to faint in shock.

Besides, Ciel seems adamant about not revealing any information about me, so that’s probably part of the reason.

「Wait, in that case, is the other inside you…」

「Come again?」

「N-no, it’s nothing…」

Professor Liens wanted to probe for information about me but was immediately shut down. This time, Ciel didn’t intimidate him much, but he probably remembered the first time.

Still, he’s on the right track. Since there are two of us, then we might have two Jobs, with the other Job possibly being incredulous and the reason why we became Central’s Princess. I’m sure that sounds more realistic in this world than the Central’s Princess being a Dance Princess.

When in reality, it’s the even more disliked Song Princess.

「It shouldn’t be unfair now, is it?」

「O-oh, right. Yes.」

Overwhelmed by Ciel’s eagerness to end this topic, the professor immediately nodded, completely swept along by Ciel’s momentum.

Satisfied by his reply, Ciel says, 「Now let’s continue from before,」 with a smile.

『You’re continuing?』

『Otherwise, what was the point of me showing myself?』

『That might be the case, but…』

I reflexively asked out of surprise, but she has a fair point; if we only needed to convince Professor Liens, Ciel didn’t need to come out. I could’ve been the one to reveal my Job, or Ciel’s Job, instead.

There was no need to reveal that Ailneige was two people either.

「Since I’ve revealed this much, we’ll come to play again in the future.」

「… Why?」

「How do I describe it? Because you caught my interest, I guess?」

Thinking back, I somewhat expected this. Still, I don’t like the way she phrased it. The professor is looking confused as well.

「You see, I don’t dislike people who dedicate their all for something. But even among everyone I know, you feel different, Liens. That’s why I want to observe you.

I don’t plan on helping with the taboo research, but I promise that I won’t be obstructive.」

「I see… If you truly won’t get in my way, then I don’t mind.」

「Now then, I’m going home. No more problems, right?」

「Y-yeah…」

While Professor Liens was taken aback by Ciel’s energy, Ciel ignored him and left the laboratory.

---

As the day was ending and we returned to our room, I asked Ciel, 『Was revealing that to Professor Liens really alright?』

While I have heard Ciel’s reasoning for keeping an eye on him earlier, I can’t really say that I agree with her wanting to interact with him in the future. How do I say this? There’s no need to risk staying close to him. Still, I do recall the Creator God warning me that I can’t defend against a divine punishment, so perhaps this is just fate.

The Creator God likely knew that Ciel and Professor Liens would be on the same wavelength, somehow.

And with me already thinking that we can capitalize on this experience, I’m probably broken in one way or another. The professor will be a first and as a result of divine punishment at that.

「Right, somehow, I just wanted it to be that way.」

『If that’s what you really want, then I don’t really mind, but you’re not actually interested in the pursuit of taboo or crafting, right?』

「Yeah, not really. I’d be different if certain sorceric tools or taboos could manifest a body for Ain, but currently the Puppet sorcery route is the most reliable path. Besides, Munyechka should have a lot of knowledge about sorceric tools, too, right? 」

Now that she mentioned it, that does sound plausible. Puppet Sorcery is like a hybrid study of sorcery and sorceric tools. With sorceric tools intrinsically tied to it, Munyechka should have some level of mastery in crafting.

『Then why did you…』

「Hmm, let me see. He felt somewhat similar to the past Ain.」

『To… me?』

「Yeah, the way he was so firm about continuing even though it would lead to death was similar. Past Ain planned to disappear on her own, after all. 」

Perhaps recalling the memories, Ciel replied with a pouty tone.

I mean, she’s right, but, except for apologizing, I can’t really do anything about that now, so I decided to continue the conversation.

『The professor certainly has accepted that he’d die via divine punishment.』

「I can’t quite fully understand what that feels like. That’s why I’m curious.」

『You think that you’d understand by interacting with Professor Liens?』

_Don’t you have me already?_ I thought, causing my tone to be harsher. However, Ciel didn’t appear bothered at all; instead, she seemed to enjoy the situation, as she was even giggling. She probably knows what I’m thinking.

「I don’t think that at all. And I don’t want to understand either. What’s most important for me is Ain and our time together. After all, if I end up dying to protect Ain, I wouldn’t be able to stay with Ain anymore.」

『That’s… right. I think the same as well.』

「Yes, and I understand that. I’m happy, you know?」

Saying so, Ciel showed me a beautiful smile; I don’t think I can ever win against her. Nonetheless, why did she suddenly say that right now? I guess there’s no point mulling about it. It’s Ciel, after all; while it feels embarrassing to hear her say that, I can’t help but feel happy as well.

『And yet you’ll still interact with him.』

「It’s why we enrolled in the academy, isn’t it?」

『Right, you certainly could say that.』

I really can’t disagree with her reply. The reason why we enrolled in this academy is, broadly speaking, to learn through interacting with various people.

Professor Liens is merely one of the many people to interact with. As for why he was chosen, it’s as Ciel explained earlier. It’s probably part of the reason why she was so direct with him.

It’s not like the Creator God forbade us from associating with him, and even if it’s just needless worry, I just need to protect Ciel as always.

『Anyway, with our goal in the academy completed, that’s a weight off the shoulders.』

「Oh, were you feeling burdened by this in our stay at the academy, Ain?」

『That’s not exactly the case, but mentally…』

「Well, that’s true. With this, we have one less thing to think about.」

With a chuckle, Ciel agreed with my sentiment. She could’ve just answered with this earlier, but I can’t help but find Ciel cute with her roundabout ways.

++++

# **Levelmaker - Chapter 603 - Zoo Date – 1 (Kanata & Sakura)**

“This outfit is from the second batch we bought some time ago, isn’t it?” Kanata wondered.

“Does it suit me?”

“It does, it looks cute. I’m pretty sure you tried it on back then.”

“Eh-heh, I guess.”

It was Sunday, and Kanata and Sakura had dressed up stylishly before leaving the house. They planned to go to the zoo for their date, so they were both excited.

“Y-You also look good in your outfit, Kanata.”

“Thanks… Shall we go, then?”

“Let’s.”

As usual, Sakura hugged the boy’s arm in their typical fashion. It was as always, though it still felt special, causing her to narrow her eyes happily while a blush crept onto the boy’s face as he felt the sensation on his arm (even though he should have been used to it).

“In what order should we look at the animal enclosures today?”

“Our curfew is later than it used to be so… well.”

Due to the kids’ relationship staying on the wholesome side for the time being, their families had extended the curfew they set for their dates. The happiest one about that was Sakura.

“The usual route, then? Like, making a circuit around the Zoo?”

“You mean start by taking a look at everything? Alright.”

They followed Kanata’s plan and took the buses and trains that would get them to the Zoo. During their one hour or so of travel, they happily stuffed their cheeks with the snacks they brought along.

“Let’s pay the entry fee, then.”

“…Are you going to pay for me again?”

“You should get used to it at this point. I mean, it’s usually because you ask like this, that I treat you to stuff.”

“Bwuh?”

After giving her a “don’t worry about it”, he bought two entry tickets (the middle schooler variant) and they passed through the gate, still holding hands.

“If we walk the usual route… the birds of prey will be first.”

“You mean Mr. Eagle and Miss Falcon?”

“Exactly… Were you trying to sound cute right now? You did, just in case.”

“Y-Yeah, I was… Thank you.”

She blushed at him calling her cute so calmly. With her still clinging to his arm, he started to walk.

“This is the first time you properly see then, right, Sakura? Eagles, I mean.”

“Wow… This is…”

The girl’s eyes, who was seeing zoo animals clearly for the first time, shone. She got as close to the enclosure as she could.

“Oh wow, they’re looking at us!”

“Maybe they see you as prey, Sakura.”

“Do eagles and falcons prey on humans?”

“They could but they generally don’t[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119570).”

The two kids took their time looking at the enclosures containing eagles, falcons, owls, and so on, before they arrived at the petting zoo.

“A petting zoo?”

“You can hold and touch animals there.”

“Can we go in?”

“As long as you don’t mind stepping poop and properly wash your hands afterwards.”

“That’s fine!”

They entered the petting area, where they found many children at grade school age.

“Which one should I pet first…? Oh, a goat!”

Sakura didn’t hesitate to touch the goatee of the passing animal.

“Sakura, this must be your first time touching an animal, right? Aren’t you afraid?”

“Huh? Not at all. Compared to being dropped in the wilderness of another world, this isn’t scary at all.”

“I can’t deny that.”

Sakura continued petting the goat until she had her fill before setting her eyes on the next animal. It was rotund and white, with long ears.

“A rabbit!”

With glowing eyes, the girl stroked the very first rabbit she met in her life. The animal let it happen while contently narrowing its eyes.

“I had no idea rabbits were so cute! Heh-heh-heh, aren’t you a cutie?”

“Sakura, you seem more excited than usual today…”

“Such a cutie pie!”

She kept petting the animal. Kanata considered telling her that she was cuter than the rabbit, but thought better of it.

“Rabbits are great…”

“How about you ask if you can pet the ears of that woman called Parasuna when we’re back in Anazumu?”

“Eh, she’s an acquaintance of Big Sis and Ayu-nii. Asking for that so off-handedly would be rude.”

“I guess.”

“And in the first place, she’s a person, not an animal…”

Afterwards, she went to pet piglets, little chicks, hamsters, squirrels, and much more. She left the place looking very satisfied. The ones she liked most were rodents like rabbits[2](#easy-footnote-bottom-2-119570), squirrels, and hamsters.

“They were adorable… but now my hands smell like animal.”

“Well… that’s probably the reason Rir doesn’t like to go to the zoo.”

“I can imagine with her overly sensitive nose.”

The two kids thoroughly washed their hands before making their way to the next animal enclosures. There, they found a multitude of tropical animals. The ones commonly associated with zoos.

“Elephants really are this big. They’re like magic beasts.”

“You shouldn’t lump animals together with monsters.”

“Giraffes! Now that I look at them, they also feel a lot like magic beasts.”

“Again, don’t lump them in with monsters.”

The kids rapidly went from one animal to the next. Sakura especially, since this was her first time at the Zoo since regaining her eyesight, was thrilled about the usual zoo animals.

“I’m pretty sure that one’s a serval. They can jump more than two meters high… or so I heard. Could Rir do the same?”

“No, even she won’t manage two meters on Earth.”

In high spirits and chatting happily like a normal couple, they made their way to the next animal enclosure.

1. I once read about people observing an eagle taking a bear cub. So, yes, they could absolutely prey on human babies and infants, but they most likely don’t since we’re too different from their usual prey.

2. As someone mentioned all the way back in volume 1, rabbits are lagomorphs, not rodents. The main difference being that the former eat their food twice, and the latter once.
