# **Chapter 604 – Zoo Date – 2 (Kanata & Sakura)**

“Look there! A lion! And not the six-legged, shiny black kind!”

“You’re right, it might eat you in a single gulp with that big mouth…”

“Grr, you keep saying this stuff for a while now.”

The two kids had made their way halfway around the enclosures for tropical animals. They kept joking about what if this were Anazumu and the animals magic beasts.

“…!?”

While they were at it, Kanata suddenly turned his head with a ghastly expression.

“Is something wrong, Kanata?”

“No… I just thought… must’ve been my imagination.”

“Okay?”

From that point on, there was an air of vigilance about the boy as they continued walking through the zoo. The two of them came to a halt in front of the monkey mountain, which was close to the eating area.

“A monkey mountain!”

“They look so different. It’s incredible to think that humans evolved from them.”

“I guess, but I keep thinking… some people, like Big Sis, feel more like they’ve evolved from squirrels rather than monkeys.”

“True, our faces are very different from monkeys,” Kanata commented on Sakura’s sudden thought. “Beauty and cuteness might be something unique to humans.”

“But Rir is a wolf.”

“From how she lets Shuu spoil her, she feels more like a puppy than a wolf.”

“That’s true.”

They (or at least Sakura) leisurely watched the monkeys grooming each other and eating apples before walking towards the eating area.

“Going to the petting zoo and looking at the tropical animals took a lot of time. Shall we eat lunch?”

“That’s fine for me. I saw on TV before that they serve authentic curry here.”

“They do. I’ve read that they conducted extensive research to make it as delicious as possible. It’s supposedly so good, they sell it as high-grade retort-pouch curry in the supermarket.”

“Then let’s get some.”

They entered the eating area and ordered one sweet and one spicy serving of the famous dish.

“…Can we eat ice cream for dessert?”

“I brought a lot of money with me today, so eat whatever you want.”

“Oh, you’re treating me to that, too? I did bring some money myself, but if you insist…”

“It’s fine.”

“Hm~…”

Thus, it was decided that they would have ice cream after their curry.

“It’s really good.”

“It truly does live up to its reputation… Should we go see the ocean animals after eating?”

“You mean penguins and such?”

“Yes, those.”

A short time later, the ice cream was brought to their table.

“…I’ll give you some of mine,” the girl offered.

“I have my own ice cream, remember?”

“But they’re different flavors… c-come on, open up.”

“Ha-ha, alright.”

After polishing off their desserts, the two of them moved towards the enclosures with penguins and marine mammals, as planned.

“Wow… penguins!”

“So far, I have seen neither a penguin beastfolk nor magic beast in Anazumu.”

“Now that you mention it, I haven’t either. Maybe they live in the north?”

“Could be… huh?”

“What’s wrong, Kanata?”

As they were watching the penguins, Kanata suddenly started staring at one point with a grave look. It felt as if he had noticed something dangerous.

“K-Kanata?”

“Sorry to interrupt our penguin watching. I… need to go to the bathroom.”

“Eh.”

Kanata was about to leave in a hurry, but Sakura quickly grabbed his hand.

“…You’re not about to stick your nose into something dangerous, are you?”

“…”

At the thought of losing the boy, she put more strength into her grip and her eyes turned moist. He patted her head after thinking for a bit.

“I mentioned it before, but someone is stalking us.”

“Huh… you mean because of the documentation about my eyesight?”

“That’s what I thought at the start, but it apparently also happened to Shuu. It feels different. I can’t help thinking that it’s related to Anazumu… And right now, this stalker is over there.”

“What!?”

Sakura quickly looked at the place where Kanata had been staring at. She didn’t see anyone there, but clearly got an ominous premonition.

“I-In that case, I’m definitely coming with you.”

“You can’t.”

“No way, I’m coming. Even if you don’t let me, I’ll just follow you.”

“…What a pain.” The boy scratched the back of his head before taking a deep sigh. “Alright. But if anything happens, you run…”

“The same goes for you.”

“What?”

“That’s only natural, right? If I were to lose you, I’d end up like Big Sis, you know? That’s why I want us to be equal and stay together… no matter the world we’re in.”

The boy stared at the girl whose eyes had turned slightly red. He could feel her strong determination.

“Alright, let’s go.”

“Eh-heh-heh… I’ll do my best to not get in your way.”

Where Kanata had been staring was a storage shed where there used to be an animal enclose, which was now deserted. There were “staff only” labels here and there, and obviously no other guests. Kanata and Sakura made their way inside.

“Somehow… if feels completely different here.”

“I mean, it’s a deserted area.”

The two of them advanced carefully, relying on what Kanata had seen earlier, until they reached what looked like a small, open space. There, someone wearing a black hood was standing.

# **Chapter 605 – The Suspicious Person (Kanata & Sakura)**

Kanata held out one arm in front of him so he could protect Sakura at any time, and advanced little by little.

“(Wh-Who’s that?)”

“(No clue. But they’re clearly suspicious.)”

The two kids moved behind the nearest storage to get temporary relief from the pressure emanated by the person who was simply standing there, and observed the situation.

“Way too suspicious…”

“Yeah…”

Five minutes after they reached this spot, the man in black finally turned his gaze on them. Then, he spoke for the first time.

“Co… come… out.”

The two kids were baffled by his words accompanied by a beckoning motion. Kanata steeled his heart and stepped forward. Sakura nuzzled up close to him, trembling slightly.

“Who are you?”

“…Identity… doesn’t matter… Let… see you… better…”

Kanata took a step forward in response to the strange demand. Sakura kept behind him, as if to hide herself.

“Hrm… Grown big.”

“Grown big…? What are you saying…?”

Kanata was perplexed by the mysterious man nodding in satisfaction. Still, he judged that the stranger wasn’t about to attack, so he asked a question.

“Are you the one who keeps following us recently?”

“Following…? Following?”

The man in black inclined his head. It made Kanata ponder that this gesture was well-suited to certain people.

“Did not follow. Rather, did watch.”

“…You watched us? Why?”

“…Know. That’s why.”

Sakura, who only felt confusion at this conversation, went to hug Kanata.

“…You also followed Shuu, didn’t you?” the boy continued his questions. “Do know who I mean? That guy who gives off a feeling of strength.”

“Understand… Did not follow. But… did watch. Won’t deny.”

“So, you followed us because you ‘know’, but why Shuu?”

“Smelled… that’s why. Scent of Anazumu.”

That made Kanata frown even harder. The reason for that was obviously the last word.

“Anazumu…”

“…Yes, anyway, hard to speak. This. Same, but, old fellow. Yes, soon,” the man muttered with a hint of regret as he clutched his throat.

His intonation was all over the place, making it sound to the kids as if he was speaking a foreign language.

“For now, tell me this: are you an enemy?”

“Enemy? About that… enemy… ha, ha-ha-ha…”

The man laughed while holding his stomach, as if something had gone exactly as planned. Still, he seemed somewhat dejected, causing Kanata to give up on trying to judge the man’s thoughts from his behavior.

“Phew… hah… MUAH-HA-HA-HA-HA-HA-HA!”

His earlier faltering manner of talking was gone without a trace. The man, seemingly shocked himself, held his throat as his laughter became more normal. Then, as if to check whether his voice worked normally, he cleared his throat and produced a few vowels before nodding and turning his gaze on the kids, never taking off his hood.

“Hrm, did I adapt to this body? Right, I never answered your question. As for whether I am friend or foe, I don’t feel like telling you. Still… we will surely meet again. This is certain, Kanata.”

“…!!”

Kanata was shocked at the man suddenly starting to speak fluently and then addressing him by his own name. Though it wasn’t enough for him to freeze up.

“Farewell, for now…” the man spoke, before disappearing with a poof, like a shadow dissolving into air.

Only the two kids remained.

“Somehow, this turned into a big deal.”

“S-Someone other than us who knows about Anazumu… no, more importantly, he said your name…”

“My name has been broadcast in the whole country, so it’s not that strange for him to know it. Still… I’m stunned that he’s actually related to Anazumu, as I hypothesized.

The area had grown silent, a stillness in the air. Sakura gasped as if remembering something and pulled out her smartphone.

“We need to contact the others…”

“Let’s wait until tomorrow with that.”

“What?”

She looked at the boy in surprise, who was shaking his head.

“We have to gather everyone anyway, which likely won’t be possible today. They’re all busy with something.”

“That’s… true, I guess…”

She stopped fiddling with her phone and put it away. When he saw her looking anxious, he ruffled her hair somewhat roughly but still gently.

“Come on, let’s continue our date.”

“Bwuh? Are you sure?”

“I am. You were having fun, weren’t you? At this point, there’s no way we’d cancel the date over a little shock like this.”

“…Yeah.”

“I know that you’re anxious, but this is us. We’ll manage somehow.”

“Y-You mean I should rely on you?

“Yep. Please do.”

They composed themselves, resumed their date, and moved on to the mountainous enclosures where bears and foxes could be found.

# **Chapter 606 – Gathering**

The enjoyable Sunday had passed, and we were back in Anazumu to start our next two weeks there. For now, we had gathered in the usual place to hear the news Shuu had.

“How did it go?” I asked.

“You mean the individual matches?”

As he’d already told me, they had won their group matches with so much leeway that not even their middle ever had to fight, so their participation in the prefectural competition was pretty much guaranteed. It was incredible. What I was asking for were the results of the individual fights that happened on Sunday.

“Well, I easily made it to the prefectural tournament. And the vice-captain, too,” Shuu replied.

“To put it bluntly, all the club members who participated made it to the next stage,” Rir added[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119577).

“I mean, it was kinda obvious…”

Their instructor’s coaching must’ve been intense to get this result. Though it might also be due to each member’s own strength. Although the club didn’t meet that often per week, they churned out many powerful fighters, which indicated how skilled the members were.

On that note, their instructor, Gorilla Sensei, taught pretty much all the judo classes at the high school. The guy was a great PE teacher to begin with, even with that ape-like face of his.

“Woof~, in any case, he did incredibly well! Shuu ended almost all his fights in an instant!”

“I wasn’t that great…”

“Huh, but didn’t Gorilla Sensei say that it ‘felt like every fight ended with a single grab and throw’? You became this strong because you trained a lot!”

Rir’s tail wagged, and her ears stood up in apparent excitement, as she spoke of her boyfriend’s heroics.

“In that case, let’s all eat dragon steak in the dining hall today. I’ll also make a cake,” I proposed.

“Ain’t that too much trouble?”

“Not at all, but you’ll have to do your best at the prefectural tournament, alright? This time, we’ll come to cheer you on.”

“Thanks, man.” Shuu scratched his head with equal parts happiness and embarrassment.

Only, the last time the four of us had come to cheer him on, they’d been treating him as if he’d brought his harem. Not that they were completely off with that.

“Oh, and thanks for the grapes. Goin’ outta your way durin’ the date to get those for us.”

“It’s fine.”

As he smiled, Rir hugged his arm.

“You worked super hard, Shuu.”

“I guess.”

“So, I’ll have _something special_ for you later… Eh-heh-heh.”

“Uh… s-sure?”

They were speaking in small voices, so it was likely meant to be only between the two of them, but I was close enough to overhear it. I could guess that this _something special_ would consist of adult pleasures. Mika and I did the same, yesterday… Heh-heh-heh.

“Oh, before you leave, there’s something I have to tell you all,” Kanata cut in, looking apologetically.

Sakura was holding his arm with an anxious look.

“Did something happen?” I asked him.

“This is something Shuu and Bro already know. Rir, too, I assume. Mika-nee should be the only one who doesn’t… Uhm, it’s about our stalker.”

“A stalker? Someone is stalking you?”

“Well, I’ll come to that during my explanation.”

Kanata’s expression turned serious.

_Looks like he has some rather grave news._

---

“-and that’s what happened yesterday.”

It was shocking. I mean, I wasn’t with them when it happened, but to think that someone else with knowledge about Anazumu had shown up.

_What in the world is going on?_

“That’s also why I can’t say if he’s friend or foe… For now, we should stay careful. All of us.”

“Agreed. But I didn’t think he’d just make contact with you, Kanata,” Shuu replied.

“Hmph, so I’m the only one who didn’t know about this? You’re all so mean!”

“I-I’m sorry, Mika-nee.”

Nevertheless… the man had known Kanata’s name from the start. This was getting more and more mysterious. That said, I doubted anyone of us wanted to get dragged in such a troublesome matter, so we’d just take a wait-and-see approach.

“Well, as long as this guy doesn’t do anything, we shouldn’t need to worry, right?” I mused.

“True, I’d rather spend my time livin’ normally than getting’ involved in somethin’ weird.”

“…I also think so,” Kanata agreed.

The verdict was unanimous. The most important part was to stay away from trouble.

“Let’s disperse, then! I’ll call you for dinner.”

“Right!”

I brought the conversation to a close when I felt that the atmosphere was right. Everyone made their way back to their respective love nests, while acting all lovey-dovey with their partners.

“Will we go back, too?”

“Yep, let’s.”

_Now, time to forget all this negativity and make out with Mika. That’s what’s most important, after all!_

“Also, from now on, tell me about it if something happens, will you? I don’t like being left out!”

“Ah, sure. Sorry for that.”

“Well, you apologized, so I’ll forgive you.”

“Thanks.”

This was our back and forth on the way back to our room. I felt bad for not telling her, so next time, I’d make sure to inform her.

# **Footnotes:**

1. Even though her typical verbal tic is missing, I assume that’s her speaking, since she’s the only other person who should have that information

+++

# **Chapter 607-1 – After the Gathering – 1 (Shuu)**

In the original, this and the next chapter are numbered 607.5 and 607.75. I have no idea what the author intended with this, especially since there was no chapter 607 previously, though a comment at the end indicated that they wanted to keep it to one chapter originally.

---

“I’m looking forward to dinner!”

“Right, same here.”

After the gathering, Rir and I had returned to our room. Still… what did she mean earlier with _something special_? I was super worried about the stuff Kanata told us, but right now I couldn’t get that out of my head. Besides, would she do that to celebrate each time we won one of the tournaments…? The though almost made me gulp.

“Everyone makes their own lunch, right?”

“I think so.”

“You can look forward to my cooking, then.”

“Right.”

In Anazumu, Rir and I spent practically every day together. Or rather, we’d been together since we first met. While I was getting used to it, I never seemed to get enough of seeing her body. This was probably my nature as a man. Not that I had anything to feel guilty about. Having these kinds of expectations didn’t make me a degenerate.

“I’ll start by giving you a massage then, Shuu!”

“Sorry for the trouble.”

I took off most of my clothes and she had me lay down. Her massage techniques had become as skilled as those of a professional before I knew it. Just when did she learn them…? This was a good time to ask.

“Hey… Rir…”

“Hm? What is it, Shuu?”

“When did you… phew… become so skilled at massages?”

“Woof, while you were training with your mechanical opponents. I came up with the idea when I was pondering what I could do for you as you were training so much. I even ended up getting a skill.”

“I see.”

_She’s always doin’ stuff for me, always… What a great wife. There probably ain’t a better one out there. Though we ain’t exactly married yet… She seems up to it… and I’d like to tie the knot sooner than later. Still, gotta finish university to become a career policeman…_

_Anyway…_

“Woof, no matter how often I touch them, your muscles are amazing. Enchanting.”

“Th-Thanks for sayin’ that.”

She vigorously kneaded my legs, but… when she pressed down on my shoulders, it felt both firm and soft. I didn’t expect it to feel so nice.

“Woof, I’m almost done with the massage.”

“Mh, this seriously feels amazin’. Thank you!”

“Woof, I can do this whenever you want.”

A short time later, it ended. She’d been at it without a break for almost three hours and had even done acupuncture and moxibustion. I was genuinely shocked. But more importantly, it felt so soft when she massaged my feet, and her smooth legs were exquisite when she straddled me.

_Geez, what’s goin’ on with me today? I just can’t forget what she said earlier._

For now, I could probably think of it as a good thing, since she spent three hours nonstop on it.

“Oh, it’s almost time for lunch,” Rir commented, as she checked the time, finding that it was a bit past 11 am, and then left for the kitchen.

“Right.”

_I wonder what she’ll be makin’. I’m lookin’ forward to it._

“I’ll be cooking omurice today! From what Alim said, we’ll be having steak for dinner.”

“Right! Huh…?”

When I looked at her, it felt like something was off. The way Ayumu made this apartment-like room, you could see the kitchen from the living area and vice versa.

Right now, Rir was in the kitchen, but… something about her looked strange. Under the apron, her shoulders, collarbone and chest were bare.

_Oy, don’t tell me…_

To see if my hunch was correct, I had to enter the kitchen.

“H-Hey, Rir.”

“Woof? What is it?”

Rir, who was cutting vegetables, even though she could’ve just made pre-cut ones with Ayumu’s make-anything-machine (though it needed to be said that everyone in this house cut their vegetables), stopped her hands and turned to me.

The moment I entered the kitchen, I was greeted by a sight to behold. She wasn’t wearing anything except for the apron and black, knee-high socks.

“R-Rir?”

“I-Is something wrong?”

“Why are you naked under that apron?”

“…Woof.”

She fidgeted in apparent embarrassment.

_I-If she’s so embarrassed by it, why’d she do it…? I mean, it’s a feast for my eyes, but still…_

“Shuu, I didn’t just study up on massage techniques and sports medicine while you were working hard…” she explained as her face turned bright red. “I-I learned about… uhm, Japan’s culture… various aspects of it. Among that, this was something I could easily do… I thought it might make you happy.”

_Even if it’s for my sake, she’s doin’ way too much. I never wanted her to go that far._

_…Nah, that last part was a lie._

“F-Feel free to do whatever you want. I-I’m confident I can keep cooking as long as you keep it to touching me! But if you go further than that…”

“H-Hey, Rir, is that what you meant earlier by _something special_?”

“Woof? Well, not exactly, though it’s part of that,” she commented as she turned around and went back to her cooking.

On her back, everything was on display.

_Not good, this feels completely different than takin’ a bath or spendin’ the night together. What’s the right thing to do now?_

+++

# **Chapter 607-2 – After the Gathering – 2 (Shuu)**

“Woof… _huff_… Here you go, enjoy your… omurice.”

“…Right.”

She had drawn a heart onto the dish with ketchup. In the end, I went as far as her tolerance allowed. Just why wasn’t I able to hold myself back? No, I was pretty sure had I managed that, Rir would’ve been disappointed. It was better this way.

“How was it, Shuu. Did I manage to play the role of a newlywed bride? I even somehow managed to cook.”

“Well… I’m not sure that’s somethin’ newlyweds do… I mean, it’s pretty much just a man’s phantasy.”

“Woof.”

She looked rather adorable as she was gripping her spoon with a bright red face.

“Wh-What should we do afterwards?”

“Not sure.”

“W-We do have time until dinner.”

_Not much to do ’bout it… maybe we can take a nap together? Let’s do that._

“After lunch, how ’bout we…”

“Yes? Yes?” she asked impatiently.

“…take a nice nap?”

“…Alright. Can we lie next to each other?”

“Sure.”

Even I as someone more thickheaded than most could see that right now Rir would probably go along with anything I proposed. That was the reason I deliberately chose something normal.

We went to our double bed right after we finished eating. I put on some light pajamas and lay down. Rir crawled under the covers next to me.

“Just as always, in that case?”

“Even if that’s normal for us, it’s quite a luxury, ain’t it?”

“Woof? It’s true that human warmth is nice. Being together with you calms me down.”

It sounded like she wasn’t quite sure what was good about it. But if our male classmates were to see this scene, they’d undoubtedly murder me. Rir had become rather popular with them.

“Y-You can do whatever you want,” she said, driving home the point.

I just hugged her.

“Hey, Rir, are you plannin’ to do this until the intra scholastic tournament is over? Preparin’ a reward each time, I mean.”

“That’s right. A whole day for each win! Could it be that you don’t consider me a proper reward…? I’m pretty sure I’ll get better with time.”

“Nah, that ain’t it.”

Was she intending to go this far to reward me on the first day in Anazumu after every win in the prefectural, provincial, and national competitions?

_Not sure if I should tell her that I’m lookin’ forward to it, or not to go crazy._

“Rir… I don’t get why you’re goin’ that far for me.”

“…Woof, it’s because I pledged my loyalty to you… and because I love you, Shuu.”

“Gotcha.”

I was caressing her head as I held her in my arms. I understood her reason, but I still though she was going too far, acting too devoted.

“Shuu… I love you.”

“Right, same here.”

“Woof~!”

She nuzzled against me, burying her head in my chest. I lay there, continuing to pet her head.

---

“Dig in, everyone! We got tons of food!”

Ayumu had called us to the dining hall. It happened ten minutes after we had woken up. We ended up sleeping almost until 6 pm.

Amazingly big steaks were spread out in front of us. Just seeing them made me drool.

We said grace and started eating. It was so good, I felt like I might faint.

“What’s the verdict, Shuu. Do you like it?”

“Yep, it’s crazy good.”

“Aright, heh-heh.”

Ayumu, who was wearing a chef’s outfit, peered at my face. It reminded me that he was a girl on this side.

“Do your best during the next matches,” Mika told me. “We’ll come watch.”

“Right.”

Hearing that my childhood friends would come to cheer me on obviously made me happy. I’d love if they’d watch the matches up to the national tournament, but that was unreasonable, location wise.

“We’ll be watching, too. Right, Sakura?”

“Yeah.”

Knowing that they’d all come watch… it felt great. Still, others would probably call me out again for my “harem”.

I devoured my steak. After all was said and done, it was abnormally delicious.

---

“That was so yummy.”

“…True.”

Only, my thoughts – and eyes – were on something slightly different. That was only natural, seeing we were taking a bath together.

“Yes, Shuu… this now is the main part of the _something special_ you’ve been curious about all this time.”

“Right.”

She’d finally said it. Well, it was clear that the naked apron also had been part of it.

“J-Just like always, right? Uhm, in the bed, I mean. I guess it’s not that special from your perspective, Shuu… but for me it is.”

In other words, she wanted us to have sex. In this case, she could’ve just brought it up normally. Well, I usually talked about it in a more roundabout way, so I couldn’t blame her.

“Sure, I’m up for it.”

“Woof, really!? I-In that case, I’m up for anything!”

_And she’ll do this again three weeks from now_[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119789)_? Well, ain’t like I can hold myself back, so I won’t complain._

# **Footnotes:**

1. Two weeks in the original. A full Earth/Anazumu round is three weeks, so I assume that’s an error.

+++

# **Chapter 608 – Life Study**

“Here you go, it’s done! That was the last one you needed from me, right?”

“Yep, sorry ’bout the trouble… It’s ’cause the prefectural tournament is next. From this point on, I gotta go all out.”

I had produced a new mechanical judo training partner for Shuu. I made it by creating a list of past judo athletes, which I used to gather videos from both male and female fighters who won gold at the Olympics, from which I extracted all kinds of data.

At the start, creating a training partner with the strength of an Olympic finalist was meant as a joke, but Shuu ended up with a 50% win-rate, which meant he already started to move on the same level as those top-athletes. Moreover, this was without using Secret Martial Techniques at all.

That was the reason I now provided him with a training partner that was a chimera created by combining stronger data, which also had a huge advantage in physique.

Well, it seemed that Shuu was a genius when it came to martial arts, just as my brother was a genius in intellect. My best friend would probably participate in the Olympics before long and attain the gold medal in a flash.

_He’s already able to beat top athletes without using his skills, so just how strong would he be in Earth terms if he did? Well, I’ll probably find out once I watch him at the prefectural tournament._

“Rir also helps you train, doesn’t she?”

“Yep, she does.”

“By the way, what did she mean when she said she’d ‘give you a reward each time you win’?” I asked in a mean-spirited way.

He grimaced in apparent embarrassment.

“Uhm, how do I put it… guess I can tell you since it’s just us.”

“Go on.”

“Well, we’re sleepin’ together.”

“I assume not in the meaning of just sleeping next to each other?”

“Y-You got it.”

_Makes sense, this is probably the best reward Rir can give him, with his proclivities. Come to think of it, did he throw away that erotic magazine? Not that it matters at this point._

“Geez, she’s a shrewd one.”

“G-Guess so… She’s waitin’ for me, so I gotta go back.”

“Alright, see you!”

He stored the training puppet in his magic back and left for his room.

_Hm, at this rate, he’ll really win the national tournament._

While they made it there last year, he regrettable had to face the one who’d end up champion in the semifinals and ended up in fourth place. In the team competition, they reached eight place, if I remembered correctly. This year, he should be able to win it.

“Ayumu, are you done talking to Shuu?”

“Yes, I am.”

My loving wife greeted me as I returned to our room. Ten days had passed since we went to harvest grapes, and nothing out of the ordinary had happened so far. We hadn’t even been interrupted by King Rama during our intimate times[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119886).

“Come to think of it, it will be almost Christmas once Shuu’s tournament is over.”

“Now that you mention it, you’re right!”

Christmas was getting closer… We’d probably spend it very differently than in the previous years. It made me look forward to it. And New Years would be hot on its heels.

“Will we go on a Christmas date?”

“We could go to a chic restaurant.”

“…What about money? It’s a bit tight for me, so maybe we should pick a normal place instead.”

“Hm~, it’s a special day, so I’ll pay.”

Recently, Kanata had taught me how to trade stocks and I split the time when Mika wasn’t with me between playing video games and making money. At this point, even if I spent 10 to 20’000 yen on Christmas, I’d be able to manage.

“Alright… I guess I’ll just let you spoil me!”

“Eh-heh-heh.”

“Eh-heh-heh~.”

Since we made such plans, Shuu and Kanata and their partners likely did too. Thinking of it, pretty much everything was different from last year.

“That reminds me, we have regular exams a bit under a week before Christmas,” I mused.

“…What are you thinking?”

“Can I be honest?”

“Yeah, don’t hold back.”

“At this point, I feel like we’d end up the best in our year even if we don’t study at all.”

“I agree.”

Well, we seriously overdid it when we studied in Anazumu. Though we hadn’t had any practice or regular exams since then.

We were at the point where we got a passing mark even when solving questions for the world’s most demanding university (Kanata got full marks, which was even scarier), so I felt like it would be enough to do a quick study session in Anazumu a day before the regular exams. Putting it like this sounded rather arrogant… In any case, it wasn’t a good thing. From society’s perspective, we were pretty much cheating[2](#easy-footnote-bottom-2-119886).

_Well, to get here we once were on the brink of death…_

“In any case, Ayumu… will we be going to bed now?”

“Huh? You want to do it today, too?”

“Yeah!”

_Having this sloppy attitude towards exams… it feels like we’re going in a dangerous direction for high schoolers. Well, can’t change the facts!_

“Alright, to the bed, then…”

“Eh-heh-heh… Ayumu~.”

I picked up Mika in a bridal carry. And that moment-

⟦Alim, Mika! It is Us, Rama! We found out the identity of the last guide[3](#easy-footnote-bottom-3-119886)!⟧

We looked at each other.

“I was afraid this would happen.”

“Same.”

# **Footnotes:**

1. Don’t tell me, did the author finally drop this worn-out joke?

2. They’re still studying for stuff and aren’t using tools during exams that are considered cheating. If you argue like this, every student going to cram school would be cheating.

3. Nevermind, still the same stupid joke
